Above the chaotic battlefield was a rippling, distorted scroll painting that wasn’t possible to see clearly. Within it, the colors black and white twisted back and forth. Occasionally, boundless might from within it swept down to the battlefield, killing anyone it touched.

The armies of the cultivators and gods were like grains of sand, flowing back and forth as they clashed. Blood spread. Corpses fell. It was extremely ghastly!

The starry sky was ripped apart. Space-time shattered. That only added chaos and danger to the battlefield. This universe couldn’t take it much longer!

Within all that chaos was an enchantingly beautiful True God clad in golden armor, with violet hair that swirled around hīm as hē strode forward.

“Your name’s Xu Qing, right?” hē said, hīs godly voice echoing forth to reach the fleeing Xu Qing. As it did, it slashed open a huge furrow in the starry sky in front of Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s gaze sharpened, revealing an aggressive light. He quickly performed an incantation gesture with his left hand, causing his immortal embryo to tower over him. The power of metal, wood, water, fire, earth, time, and space surged, becoming like shooting stars that streamed around the immortal embryo. Overlapping projections of himself appeared, which was the unleashing of the canons of space-time and parallelism.

When all of that combined, he lunged forward. A deafening rumbling sound echoed out. By lunging forward, he ended up shooting right into the furrow that had opened up in front of him. Then his canon flared before dimming. He shot through the furrow.

When he was an early Quasi-Immortal, he could fight a peak Altar God. Now that he was a mid Quasi-Immortal, his battle prowess wasn’t sufficient enough to truly bridge the gap between himself and a True God, although he could at least defend himself.

Upon emerging from the other side, his face was pale, but he still accelerated.

This battle is already chaotic. Even if I make it back to the cultivator forces, I’ll still be in the middle of the fighting. Therefore... to get away from the battlefield, I first need to leave the entire area.

He had made his decisions, and yet... despite accelerating after making it through the furrow, the pretty True God was right on his tail.

Upon closing in, the True God waved hīs hand, causing a second furrow to open up in front of Xu Qing, blocking his path. Then came a third, fourth, and a fifth furrow.... In total, ninety-nine of them appeared, surrounding Xu Qing and cutting him off from everything else.

It was very obvious how incredibly mighty a True God was. Next, the pretty True God clenched hīs right hand into a fist. The ninety-nine furrows suddenly seem to come alive, splitting out from the backdrop of the starry sky and turning into threads.

Then those threads all began to converge on Xu Qing! They thrummed with sealing power as well as mighty cutting force. What was more, they pulsed with the explosive power of a True God. They sped toward Xu Qing!

As the crisis mounted, Xu Qing’s pupils constricted. In another place and situation, he could take the time to fight this opponent. But there was too much happening on the battlefield, making it very unsuitable for sustained fighting.

In terms of trump cards, he did have the dao weapon of an Immortal Lord. But that dao weapon was too powerful. Even if he did use his destiny aura to unleash it, he would be significantly weakened as a result. Unless he had absolutely no other options, he didn’t want to use it here on this chaotic battlefield.

Therefore, as the danger mounted, his eyes glittered, and he thrust out his right hand to reveal the unconscious Goddess Starryeyes. He used hēr to block the first of the slicing furrows.

The pretty True God’s eyes hardened. With the wave of a right hand, hē stopped moving. The slicing furrows also lurched to a halt.

Taking advantage of that split-second interruption, Xu Qing shot forward with a burst of speed. The overlapping sensation around him became more pronounced, as a host of different space-times formed around him. By shattering some of them, he managed to break free from the area.

After, he zipped back and forth through the battlefield, seemingly at random.

Behind him, the pretty True God’s face flashed with golden light as hē made a decision. If Starryeyes died, shē could be resurrected. If hē kept worrying about hēr safety, then this opponent would be able to constantly keep hīm in a passive position.

“Ah, whatever!” the True God murmured. Hē took a step forward, spanning the battlefield, all while speaking in a voice that echoed around Xu Qing. “Do you know why I was selected for this little exchange? It’s because the more chaotic this battlefield is, the better my godhood works.”

Xu Qing heard the words, and his expression darkened visibly. There was no reason for this god to be talking so much, and yet hē seemed to be constantly saying something. The words hē spoke were chosen deliberately.

Is it related to hīs godly authority?

Even as that thought occurred to Xu Qing, an intense sensation of danger struck him.

The pretty True God was clearly quite a distance away, yet hīs words swirled in the area, and even caused golden threads to appear. It was a similar effect to the slicing furrows from before, yet at the same time, was somewhat different.

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted as the golden threads suddenly spread out behind him. As it turned out, their target wasn’t him. It was... the corpses of the gods and cultivators floating in the area. Every single golden thread connected to one of the mangled corpses, until there were thousands of such connections.

Then... every single corpse twitched and opened its eyes. Those eyes glowed with golden light! It was exactly the same thing the pretty True God had done to the five human cultivators from earlier. Xu Qing’s face fell as he realized that they were god puppets!

So this is hīs godly authority! Hē turns hīs will into threads, then connects the threads to corpses. It doesn’t matter if they’re gods or cultivators. They all turn into puppets!

Xu Qing frowned. It was definitely true that a godhood power like this would be particularly effective on a battlefield.

As soon as the corpses awakened, they all flew up into the air and then bore down on Xu Qing. Though their cultivation bases were only partially intact, given how many there were, they formed an astonishingly deadly force.

Xu Qing fell back urgently, all while waving his hand to unleash a space-time tempest to block the corpses. At the same time, he landed on a head-shaped asteroid. Unfortunately, the moment he landed, golden striations appeared on the asteroid, which wriggled into the shape of facial features, as if the thing was alive.

The asteroid had been turned into a puppet! It opened its mouth and spewed a curse mist.

Just before impact, Xu Qing borrowed Starfire’s power, unleashing a god curse that negated the incoming curse. Without a sound, the asteroid crumbled in on itself and collapsed into dust. Unfortunately, that short delay gave the corpses time to get a lot closer. Off in the distance, the pretty True God was now visible.

Xu Qing scowled at the realization of how powerful the enemy’s curse was. That said, he now knew how gruish this godly authority was.

It can turn anything into a puppet?

Xu Qing waved his hand, and the iron skewer appeared, shooting forth with aggressive power. At the same time, the chime of a bell echoed out, and all the corpses stopped, allowing the skewer to hit many of them.

Of course, Xu Qing didn’t stop like the corpses. He used a secret magic to shoot away even faster than before. His clothes were already in tatters as he flew along. As he passed, the remains of heavenly bodies and numerous corpses would glitter with golden light as they awakened.

Puppets were charging toward him from in front and behind.

“STARFIRE!” Xu Qing howled inwardly. In response, Starfire again opened hērself up, becoming the medium for Xu Qing to transpose between immortal and god. Xu Qing then let loose an audible shout.

That sound became a godly voice. It was a god magic! Sound seizing!

The battlefield was a suitable face for this pretty True God, but... it was also very suitable for Xu Qing’s sound-seizing god magic. Instantly, Xu Qing’s sound erupted out, and the godly voice became an ancient curse that emerged from every sound on the battlefield.

The booms became godly voices. The sound of slaughter became godly voices. The screams of death became godly voices. The godly voices turned into mysterious admonitions that entangled the puppets as well as the approaching True God. freewebnovel.com

This was not something the pretty True God had considered might happen, and it caused hīs eyes to shine.

“You can use god magic?”

He waved hīs hand, and more golden threads appeared out of nowhere, piercing into the admonitions of Xu Qing’s godly voice, and... turned them into puppets as well! Then they spun back and raced toward Xu Qing.

However, there were just too many unexpected things that could happen on a battlefield. Whether it was the clash of the armies or the shock waves from the God Lord and Immortal Lord, there were many factors that could affect the chase between Xu Qing and the True God.

At the moment, a stray flow of power from the God Lord hit Xu Qing, and blood sprayed out of his mouth. Even the pretty True God was forced to take evasive action.

And thus, Xu Qing and the True God flew across the battlefield. As Xu Qing sped along, he launched attacks to destroy some of the remnants of heavenly bodies and the corpses of gods and cultivators, turning them into stellar rubble. What he couldn’t destroy were latched onto by the pretty True God, who turned them into puppets that attacked Xu Qing.

As the chase continued, the distance between them decreased.

Then something happened that caused Xu Qing’s heart to sink. Off in the distance, another True God started heading toward him. Thankfully, a Lower Immortal moved to block the god.

However, it still left Xu Qing with a sense of mounting crisis. Looking around, he identified a location that he needed to reach. But then, his eyes glittered coldly, and he made a decision. Stopping in place, he turned. He would not flee any more. Settling his energy and clearing his mind, he put his hand on his forehead. Soul fluctuations turned into a dao will.

“Crescent Moon!”

Astonishingly, the image of a moon floated off Xu Qing’s forehead. He had used the destiny aura of a true monarch to call out to the dao weapon of an Immortal Lord! At the same time, within the parallel space-times around him, all the other versions of himself did exactly the same thing. They spoke exactly the same words.

“Crescent Moon!!”

As the sound echoed out in all the space-times, the moon projection on the forehead of the real Xu Qing revealed a curved, blood-colored blade, something that could pierce planets and slash the sky. It slowly emerged from his forehead.

It looked like the sliver of a fingernail ripped off of a corpse’s finger, covered with millions upon millions of blood vessel striations. Each striation seemed to flow with starlight from a different time period. Some of the light was like the marrow of stars, pale violet, which had existed for countless years. Other light was like the rubble of planets that had been immersed in the Primeval Sea for countless years. And in the middle was a pulsing artery that seemed to form an image of the entire Fifth Star Ring!

It was extremely ghastly! Gruish scarlet light spread out that represented death and blood.

All planets in the vicinity collapsed. Asteroids and corpses melted.... It was like flowing tears of blood.

Off in the distance, the pretty True God saw what was happening, and for the very first time... hē was completely taken aback.

“A God Lord’s dao weapon!” The sight of the curved blood-colored blade coming out of Xu Qing’s forehead caused the pretty True God to reel! The full mightiness of a God Lord became a crushing will that made it a struggle for hīm to breathe. An intense sensation of deadly crisis covered the heavens and moons of hīs god kingdom.[1]

He has a God Lord’s dao weapon!! No, wait. That can’t be. A Quasi-Immortal shouldn’t be able to use a dao weapon like that.... What’s more, my omniscience couldn’t sense it.... Someone made it so that this person’s information can’t be accessed via omniscience!!

The pretty True God was shaken to the core. As of this moment, the scarlet blade coming out of Xu Qing’s forehead hadn’t even emerged by half. Yet even that small portion caused his face to distort. His fleshly body felt like it was being ripped apart, and his soul was writhing. It seemed like he was just on the verge of being killed in body and soul.

This dao weapon was just too powerful. Despite being a true monarch and the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring, there was no way he could unleash it in its entirety.

And yet, Xu Qing’s eyes flashed with immense determination. Using the destiny aura, he continued to activate the crescent moon blade!

It emerged from his forehead by another inch. The scarlet glow expanded, causing fights on both sides of the conflict to look over in astonishment and back away. Eventually... a strange grating noise filled the depths of the starry sky.

It sounded like some entity scraping bone with a fingernail. The sound caused all the nearby asteroids to start vibrating. Countless corpses and the rubble of planets also vibrated. At the same time, vein networks appeared on them similar to what covered the blade. Anyone in range to hear, be they cultivators or gods, were visibly astonished.

The pretty True God’s pupils constricted as the shock in hīs heart escalated. Hē quickly started falling back.

Unfortunately, just as hē started moving, Xu Qing, his eyes bloodshot, shouted something in a voice that hardly sounded human.

“Come forth, Crescent Moon!”

Xu Qing shook violently as the flesh of his forehead split and blood spilled down, soaking him. That was the price he paid to pull the blood-red blade one more inch out of his forehead!

Now, more than half of the blade was visible. What was immeasurably gruish was the fact that a host of tiny black holes covered the surface of the blood-colored blade. From within them emerged the distorted voices of souls.

“The fingernail brings tribulation to the gods; when the tribulation ends, the fingernail is born again.”

The voice split the void, causing numerous rifts to open in the starry sky. Out from those rifts poured a rain as thick as blood. It looked extremely ghastly.

All hearts were shaken by the voice, but the effects were especially pronounced on the gods. Out on the battlefield, an Altar God accidentally ran into one of the rifts. The god suddenly screamed with madness, reached up, and clawed hīs eyeballs out of their eye sockets.

Hē threw them to the side. But then the eyes transformed into twitching projections of blades that seemed to possess a life of their own as they cackled and started flying about on their own.

All cultivators in the area felt themselves drawn to the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring. However, because the item had been forged by Immortal Lord Deepgloom, the effect wasn’t very strong. Despite being shaken, they took advantage of the moment to attack.

As for the pretty True God, hē was too close, and suffered a huge effect from the attack. God blood sprayed out of hīm as hīs golden armor started cracking. Then a boom could be heard as the armor exploded, turning into a host of fragments that shot in front of hīm to form a barrier.

That just managed to spare hīm from the attack, and hē fled backward even more quickly, all while drawing on the full power of hīs godhood. Countless golden threads spun out in all directions, forming something like a defensive cocoon around hīm.

However, the scarlet light just kept coming. As soon as it hit the cocoon, the light caused the golden cocoon to rust. The effects of the rust were bizarre! If you looked closely, you would see that the golden surface had spiral designs, almost like the fingerprint of a curse.

Deep red light shone from the designs, within which concealed millions upon millions of distorted faces. Altogether, they made a design that started to break open the cocoon to devour its contents.

The pretty True God’s godhood was trembling. At that moment of crisis, hē wasn’t thinking at all about hīs mission. Hīs instincts were telling hīm to get as far away as possible.

Unfortunately, the battlefield was shattered. Space-time was in chaos, and since hīs godhood related to space-time, it meant that hē couldn’t easily escape. Hē couldn’t teleport away. The only chance hē had was to find a spatial nexus. Unfortunately, just because hē wanted to find one didn’t mean hē would be able to right now.

Even as hē went all out to defend hīmself, all while fleeing, and also while using divine will to search for a spatial nexus... Xu Qing was soaked in blood and looked more ferocious than ever. With his left hand, he held nothing back to drain Starryeyes of ringsource.

And with his right hand, he reached up... grabbed the blade protruding from his forehead and he ripped it out! Intense rumbling sounds echoed out from his head. He... dragged the blade out into the open!

It was fully out in the starry sky! Crimson light shone everywhere. Within that light was the five-inch blade that resembled a crescent moon, with its tip pointed in the direction of the pretty god.

Then he flicked his wrist, and the blade shot out of his hand toward the fleeing True God.

Looking at the scene from a distance, the way the blade sliced through the starry sky made it seem like it was cutting open skin. Blade light surged as the blade slashed into the golden cocoon.

The cocoon vibrated briefly before collapsing into fragments. The countless faces in the rust joined the blade as it slashed toward the True God.

The True God was stunned. However, hē quickly unleashed a secret magic, which hē used to rip open hīs chest, rip out hīs heart, and stuff it into hīs mouth. Hē devoured it! That was the origin of hīs god kingdom and hīs godhood.

Upon swallowing it, hīs destroyed god kingdom turned into pure god power. By using hīs godhood to devour the flame of hīs true name, hē achieved a huge boost in battle prowess.

Hīs energy surged, and it blocked the blade! Intense rumbling sounds echoed out as the blade stopped in place. By losing hīs heart, the pretty True God was able to mount a brief defense and fall back. But then the veins covering the blade erupted.

What came out wasn’t blood. It was a sound pressure that could exterminate universes. The result was that the god power formed when the True God devoured hīs god kingdom began to crumble. Then, the mouth-like black holes on the surface of the blade opened and exerted a sucking force. To hīs shock and horror, the True God’s god power began to stream toward the black holes. Those ‘mouths’ began to devour all of it!

Then the surface of the blade began to wriggle gruishly as a host of fleshy tendrils spread out from it. In the middle of the writhing tendrils, a host of blood-red eyes appeared. It made it seem like the crescent moon was smiling!

The pretty True God was struck senseless by the sight of it. Then the crescent moon shone with dazzling light as it slashed toward hīm. From a distance, it looked like a long, red river flowing up from the Nine Serenities underworld!

It swept past the True God’s head. God blood sprayed everywhere!

The pretty True God spasmed and staggered backward. Hē could sense the grievous injury to hīs head, and could sense hīs life force flowing out of hīm. Acting on instinct, hē reached up to push hīs hand down onto the head wound.

Yet as hē did, he realized that there was a host of bizarre green fingernails burrowing out between hīs fingers. In a daze, hē looked down to find that there were gruish fingernails growing out of hīs skin all over.

As a result, hīs entire body looked like it was covered with demonic scales.[2]

And then... the scales all flipped around and burrowed directly into hīm toward hīs soul. Indescribable torment filled every part of the True God, starting in hīs soul and exploding outward from here.

An anguished, grating scream escaped hīs mouth. It was the sound of life force being cut away. God blood then spurted out of all the wounds. But the flow of blood quickly dried up, and then what came out wasn’t god blood, but coldly shimmering fingernails!

The blade that had slashed through hīs neck then appeared behind hīm in its full form. The blood vessels that covered it had spread outward, surrounding it to form a wheel of life.

It looked like a gear, and on every gear tooth was sealed the life force that had been devoured by the blade. And deep on the wheel, it was possible to see blood-colored inscriptions that looked like they had been scratched there by a fingernail.

“When you look at this blade, the reflection you see will be of nine reincarnations, growing in your fingernails, that are not your own. And thus, whoever returns will not be you. The work of Deepgloom.”

As the pretty True God looked at the blade, it was reflected in hīs eyes. Those eyes could not sustain the effort, and exploded. The blade remained. Those eyes had already been drawn into the crescent moon, and were now part of the dao weapon!

The skin of hīs face began to collapse, as if it were being peeled off by fingernails. Revealed beneath was blood and bone and flesh. Then the wound on hīs neck opened wide, and hīs head fell off.

Taking the pain in hīs eyes with hīm... hē collapsed into ashes. Hē had been destroyed in body and soul.

The blade turned into blood-red moonlight that returned to Xu Qing, entered his forehead, and was seen no more. Everything was quiet for a moment. Then the sound of slaughter and battle returned.

Xu Qing coughed up a huge mouthful of blood. He had been severely weakened, and his heart was pounding.

This was his first time using the dao weapon, and the sensation had been bizarre! It felt like his own fingernails were itching, as if life were forming within them. Scalp tingling, he burst into motion and headed toward the spot he had identified earlier.

It was a spatial nexus. Xu Qing had space-time canon. While the space-time in this location was in chaos, Xu Qing was actually much better at identifying spatial nexuses than the pretty True God. That was why he had chosen to make his stand against the True God in that spot. If he wanted to leave the battlefield, he could attempt a teleportation at a spatial nexus.

He had no idea where the nexus led. But given his weakened state, anywhere but this battlefield would be good. Without any hesitation, he raced toward it.

Along the way, he noticed that, though he was still extracting ringsource from Starryeyes, and the goddess was trembling, shē was peaceful, as if shē wasn’t cursed like before.

Xu Qing looked over. Starryeyes immediately closed hēr eyes, not daring to make eye contact with him. Shē feared him. Before, shē had not feared him. Shē had hated him. It was a very deep-seated hatred. But after what shē had just witnessed, especially that gruish dao weapon, hēr heart was filled with terror.

Dying in that way, and especially in the way described in the inscription, which was the same as not returning at all, turned hēr hatred of Xu Qing into dread. Add in what had occurred with Spirit Jade, and shē now believed that the Fifth Star Ring really was a place that had figured out the secrets of the gods’ ability to return from death!

Xu Qing noted hēr reaction thoughtfully, then focused on reaching the hidden spatial nexus. He had no time to pay close attention to Starryeyes. Upon reaching the nexus, he didn’t hesitate to activate his canon and send it into the nexus.

At the same time, a golden stream of light appeared off in the distance as a three-headed six-armed True God suddenly started racing toward Xu Qing. Clearly, hē believed that Xu Qing couldn’t use the curved blade again, and considering how weak he was, it would be easy to kill him.

Xu Qing looked down. Not pausing for a moment, he continued to activate his canon and open the spatial nexus. Then... it erupted! Rumbling sounds echoed out as space collapsed, destroying everything.

Xu Qing was no longer visible on the battlefield!

1. This is the third time in the novel that god kingdoms have been mentioned. The previous times were in 1196 and 1243, however neither of those chapters defined them or explained exactly how they work. Starting at this point, we will learn more about them, but it’s all by ‘observation.’ The author never outright explains them in the narrative. ☜

2. Visually, this works fine in English, as you can imagine fingernails looking like scales. But there is an additional level of wordplay in Chinese, as the words for fingernail and scale (of a fish, the type of armor, etc.) contain a shared character. ☜

The sky looked like a dark, hazy curtain as far as the eye could see. There was no sun or moon. It seemed like this location existed in perpetual night. However, there were 360 emerald-colored halos above, almost like a gigantic bracelet, that shone with a soft light.

This was a planet in an unknown universe. It had a sea, land, mountains, and islands. The sea was a phosphorescent ocean, the land was made from stellar rubble, and the mountains were made from some mutant amethyst.[1]

As for the islands, they weren’t in the sea. They were actually islands that floated near the cliffs of the amethyst mountains, suspended in the air by means of light-consuming vines. The vines were semitransparent, and their roots dug into the air itself, making it hard to tell where they got nutrients from. And it also made it seem like the islands were suspended from nothing at all.

A person had just appeared above one of those islands. He wore a tattered daoist robe, his hair was disheveled, and his face was splattered with blood. His aura was weak, and he hardly seemed conscious as he dropped down onto the island. When he landed, a space-time breeze seemed to float out from him, causing the vine-covered island to tremble and wither visibly.

The island couldn’t hold the figure that had just fallen onto it. A hole crumbled open, and the figure fell down through the entire island. Down he fell, ultimately landing in the vast forest at the base of the cliffs.

For some reason, even though he didn’t land with much force, all of the trees for 300 meters in all directions collapsed, turning into a dust of starlight that rose into the air and obscured the area. Visible within that glittering dust wasn’t just that one person. He... was holding another person by the throat.

That second person was unconscious, yet the first person maintained a vice-like grip, despite the fact that he was also unconscious.

It didn’t take long for things to become silent again. The dust slowly settled, turning back into trees so that the forest was whole again.

The vegetation in this forest wasn’t actually true and real. It was made from dust! It consumed starlight that drifted in from the surrounding universe. Apparently, the dust operated according to some ancient magical law; it would extract memories from the starlight and display them as moving images within the forest.

Time passed.

Soon it started to rain. However, the rain wasn’t made of water, nor did it behave like ordinary rain. It came in the form of millions upon millions of phosphorescent flying objects in the thin atmosphere of the planet, which would slowly drop down from sky.

From a distance, it almost looked like the result of a god out in the void, ripping up sutra books and tossing the pages down. The ripped pages would eventually catch fire and emit both a bright light and a sound like a godly voice chanting.

“Glorious illumination... glorious illumination....”

As the chanting drifted out, blurry projections appeared in the light cast by the burning sutra pages. Gradually, those projections grew clearer. All of thēm looked exactly the same. Thēy had bodies made of woven light, and were neither male nor female. What was more, each one had twelve wings of light protruding from thēir backs, which produced iridescent vortexes as thēy flapped.

Thēy formed in the sky and then spread in all directions, chanting. Thēir passage caused the dust on the ground to rise up and become a whimpering wind. The amethyst mountain ranges shook, and a sound like the ancient song of a flute greeted thēm.

In the phosphorescent ocean, glowing pillars of light rose up, turning into a staircase that thēy could dance upon. The vines suspending the islands began to exude golden sap, which congealed to form hexagonal crystals that conformed to the magical laws of this universe, which then floated up like sacrificial offerings. Down below, the forest beneath the islands was crumbling and turning into a dust storm that swept up to offer worship to thēm.

The only thing left behind after that were the two people who lay there unmoving.

However, it didn’t take long... before the young woman whose throat was being held slowly opened hēr eyes. Shē first looked around in astonishment, and then hēr eyes lit up with joy. Next, shē looked over at the person lying next to hēr, and shē seemed to fill with hesitation and fear.

Shē didn’t act rashly. Instead, shē looked up at the glowing figures above, and opened hēr mouth as if to speak in a godly voice. Shē had been sealed, and could not project divine will. But if shē could speak in a godly voice, shē was convinced that the spirit gods above would hear hēr.[2]

Yet just as shē was about to speak... the hand on hēr throat clamped down with much more force than before, making it impossible for hēr to produce even a bit of sound.

Starryeyes trembled and looked over at Xu Qing. His eyes were open now. Shē didn’t dare to do anything, not even move. Xu Qing didn’t move either, nor did his facial expression change in any way.

Eventually, the glowing figures overhead disappeared into the distance, and everything went back to normal. Only at that point did he look over at Starryeyes and start extracting some ringsource from hēr.

Starryeyes despaired as the terrifying force wreaked havoc and dragged hēr ringsource out of hēr. Shē had only just formed some more, and now it was gone. When the process was over, shē felt weak and limp.

Afterward, Xu Qing sealed hēr voice again, strengthened all the other seals on hēr, and then trussed her up with chains and put hēr away. Having accomplished that, he carefully sent his divine will out to scan the area. Gradually, his expression turned grim. A moment passed.

“Thank you,” he said softly.

“There’s no need to thank me, Young Lord. Have things become that awkward between us now?” Starfire sounded a bit weak, but was just as flirtatious as ever. Shē knew why Xu Qing was thanking hēr. Upon arriving at this planet, shē had noticed the unusual surroundings, and had taken the initiative to cover Xu Qing with hēr godly aura to protect him. Shē had also noticed Starryeyes acting suspicious, so shē had used hēr godsource to wake up Xu Qing.

“Going forward,” he said softly, “you don’t need to keep bolstering me.”

Sitting up, he closed his eyes to meditate and heal. He had some speculations about his current location, but whether it was to simply confirm those speculations or leave, he needed his cultivation base in good shape.

Thus, the most important thing to do now was heal his cultivation base. Whether it was the price he paid to use the dao weapon or the danger of the chaotic spatial flows he had just endured, he was now in an extremely weak state.

Thankfully... he had a nice ringsource stockpile. His reward from capturing Starryeyes was enough to restore his cultivation base, and that wasn’t to mention that he had the god imprisoned in the Aurora Immortal Palace to harvest from. Plus... he still had Starryeyes as well. Considering that shē didn’t seem capable of completely running out of ringsource, shē was like a precious treasure to him.

In that manner, time passed. Half a month went by.

During that time, Starfire kept Xu Qing hidden in the forest of dust trees. Xu Qing continuously absorbed ringsource and used it to heal. There were additional instances in which ancient scenes played out in the forest, and that same rain occurred.

Xu Qing could sense something god-like in those twelve-winged figures of light. However, thēy seemed very different from other gods that he had seen before. That said, he had no intention of deeper study and analysis until he was completely healed.

Ten more days passed.

As Xu Qing sat there cross-legged, he opened his eyes, and they glittered brightly. His cultivation base... had recovered by seventy percent. The reason he hadn’t fully recovered was because of the lingering effects of the dao weapon. It would simply take time. However, Xu Qing could tell that once he had fully recovered, the tempering his soul had gone through would make it purer than before.

Well, I suppose I should look around and determine where I am!

He looked up, his eyes glittering. Next, Starfire’s godly aura swept out, covering Xu Qung, then the entire planet, and then spreading out into the starry sky. Mutagen levels were high, and godly fluctuations filled the area.

There was no way he was in the Fifth Star Ring. Though he had suspected as much when he woke up, after getting a good sense of his surroundings, he sighed. This was a completely unfamiliar starry sky. Given how happy Starryeyes had seemed earlier, Xu Qing could only come to the conclusion that this was the Fourth Star Ring.

As for the specific planet.... Xu Qing’s divine will was telling him that the planet was located on the very edge of a nebula. The planet was emerald-green, and as it slowly rotated, it was possible to hear something that resembled the sound of a subterranean meridian slowly breathing.

On one part of the planet was a crystalline plain inhabited by scaled oxen with wings. Their scales were very special, as it allowed them to form a resonance with the land around them. And when they flapped their wings, they would send out delicate motes of light. Even more strange was that these oxen were apparently intelligent. They actually had formed a civilization. A kingdom.

They also had a temple in which they offered sacrifices to their god. That god looked like a glowing butterfly. Īt was not a True God, just an Altar God.

As Xu Qing observed, he noticed one of the scaled oxen approach a temple. It was dying, and as it prostrated in front of the temple, it gradually transformed into a similar type of glowing butterfly before entering the temple.

That wasn’t the only place where gods could be found.

In a location far, far away from the scaled oxen was a vast field of fluorescent mushrooms! As they chanted into the wind, their roots linked together to form a massive kingdom. When the fire of rain fell from the sky, their bodies would burn and turn into a blue mist that rose into the air. Within that mist was an ethereal mayfly that consumed sound waves. Inside the transparent belly of that mayfly was the god of their species.

The planet also had a humanoid species. They lived in the southwestern part of the planet, where magnetic storms were frequent. They built their homes in roving crystalline forests. The trees in the forests devoured lightning to survive, and the sparks they shed when they broke open were believed by the humanoid species to be a punishment from the gods. Maybe it really was a punishment. After all, Xu Qing’s divine will made it clear that the lightning contained the aura of a god.

What caught Xu Qing’s attention the most were the 360 emerald-green halos in the dome of heaven. That was where the twelve-winged figures of light came from... and it was also where an extremely ancient temple existed. However, it seemed mostly dark.

There is no True God here.... It should be a good place to hide out.

Xu Qing retracted his divine will and thought for a time. In the end, he decided to wait here until his cultivation base was fully recovered. Only then would he consider leaving.

Blurring into motion, he vanished from the forest of dust. When he reappeared, he was in the distant amethyst mountains. There, he hewed out a mansion grotto and sat down cross-legged inside.

Time passed. The planet rotated. Fire from heaven occasionally fell.

The scaled oxen offered sacrifices thirty times. Their god became increasingly glorious. The chanting of the mushrooms became a requiem to calm the soul as the fire fell, and the mist danced wildly.

The forest of dust continued to take the memories of starlight and weave them together. For some reason, the starlight that it had been absorbing lately contained images of some unknown human civilization.

Within those images was a cultivator with white hair holding his dead wife. His sorrow turned into rage, and he threw his head back and cursed heaven. Eventually, he stepped up into heaven and waged war against the heavenly daos! There was no sound in the image. But the madness of it caused the entire forest of dust to turn as red as blood.

A month passed in which Xu Qing’s cultivation base reached a state of ninety percent recovery. He immersed himself in cultivation. And then one day, when he was just on the verge of complete recovery....

Within the sound of breathing that came from the planet's subterranean meridians, an unfamiliar voice spoke.

“God Emperor Death Departure has issued an imperial order. A human cultivator has fled into one of the millions upon millions of universes here in the Fourth Star Ring. He has taken Goddess Starryeyes captive. All gods will hunt for him. Anyone who provides clues leading to his capture will be given 100 portions of ringsource. Anyone who captures him will be given the dao weapon of a God Lord!”

As soon as the voice rang out, a terrifying stream of divine will swept out of the starry sky and over the entire planet.

1. The literal characters for ‘amethyst’ are violet+crystal. However, this combination is different from the ‘violet crystal’ inside Xu Qing. To be specific, the characters for the one inside Xu Qing are ‘violet+colored+water+crystal’ while here is simply ‘violet+crystal.’ The combination of water+crystal is the common word for crystal (my understanding being that ancient people thought there was a connection between water and crystals). In any case, I’m just rendering these mountains as amethyst because there is not a connection to the violet crystal in Xu Qing. ☜

2. The author transposes the characters that I normally translate as ‘god,’ seemingly to imply that the glowing creatures are not the same species as ‘the gods,’ yet are somehow godly. He did use the divine pronoun for them. This term has never come up before, nor does it come up again, at least not in the chapters I had access to as of translating this chapter. ☜

It was True God will!

Inside the amethyst mountains, Xu Qing’s face fell, and his heart filled with intense fear. His heart started pounding, and the hair on his neck stood on end.

It’s not a single True God. It’s seven True Gods!

His pupils constricted as the entire planet seemed to distort, and all the living beings on it writhed. The emerald-green halos dimmed and lost their color. The encroaching will turned them into black clouds that covered the sky. The combined divine will of so many True Gods was like a huge wave that turned the starry sky into a sea, and made all the planets like islands about to be covered over.

Xu Qing’s fear intensified. It looked like the divine will was about to reach his hiding spot.

At that moment of crisis, Xu Qing wiped out all of the immortal energy he had been using and had Little Shadow spread out to cover him. Starfire didn’t need any prompting; she quickly appeared in the open next to Xu Qing and unleashed a godly aura to further conceal him.

That combination, coupled with the fact that Xu Qing was inherently different from other cultivators, ensured that the mutagen in the area was very strong. But all of that still wasn’t enough.

At the critical moment, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered and he pulled Goddess Starryeyes out of his bag of holding and tossed hēr to Starfire. Starfire immediately understood what Xu Qing wanted. Starfire grabbed the goddess by the throat and covered hēr eyes.

Xu Qing immediately shrank himself down until he was as small as a speck of dust, and then shot toward one of her scapula wounds. Then Xu Qing entered her flesh and used every invisibility technique he could think of!

He was making a gamble! It seemed likely to him that this divine will inspection by the True Gods had a dual purpose.

The first was to look for immortal energy in order to locate him. The other was to look for bloodline evidence or unique ringsource fluctuations to find Goddess Starryeyes.

Although they knew Xu Qing and Starryeyes were together, it made sense to carry out a dual search. However, that method had an inherent flaw. And that flaw was that it overlooked other gods!

Inside and out, Starfire was a god! Even with multiple True Gods combining their divine will, that flaw still remained.

There was always the chance Xu Qing was wrong in his assessment. But there was nothing he could do about that. There was no way he could feel comfortable just leaving Starryeyes on hēr own. There were too many things that could go wrong. So he needed Starfire outside as well, to keep Starryeyes in check. It didn’t matter that Starryeyes was actually unconscious. Xu Qing could not give hēr any opportunity to raise an alarm.

The entire point was to be able to effectively hide inside hēr. As for whether or not hiding would work.... Xu Qing wasn’t completely sure it would work. But he was confident, and that confidence came because... of the power of the seal put into hēr by the Immortal Lord!

Back when I fought that pretty god, hē was obviously taken by surprise when I pulled out the dao weapon. The fact that hē didn’t bring out some treasure specifically designed to counter it shows that hē wasn’t aware that I had the dao weapon.

All the cultivators on the front lines knew, but hē didn’t.... It seems likely that the information about me was concealed by the Immortal Lord, so that the gods didn’t find out. He concealed the information about me and also gave me a dao weapon.... And he left a sealing mark inside the goddess....

As that information flitted through Xu Qing’s mind, the terrifying stream of divine will swept over the area, completely covering the amethyst mountains. Xu Qing stayed alert, his eyes flashing coldly as he prepared for something unexpected to happen. His space-time canon was ready.

But then, an ancient will suddenly erupted from inside Starryeyes. As it spread out, it covered all traces of hēr. Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. In the end, the divine will didn’t notice anything in the amethyst mountains. It quickly swept over the entire planet, then left to inspect other parts of the starry sky.

Xu Qing remained motionless for about two hours until, sure enough, the streams of divine will suddenly returned and checked the entire nebula, including all of the planets in it. After finding nothing, they finally left.

Even then, Xu Qing didn’t do anything. He waited. About four hours later, a third wave of divine will returned to the nebula. These streams of divine will were from different gods. Over the next few days, the same type of thing happened repeatedly. Streams of divine will would suddenly show up, then leave, then come back. Days passed....

Eventually it seemed the event was over.

Xu Qing waited nervously for three more days to make sure the coast was really clear. Only then did he fly out of Starryeyes’ wound and return to his normal form. He looked grimly outside, then turned to Starfire. Starfire had been equally nervous over the past few days, and was only now calming down. Glancing at Starryeyes, shē chose not to speak out loud, and instead transmitted some words to Xu Qing.

“Young Lord, the divine will of those True Gods paid no attention to me after noticing my god altar. It seems to me that thēy were mostly looking for immortal energy. Now that it’s over, my sense is that if you hadn’t hidden in the goddess, my concealment efforts wouldn’t have been enough to keep you safe.”

Xu Qing didn’t say anything. He had come to a similar conclusion as Starfire. The key to avoiding detection had really been the sealing mark left behind by the Immortal Lord.

Did he predict that something like this would happen? Did he leave that sealing mark behind as a life-saving magic?

Xu Qing thought about it for a moment. Well... even if he did predict it, things can’t be going totally as expected. The seal... is not going to last forever in the mutagen-rich environment of the Fourth Star Ring.

Because the sealing mark had activated so many times over the past few days, Xu Qing had been able to sense that it was weakening.

Every time it activated, it got worn down a bit. It seems to me it will only last a few more times before it goes away for good. And when that happens....

He was feeling very uneasy.

Of course, all of the inspections were done by True Gods. And the God Lord sent down orders, but didn’t come personally. And that seems to indicate that the war is still going on, and the God Lord can’t leave the battlefield! I still have time! I need my cultivation base to recover as quickly as possible. Then I’ll find a star chart and figure out how to get back to the Fifth Star Ring!

Xu Qing’s eyes shone with determination. As for this specific location... considering how many times they inspected it, I should be safe here, at least temporarily.

Even as Xu Qing was thinking those things... the divine will of a god appeared again, rumbling through the amethyst mountains. Face falling, Xu Qing once again transformed into a piece of dust that flew into the goddess’ wound.

Moments later, a puzzled look appeared in his eyes. The reason was that the divine will wasn’t very strong. It was not from a True God, but rather, a peak Altar God. It passed quickly through the amethyst mountains before focusing on the dust forest where Xu Qing had originally landed.

As long as it wasn’t True God will, Xu Qing was confident that hiding inside Starryeyes would be sufficient.

After the divine will passed, he emerged again from Starryeyes’ wound. Looking very grim, he grabbed the goddess and slapped hēr across the side of the face.

A thump rang out, and the goddess’s face started to swell up. Opening hēr eyes, shē glared sullenly at him. Shē knew exactly why he had just slapped hēr. He clearly thought that shē had somehow left clues about hēr presence when they teleported to this location. Of course, shē knew that shē hadn’t.... It wasn’t that shē hadn’t wanted to do such a thing, it was just that shē never had time to do it. Xu Qing had woken up before shē could.

The feeling of being wronged caused the hatred within hēr to yet again swell to immense heights.

And shē decided to throw caution to the wind! Before, shē had feared the dao weapon. And the truth was that shē had actually regained consciousness days before, but had been hesitant to call for help because of Starfire. There was no way the damnable Xu Qing was going to let hēr go. Nor would he kill hēr, as he needed hēr to stay hidden. In that case, there didn’t seem any reason to stay scared.

Bubbling with hatred, shē glared murderously at Xu Qing. “If you’ve got what it takes, kill me! I dare you!”

Xu Qing looked back at hēr coldly. “Your father ordered that I be captured, not killed.”

Hēr face stiffened, and shē prepared to talk back to him. He didn’t give hēr the chance. His hand latched onto hēr neck, and he sucked ringsource out of hēr viciously. Inside, his immortal embryo surged, and his soul injuries healed even faster.

Starryeyes wilted, but the hatred in hēr eyes became an unspoken curse. But then, his canon stabbed into hēr scapula and spread through hēr. The pain caused hēr to tremble, but at the same time... it caused ringsource to start building up in hēr again.

Xu Qing continued with the extraction.

In that manner, time passed. A few days later... Xu Qing was very close to reaching complete recovery. As for Starryeyes, shē was hardly more than skin and bones.

That was when something happened that caused Xu Qing to frown. After having been drained out over and over again, the goddess had reached a state that was similar to death. The ringsource produced had slowed to a crawl. It was as if shē had grown used to the provocation.

No further pain would cause hēr to produce any ringsource. And if he pushed things any further, it was entirely possible it could kill hēr .

When Starryeyes realized that, it no longer became possible for hēr to contain hēr hatred and rage.

“Now what are you going to do, Xu Qing??” shē screamed. “So, you’ve tormented me as much as you can? I dare you to kill me! You’ve got nothing left that you can do. I thought you were better than this!

“But guess what? There are infinite things I can do to you. One of these days, you’ll fall into my hands, and then I’ll make sure that you experience ten thousand times as much suffering as I have!”

Xu Qing looked coldly at the hysterical goddess. His eyes narrowed. He was about to return hēr to his bag of holding when he heard Starfire laugh.

“Young Lord, I’ve been watching all this time, and probably should have said something earlier. Your extraction technique isn’t very efficient.” The bewitchingly charming Starfire approached Starryeyes. Licking hēr lips, and hēr eyes glittering excitedly, shē lifted the goddess’ chin with hēr finger. “Let me give you a suggestion....”

Starryeyes had no choice but to look up at Starfire, and hēr eyes were filled with fear. Shē was suddenly feeling very uneasy.

Starfire licked hēr lips and looked Starryeyes up and down. Smiling, shē said, “Young Lord, you’ve been using a very crude method. Haven’t you heard about the concept of showing pity and tender love for women?”

Xu Qing frowned.

“The kind of stimulation you’ve been using is surface-level, and easy to acclimate to. Oh, you! You still just don’t understand gods, and you especially don’t understand female gods....” Smiling, Starfire reached out and slowly ran hēr finger down Starryeyes’ skin.

Starryeyes felt more vigilant than ever. Stiffening, shē glared at Starfire and shouted, “What incredible gall!”

Hēr voice was backed with the personhood of hēr bloodline, which made it especially mighty to other gods. Starfire’s finger stopped moving.

But then, Starfire’s eyes lit up, as if the more Starryeyes acted like this, the more exciting it was.

“That’s the feeling I’m going for!” Heart racing, Starfire leaned over and whispered into the goddess’ ear. “Oh, lil’ sis, don’t you know I’ve been thinking about you for so long now? Make sure to keep acting like this going forward.”

Starryeyes shivered from head to toe, and all of a sudden, the fear rising within hēr made hēr want to flee. That uneasy feeling felt more intense than ever. But shē knew that if shē showed any fear whatsoever, it would completely undermine the facade shē was putting up. With great effort, shē suppressed the fear and glared coldly at Starfire with all the nobility of hēr bloodline.

Starfire chuckled and waved hēr hand. The air rippled, and in the blink of an eye, a white jade altar appeared in the chamber. Starfire shackled Starryeyes to the altar.

Starryeyes’ dilapidated garments then shimmered and flowed as they transformed into a pink, muslin gown.

To improve the experience, Starfire didn’t hold back from imbuing Starryeyes with some ringsource. As a result, the white jade made the ideal background, and the flowing pink muslin accentuated Starryeyes perfectly. Thanks to the ringsource, Starryeyes’ skin was lustrous again. In fact, it was as smooth as flawless white jade. Hēr eyes twinkled like stars in the night sky, while at the same time being filled with the same nobility and coldness as before.

“You puny lesser god!” shē snapped angrily. “You’re despicable! What are you trying to do here??”

“Oh, calm down, lil’ sis. I still need to add some props.” Starfire’s eyes glittered with excitement as shē lifted hēr hand to produce a little red bottle. Shē popped open the bottle, and a fragrant, green oil flew out.

“I made this oil from a gruish plant that grows in god domains. After refining it for a hundred years, I fermented it for a thousand years along with other precious materials. The end result is this truly precious oil. In fact, I wouldn’t even think of using it were it not for your blood being so noble, lil’ sis. I can form this oil into a wax, and then all I’ll be missing is a wick.”

Starfire reached out to Starryeyes’ long hair and plucked away a few strands, which she coiled into a wick. Finally, she combined the oil and the hair to make a green candle!

Starryeyes frowned as shē looked at the candle. Shē wasn’t completely sure what this lesser god was planning to do, but shē was already starting to get an idea.

“You think you can bewitch me?” shē said coolly. “You obviously don’t know anything about superior gods!”

Starfire laughed softly. Then shē snapped her fingers, and the candle lit up. As the flame danced, an incense-like smoke began to fill the chamber and surrounded Starryeyes.

Starryeyes wanted to keep it away, but as the incense smoke reached hēr, it entered hēr through hēr skin. Shē immediately started breathing raggedly. Then hēr pupils constricted as shē realized that there was something very wrong with this incense smoke. All of a sudden, shē was feeling emotions besides the basic instinct to stay alive and avoid death. It was a very foreign feeling to hēr.

Speaking in an airy voice, Starfire said, “The plant I made the oil from only blooms once every 3,000 years. When it blooms, the surrounding 500,000-kilometer area is covered with a dense fog. That fog can degenerate the soul, and produce unimaginable emotions. It does to the gods what the poppy flower can do to mortals.”[1]

Starryeyes shivered in the depths of hēr heart, then used hēr bloodline power to suppress the unfamiliar emotions.

But then Starfire approached the altar with the candle. Tilting the candle forward, shē let a drop of oil splash down... onto the skin of Starryeyes’ neck!

Starryeyes’ suddenly craned hēr neck as golden striations appeared on the snow-white skin of hēr neck. Hēr eyes glittered as powerful emotions went wild within hēr. However, shē quickly used hēr bloodline power to suppress them.

That only seemed to make Starfire more excited, though. Shē tilted the candle again, and started dripping oil on specific spots on the goddess’ body. Every drop was like a tempest striking with heaven-rending, earth-crushing force.

They stabbed through Starryeyes’ defenses and suppression abilities! And they provoked innumerable emotional fluctuations! Starryeyes' insides were in chaos, but shē refused to surrender. Glaring at Starfire, shē revealed no terror, only calmness.

“You despicable lesser god!”

Starfire’s eyebrows shot up.

As for Xu Qing, a strange expression could be seen on his face as he finally stood up. “I’m going to head out for a bit.”

With that, he turned to leave.

Starfire sighed regretfully. Shē had wanted Xu Qing to watch the entire process, but since he wasn’t inclined, shē wouldn’t try to force him. “Don’t worry, Young Lord, everything will be settled by the time you return.”

Xu Qing said nothing. He disappeared.

With Xu Qing gone, Starfire put the candle down, stretched at the waist, and then smiled down at the stubborn Starryeyes.

“It’s fine that he’s gone. Certain things will be more convenient that way.”

Starfire waved hēr hand, and a number of things appeared. There was a rope, some tongs, a whip, some bottles, a gag, and a very large copper mirror....

Starryeyes wasn’t sure how those things were to be used, but hēr heart started pounding nonetheless.

Starfire, meanwhile, licked hēr lips. Cheeks flush with excitement, shē laughed softly. “The fun has just started.”

***

Xu Qing was up in the dome of heaven. By drawing on the local mutagen, and also having Little Shadow cover him, he was confident he wouldn’t be noticed by anything but a True God.

He had come out here because he had no interest in watching Starfire work. More importantly, he needed to get a star chart so that he could start planning a way to leave.

He had already identified the best place to do that. And that was the butterfly god in the temple of the scaled oxen! His previous investigation had indicated that the butterfly was an Altar God, and an early Altar God at that.

Given his current battle prowess, he could deal with such gods easily. His main concerns were acting quickly and staying out of sight. He didn’t want this god to have any clue what was about to happen.

And thus, he stayed invisible as he sped along so fast that he wasn’t visible to the naked eye. In fact, not even someone using divine will would be able to detect him. He eventually appeared on the crystalline plane, in the kingdom of the scaled oxen. Without pausing, he sped undetected into the dark green temple, and shot right toward the forehead of the butterfly statue.

The statue trembled as he pierced into it. It struggled only briefly, then went still. Shortly after, golden blood flowed down the statue, only for it to retract a moment later as if nothing had happened. In fact, there were still followers outside making offerings.

The butterfly’s eyes opened.[2]

Xu Qing did not kill the butterfly god. Rather, he erased the god’s mind, turning īt into an empty shell that he could wear almost like clothing. It was similar to the way he would use Starfire’s aura, and it also gave him access to everything the god knew.

He was currently studying a star chart that the butterfly’s memories contained.

So, we’re over 10,000 universes away from the Fifth Star Ring.... It turns out the gods in the Fourth Star Ring are fairly similar to those in the Revered Ancient mainland. Most of thēm have personal territory with species there that offer worship. And thēy guard thēir borders jealously....

The gods on this planet are no exception. And of course, there are higher level gods that rule over thēm. The Godfolk who rule this planet inhabit the 360 emerald halos. In the past... they produced a True God!

The reason this place was investigated so thoroughly is that the ruling gods discovered some spatial evidence of my passage.... Nothing like that had ever happened on this planet before. Given how big the Fourth Star Ring is, thēy apparently didn’t believe it could be a coincidence.

After some thought, he flew out of the temple in the form of the butterfly. Countless scaled oxen groveled. Ignoring them, Xu Qing flapped the butterfly wings and disappeared into the sky as he shot back toward the amethyst mountains.

I wonder if Starfire has unlocked any of the goddess’ ringsource.

***

In the dark mansion grotto in the amethyst mountains, candlelight flickered. A gentle aura filled the chamber.

Atop the white altar, Starryeyes’ skin was scarlet, and shē was trembling. Shē still wore the pink gown, but shē was tied up with a rope, in a very skillful manner with special knots. In fact, every single knot was tied in a way that made it into a special sealing symbol. Not only did it force hēr into a specific pose, but also, it created a type of tension between hēr soul and body, and if shē struggled, it got tighter.

The rope was made from special materials that glittered with five-colored light that was like a flowing dream. Clearly, it was a material that could plunge someone into an endless illusion. A sense of unease constantly stabbed through Starryeyes, causing hēr to twitch uncontrollably. Shē tried to free hērself from the constant stimulation, but the rope made it impossible to move.

Even more shocking than all of that was the copper mirror hanging above hēr. Whenever shē opened hēr eyes, shē would see hērself reflected in the mirror.

The mental humiliation and the physical discomfort combined, and they were pushing hēr to the brink. And then, Starfire started dropping oil on hēr again.

Starryeyes’ mind spun. All attempts at resistance crumbled, and millions upon millions of streams of fire appeared in hēr pupils. The grandiose look in hēr eyes faded away, crumbling into nothing but dust in the wind.

Love. Hate. Passion. Animosity. The seven emotions and six sensory pleasures erupted. All things from hēr past suddenly meant something completely different. Everything was more colorful. More meaningful. Hēr mind began to collapse, until finally, shē heard someone speaking.

“Welcome to the human world,” Starfire whispered into hēr ear.

1. I feel like I don’t need to put this footnote here, but who knows, maybe some younger readers don’t know that opium and heroin are made from poppies. If you didn’t know before, now you do. More info here. ☜

2. I know that many of you are probably thinking, ‘Hey, don’t butterflies have compound eyes that don’t really open or close?’ Well, you are clearly unaware of the reality of magical xianxia butterflies. Besides, here is evidence that butterflies can open and close their eyes. ☜

By the time Xu Qing got back, everything in the chamber was back to normal. The gentle aura was gone, and a very strange scene met his eyes.

Goddess Starryeyes was sitting there, eyes closed, motionless. Starfire stood behind hēr, combing hēr hair with a wooden comb.

A strange expression could be seen on Xu Qing’s face as he studied the scene. However, he quickly realized that the goddess’ ringsource was no longer overdrawn and locked down. It was thrumming vibrantly. A lot had already built up.

He couldn’t help but look at Starfire. Shē chuckled.

“Young Lord, in the future, don’t treat lil’ sis Starryeyes so crudely. Shē’s agreed to cooperate going forward. Isn’t that right, lil’ sis Starryeyes?” Starfire leaned down and exhaled softly into Starryeyes’ ear.

Starryeyes shivered, then opened hēr eyes and looked at Xu Qing. Somehow, the hatred in those eyes had significantly diminished. No longer did shē think of Xu Qing as being a nightmare. He had been extracting hēr ringsource to use in cultivation. That was all. The standing between the two of them had long since been established.

The real nightmare was the god behind hēr. Starfire was fiendish, even abyssal. Shē was a vile devil that would forever lurk in Starryeyes’ heart.

Considering Starryeyes had the blood of a God Lord in hēr, it meant hēr ringsource was unusually pure. Being a noble, no one had ever treated hēr badly growing up. Therefore, when shē was flooded with emotions and had a mental breakdown... shē realized that she was no longer pure. Hēr mind was filled with the seven emotions and six sensory pleasures. Countless unfamiliar emotions had assailed her. Shē had descended from being a god.

Thus, after looking at Xu Qing, shē lifted hēr hand. Ringsource pulsed into hēr palm, which she sent directly to Xu Qing. It entered his eyes, ears, nose, and mouth, flowing through him so that his cultivation base stirred.

Xu Qing’s expression became even more shocked. The ringsource was very different when she gave it to him as opposed to him taking it. For example, he didn’t need to remove hēr will from it. It was far more pure.

“How’d you do it?” he asked Starfire. He wasn’t asking about what shē had done after pulling out that candle. Instead, he wanted to know the logic and reasoning involved.

Chuckling, Starfire continued to comb Starryeyes’ hair. “Normally speaking, it would have been very difficult for me to tug at lil’ sis Starryeyes’ heartstrings. That’s especially true considering that shē was once a True God. But the sealing mark on hēr cut off all of that and made it impossible for hēr to fight back. Of course, you provided a lot of assistance, Young Lord. The way you extracted all of hēr ringsource really put hēr on the brink of collapse.

“All I did was apply a little bit of a push at the right time.... And thus, lil’ sis Starryeyes came to the human world. And the lock became unlocked, all on its own.” Starfire blinked a few times and then looked at Xu Qing. “By the way, Young Lord, did things go well just now?”

Xu Qing looked at Starfire, then Starryeyes, and then decided not to ask for any more details.

“We can leave now. I’ve identified a better place to hide out. As for hēr... I’ll have you look after hēr from now on. You’re confident you can avoid any slip ups?”

Starfire’s eyes lit up. “Don’t worry, Young Lord. I never make mistakes.”

Starfire flicked hēr sleeve to collect up Starryeyes, and then turned into a stream of light that shot into Xu Qing’s palm. There, shē turned into a special symbol.

Xu Qing walked outside and erased all traces of the mansion grotto’s existence. Then he flew up into the sky over the amethyst mountains, where he turned back into the multicolored butterfly. He flapped his wings, and seven-colored light swirled as he flew away.

The location he had mentioned to Starfire was the temple in the kingdom of the scaled oxen. The scaled oxen were all prostrated as Xu Qing returned in butterfly form. Flying back into the temple, he transformed back into a statue. Godly might pulsed from the statue, spreading from the temple to fill the entire kingdom.

Upon sensing it, the scaled oxen folded up their wings and prostrated piously. The priests among them emitted excited hooting sounds, which was their language, in which they described the miracles of the gods.

Xu Qing looked out at the scene calmly. In the following days, he was the turtledove occupying the magpie’s nest. He wore the butterfly god like a second skin, and essentially became that god! It kept him even better concealed than before.

He had made a new decision about leaving this planet. He hadn’t just used the butterfly’s memories to check how far away he was from the war. He had also identified a nearby teleportation portal. It belonged to the Godfolk who had once produced a True God on this planet.

According to the butterfly god’s memories, there was no True God among them anymore. It was a peak Altar God. That said, even if an Altar God did show up, he had a plan. If he tried to force his way to the portal, and everything went smoothly, then of course that would be great. But if the slightest thing went wrong, he would be exposed. And if he was exposed, resulting in a True God showing up, then it could endanger his chances of teleporting away. After considering the situation, he decided to avoid doing anything rash.

And that was because... soon enough, an opportunity would present itself. According to the butterfly’s memories, it was only a few months before that the ruling gods on this planet had sent out a recruitment announcement. They were enlisting local gods to enter their special pocket realm.

And that pocket realm was located in the very depths of the planet! That, combined with what Xu Qing had noticed with his own divine will, led him to the conclusion that it was the same place where he had heard the sounds of breathing as if from subterranean meridians.

The best time for me to leave will be when they’re going into that pocket realm! That’s two months from now....

He already had an idea of how to make sure this butterfly form wasn’t forced to participate in the pocket realm event.

I’d rather not use the butterfly form to travel the long way through the sea of stars, all the while trying to avoid other gods. The teleportation portal is definitely the safest option. That will be the fastest way to make the journey to the edge of the Fourth Star Ring. Now, as for breaking through the star ring barriers....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered. He had the star ring hemp as well as his Sageheaven Pagoda. So he was fairly certain he could break through the star ring barriers to get back home. With that thought in mind, he closed his eyes. Remaining in the butterfly statue form, he absorbed the ringsource willingly given by Starryeyes, and worked on his cultivation.

Time passed.

Because gods were independent entities with personal territory, no one had any idea that he had possessed the butterfly god. Another reason was that many of the gods had already responded to the recruitment message by the ruling gods, and had traveled to the emerald halos to prepare for the coming event. It also helped that he was already familiar with how gods operated, and also had the help of Starfire. freewebnovel.com

Given all those factors, he had no trouble staying hidden. That said, he still had no way to truly avoid the divine will of True Gods.

A few days later, the divine will of True Gods once again appeared in the starry sky. By means of the Immortal Lord’s sealing mark in Starryeyes, he was able to avoid detection.

But... there were still several days left until the pocket realm event. Perhaps it was because the True Gods had not yet found what God Emperor Death Departure was looking for... that thēir search continued. This time, thēy were being very meticulous. And most importantly, thēy were not making the same mistake thēy had made before. The True Gods weren’t just looking for evidence of Starryeyes and immortal energy. They were also checking ordinary gods! They were closing the net, and were being very careful to fish out anything suspicious.

The experience left Xu Qing with a sinking feeling. The problem wasn’t just that Starfire could be detected. The fact that he had possessed another god was also a danger. Otherwise, he and Starfire could just hide inside Starryeyes. But despite how cooperative the goddess had been, Xu Qing still didn’t want to give hēr a chance to betray him. He was facing quite a quandary.

Just now the divine will of two True Gods very nearly noticed me.... Is it possible they got some new information? Do they know that I’m working with a god? Or do they possibly know that I have a way to possess gods?

Xu Qing frowned. Of course, when it rains, it pours. Not only were the True Gods being much more thorough in searching, but also, the Immortal Lord’s sealing mark in Starryeyes was on the verge of disappearing.

It’ll last for another seven days at the most.... Xu Qing was really starting to feel uneasy. I can’t keep gambling that only two True Gods will be looking for me at the same time!

He was just about to make a decision about what to do when Starfire suddenly spoke up.

“Young Lord, I have a secret magic.... Actually, it’s the first part of a special god magic that allows me to fuse my godly aura with the outside world, and then boost the range of other god magics. If the outside world has no other godly auras, then using the technique will attract attention. But if there are other godly auras present, then I can mix my aura with them... and become a part of the chaos.”

The truth was that Starfire was also starting to get anxious. Shē knew full well that if Xu Qing was captured, and it came to light what shē had done to Starryeyes, then hēr fate would be exponentially worse than Xu Qing’s. After all, the God Lord had ordered that Xu Qing be captured alive.... Therefore, shē was wracking hēr brains to try to come up with an idea.

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered in response to hēr suggestion. “Are you saying that, since we can’t stay hidden for much longer, we might as well go somewhere crowded?”

“Exactly,” Starfire said. “Young Lord, it will achieve the same result of keeping us hidden. At the very least... we can buy some time and increase our chances of success!”

“How confident are you that it will work?” he asked.

“Fifty percent...” shē replied hesitantly.

He thought about it, then nodded. “Teach me the technique. We can use it together!”

Shē quickly used divine will to transmit the technique to him. It wasn’t difficult. After studying it briefly, he mastered it. After that, he showed no further hesitation.

“If we’re looking for a place with a lot of auras, there’s one obvious choice.”

With that, he disappeared from within the temple, and reappeared in the dome of heaven. From there, he shot... toward the 360 emerald-green halos.

The species of ruling gods on this planet were called the True Radiants. According to the rules in the Fourth Star Ring, only species that had produced a True God could be honored by adding “True” to their name.

The memories of the butterfly god indicated that the True Radiants didn’t just rule this one planet. Thēy actually controlled the entire nebula, as well as a few nearby universes. Originally speaking, that should have lasted forever. After all, a True God that died could come back. So unless another True God came along to disrupt the balance, nothing would change.

But something unexpected ended up happening to the species. Thēir True God had perished some years earlier and had never returned.... The consequences of that situation slowly manifested as the True Radiants lacked the power to control all the species in the area thēy controlled. Gradually, thēir territory shrank, until only a dozen or so planets would heed thēir recruitment calls.

It wasn’t very common for True Gods to fail to return, but it also wasn’t unheard of. Normally speaking, it meant that thēy had suffered from some sort of targeted attack during thēir return.

Xu Qing himself had participated in things like that. The first time it happened, he had been the bait.... That was the time that Yu Liuchen wanted to hook a returning True God.[1]

So, the secret of how True Gods return isn’t some ironclad situation. Over the ages, both gods and cultivators have studied it.... Some glories only exist in the past.

Xu Qing in butterfly form got closer and closer to the 360 emerald-green halos. He could already sense that there were a lot of gods gathered there. This was enlistment headquarters for the now-shrunken territories controlled by the True Radiants. And it was the crowded location that Xu Qing felt was most suitable to use Starfire’s secret technique.

Hopefully it works!

Of course, he already had contingency plans ready in case it failed. So with a final burst of speed, he appeared right in front of the 360 halos. Emerald light spread out, along with godly might. Without pausing for a moment, Xu Qing flapped his wings and entered.

Everything was emerald-colored as far as the eye could see. Even the air itself seemed to be that color. It was like a giant painting unfurled in front of him. It was a painting full of exquisite detail, with countless lines forming a larger outline of something. The larger outline was somewhat abstract, making it difficult to identify it at first glance. It looked mostly like a conglomeration of random shapes.

Xu Qing narrowed his eyes suspiciously as he studied it. It didn’t take long for him to realize that there was something very strange going on.

That image....

The image wasn’t really abstract. That was just the word someone would use to describe it if they didn’t understand it. In truth, because of Xu Qing's mental acuity and cultivation base, what he saw was an image of heaven and earth. It was a world.

It was just... the three-dimensional world of living beings and inanimate objects, painted with a brush onto a canvas. Given that, a single look revealed something bizarre, distorted, and abstract.

There’s no way an Altar God could make something like this. It’s definitely on the level of a True God. Don’t tell me that what’s visible on the inside... is what causes the surroundings to be distorted by godly might?

More curious than ever, Xu Qing approached the painting. However, that was when numerous streams of divine will emerged from the world in the painting. At the same time, numerous gods could be seen in the fragmented painting, who were the source of the divine will. There were well over a hundred, ranging from gods with true flame to Flawless Gods. There were even some Altar Gods.

A few were very eye-catching to Xu Qing.

One bore the form of an evil bronze eye covered with rust. Astonishingly, the pupil of the eye was a bronze bell. Outside of the pupil was flowing stardust, as well as a host of tentacles with suction pads on the ends. As this god breathed, the pupil expanded and contracted, and the bell would chime in a godly voice.

Another god was even more bizarre. That god looked like a wizened old woman, completely naked, with hēr skin covered with strange bumps. The bumps were actually a total of 36,000 planets with human faces, flowing beneath hēr skin. The dried-up hair that flowed behind hēr was connected to 10,000,000 ancient corpses that floated along, each of them reciting funeral sutras from different past epochs.

Another of the gods embodied the polar opposites of withering and growth. Half of hīs body was covered in flowering crab-apples that offered glimpses of past lives, while the other half looked like a charred tree with chunks of it falling off. Floating within hīs chest cavity were nine bronze soul lamps, within the flames of which were drowning god souls. Hīs legs were rooted in chaotic space-time, with hīs left foot stepping on an ice age, and hīs right foot stepping on a scorching planetary core. [2]

That last god was the most eye-catching to Xu Qing, as he could sense upon hīm a godly authority similar to his own canon.

What was more, Xu Qing could tell that most of these gods were not local to his planet. That was why thēy appeared in their godly forms. It was also their method of establishing thēir standing among each other, similar to how cultivators would use a dao will to do the same.

This is a great opportunity....

Starfire could tell what Xu Qing was thinking. Working together, the two of them could use the butterfly’s godly form and the secret magic to blend into the outside world.

Xu Qing seemed to vibrate as the butterfly began to transform.

The wings spread out, and they looked like millstones of reincarnation. Each wing was woven from the skin of unknown living beings, and were filled with glowing crimson light that could absorb the void. Astonishingly, the front wings each had 9,600 compound eyes that wept blood, with pupils full of lightning. And each flap of the wings would cause a sound to echo out like souls wailing in the underworld. They seemed to be responding to the divine will of the host of gods.

Even more gruish was that the butterfly’s antennae encircled a crimson river. The antennae had bifurcated ends, upon which hung rust-colored netherworld lamps. The flapping of the butterfly’s wings seemed to conform to a specific cadence. Within the left wing was a tide of nirvanic extermination, while the right wing contained the sweet dew of extreme beginnings. And the dust scattered by the flapping of the wings contained millions upon millions of scaled oxen, all prostrated in worship. This was the godly form of the butterfly Xu Qing had possessed.

The gods that had sent the divine will over seemed respectful now. Those that had stood out to Xu Qing seemed to rein in their auras a bit. They allowed Xu Qing to enter the painting, and take an empty spot there.

At the same time, a godly voice echoed out.

“Everdoom Netherfly! I haven’t seen you for a hundred years! Looks like you’re not far from a breakthrough.”
