As the words were spoken, a huge black lotus rose up within the painting. Inside the black lotus was a dwarf seated cross-legged. The dwarf was pitch black and surrounded by 360 ancient corpses, each of which pulsed with extraordinary power.

Visible on the dwarf’s forehead was a golden stud that was an accumulation of the blood of a True God. Emerald halos flickered in hīs pupils, and hē was fiddling with a scale that emitted a sound that shook the entire painting, and caused all the gods therein to bow thēir heads.

This was the True Radiant god who was in charge of the planet. From the memories of the butterfly god, Xu Qing knew that this god was the one who had issued the recruitment message.

Xu Qing bowed his head in a show of respect. freewebnovel.com

The dwarf nodded and said nothing further. Closing hīs eyes, hē went back to meditating atop the black lotus.

Everything went quiet. The gods were all waiting.

Xu Qing went from the godly form back to the normal form. However, with the help of Starfire’s secret magic, he made sure that his aura was mixed in with all the other auras present. He stayed in that state as time passed.

Three days went by fairly quickly. The appointed day was approaching. During the three days that passed, a few dozen additional gods arrived. Most were from other planets, but a few were like the butterfly god and came from this planet. They included the lightning worshiped by the humanoids and the god of the mushroom people.

The divine will of True Gods scanned the area a number of times. On one occasion, it was the combined divine will of three True Gods. Xu Qing kept his guard up, but Starfire’s technique worked well. Thēy never noticed Xu Qing. The other gods had become used to the inspections, and didn’t resist in any way.

As long as there isn’t an inspection by five True Gods, then this secret magic should keep me hidden. Only two more days... and then when these gods leave, I can make my escape!

Those last two days seemed to crawl by. Thankfully, everything went smoothly, and the True Gods never noticed Xu Qing.

At long last, the day came. All of the gods released thēir auras, and the dwarf on the black lotus opened hīs eyes and waved hīs hand. A host of black stones flew out and came to hover in front of each of the gods. When Xu Qing took the stone in front of him, he realized that it was a seal made by the godhood of a True God. The stone wouldn't be of much use to him, but it could be very helpful to a god seeking to achieve a breakthrough.

“Ladies and gentlemen, these are the true god stones mentioned in the agreement. True god stones have also been prepared for after we explore the pocket realm. And now... let’s be off!”

The drop of golden blood on the dwarf’s forehead became a beam of golden light. The beam turned into an emerald-colored halo, within which, the outside world was visible. Teleportation ripples began to spread out. Gods were already moving toward the halos and disappearing.

As the gods began to depart, Xu Qing prepared to implement the escape method he had prepared. Unfortunately, just before he did, an extremely dangerous development occurred.

The majestic will of some True Gods appeared in the starry sky. The combined divine will swept through all the planets in the nebula. And this time, there were ten True Gods!

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted, and his heart started pounding. He knew that if the divine will swept over him, he would be exposed. As the crisis mounted, he unhesitatingly abandoned his plan and shot toward the halo and jumped inside.

He vanished.

It was a gloomy world. A thick, pitch-black substance like bitumen surrounded the world, creating something like an exterior shell around it. Inside the world, the sky was full of dark red striations that spread out almost like a spider web. Drops of blood oozed out of the striations, falling down onto lands riddled with holes. It was like rain.

In the middle of the striations that leaked the rain of blood, high in the canopy of heaven, there was an astonishing sight. It was a massive tumor! Īt looked like a dead sun high overhead, or perhaps some misshapen god that had parasitized this world, creating an incomparably gruish and eerie sensation.

Xu Qing and all the other gods who had disappeared into the halo... were now materializing into that rain. This was where they had been teleported to.

Upon appearing in the gruish blood rain, the gods instinctively scanned the area. Clearly... this was the first time any of thēm had been to this place.

Xu Qing was there, and he surveyed the surroundings more thoroughly. He didn’t just scan the world, he also scanned the area outside of it. Thankfully, he was now isolated from the danger he had sensed earlier, thanks to the unique properties of this place. The divine will in the starry sky could not come here. That realization caused Xu Qing to breathe a sigh of relief. At the same time, he was now a lot more curious about this strange world.

So this place isn’t the location of that earth meridian I sensed?

Xu Qing looked up at the dome of heaven. Upon noting the blood-red striations and the gruish ball of flesh, his pupils constricted. Just looking at the tumor gave him an idea of what might be going on here.

He looked down at the ground. The lands were black, and when the blood rain fell, it created a sludge that looked like a festering scar. Countless blood-red imps came to life when the blood rain fell. They had no facial features, and they just numbly went about doing specific forms of hard labor. Off in the distance were successive mountain ranges that looked like the flayed bones of enormous beasts.

The valleys in between the mountains were full of thick fog. Within that fog were withered trees, monstrous and distorted in appearance. Their bark was a pale, sickly color, and their roots looked like fractured vertebrates strung together. They had long, thin branches that reached up into the sky like hands trying to grasp the canopy of heaven! But when the blood rain fell on them, it corroded them, causing them to leak black sap that converged and grew into umbrella-like mushrooms that could block the rain. The mushroom umbrellas came in all sizes. From what Xu Qing could tell, the big ones were in locations where there were many withered trees, and they were the size of cities.

Beneath the umbrellas grew numerous pustules that almost resembled grapes. Atop the mushrooms were delicate crystals that emitted a glimmering light that contained both illusion and reality.

It was the light that caught Xu Qing’s attention. Apparently, the glimmering light contained a vast minor world! The world seemed to be hiding something as it flickered in and out of view within the angular surfaces of the crystals.

Xu Qing felt even more curious than ever. It’s almost like heaven and earth are at war here!

He came to that conclusion after noting the specific type of work the imps in the blood rain were doing. They had axes that they would use to hack at the withered trees. Each blow of an ax would leave a scar on the trunk of a tree. In other areas, the axes hacked against the rocks on the mountains, causing sparks to fly, along with what appeared to be fragments of teeth and nails.

Apparently, the trees and mountains in this place were living things! Furthermore, there was danger in the work being done by the imps!

As Xu Qing observed, he saw an area in one of the mountain ranges where the imps were at work with their axes. All of a sudden, the withered trees there spasmed. An instant later, a host of mushroom umbrellas sprang out of those trees, covering the grape-like pustules and causing them to explode!

Innumerable streams of sap then swept out like threads that stabbed toward the imps. The skin of the imps that were touched turned as gray as ash. Then, that skin would crack, and red light would seep out from within before they exploded.

Xu Qing’s gaze hardened. He could now see what was really going on in this world.

This is the work of two terrifying True Gods, presumably, peak True Gods! One is up above, one is down below, and this is the manner in which thēy fight each other.

Given this strange state of affairs, thēy must be at an impasse. The True God in the sky wants to break the world apart. Hīs strategy is to send hīs own god blood down, which turns into those imps, which then try to chop down the trees and break apart the mountains. The trees and mountains are the other True God, who is fighting back, but has gradually lost the initiative in the fight.

So, what do the True Radiants want to accomplish here...?

Xu Qing’s mind raced as he kept his guard up. Meanwhile the other surrounding gods were also closely studying the surroundings.

Finally, the True Radiant dwarf seated cross-legged on the black lotus spoke. “Although all of you are mere subservient gods under our rulership, because you answered our call, I won’t hide things from you any longer. Everybody on the outside believes that our True Radiant True God perished years ago, and cannot return, but the truth is... that our True Radiant True God isn’t dead at all. Hē’s right here!”

The dwarf stood and pointed at the huge black tumor. “Hē set a trap and is now on the verge of assimilating another True God! Your mission here is to help our True God by clearing the trees and mountains. You will alleviate some of the pressure our True God faces, and ensure that hē can complete the assimilation process.

“When the time comes that our True God awakens, all of you subservient gods will be handsomely rewarded. And there will be other benefits as well. You will be granted god seals that can be used to gain one-time protection from our True God.”

Most of the gods who had teleported here were, in the strict hierarchy of the gods, subsidiary to the True Radiants, and thus had no objection to the mission. After receiving the instructions, the gods prepared their various god magics and then headed toward either the withered trees or the wild mountains.

Of course, only those who were at the Altar God level qualified to consider the pros and cons of the situation. Those were the gods that Xu Qing had taken special note of earlier. After further communication with the dwarf via divine will, those gods nodded and joined the effort to help the True Radiants’ True God.

However, thēy did not work at felling trees or chopping mountains. Instead, thēy flew up into the dome of heaven and settled down in the air cross-legged around the black tumor. From those positions, thēy sent their godly aura into the mass of flesh. By connecting directly with the True God in that manner, thēy could help alleviate some of the pressure hē faced.

Offering their godly auras to help the True God was like throwing a cup of water on a burning cart of firewood. However, having even a bit of additional help to alleviate pressure in critical moments would still be of help to this True God.

That was when Xu Qing heard the dwarf speaking into his mind via divine will.

“This entire mission came about because our True God used a bloodline magic to summon me. Hē is hovering on the brink of fully assimiliating. Since you’re an Altar God, you can send your god power into the canopy of heaven and connect directly to the True God. After our True God awakens, you will be bestowed a fragment of godhood!”

That was a very enticing reward. But Xu Qing... had no way of helping out.

In the end, he wasn’t a god. Given the circumstances, he couldn’t actually connect to a True God without his true identity being exposed. All in all, this was a peak True God. In fact, even just being this close felt very dangerous to him.

He sighed inwardly. Here in this star ring of the gods, there were wolves in front of him and tigers behind him. It made it really hard to do just about anything.

“Oh, Exalted God,” he said, “this is a very important matter in which mistakes cannot be tolerated. My level isn’t sufficient for me to be of any help here. Can I request that you simply activate the teleportation and let me leave?”

Xu Qing even sent the true god stone flying back to the dwarf. He had only come here as a last resort. And though it didn’t seem likely he would be able to leave, he wanted to at least try. Being able to leave would be the ideal outcome. But if it didn’t work... well, it chilled his heart to think about it.

As of now, Xu Qing and the dwarf were the only ones left hovering in the rain of blood.

In response to Xu Qing’s request, the dwarf expressionlessly lifted a finger and tapped the true god stone. The black stone trembled and then collapsed into ashes that quickly dissipated.

Hē looked coldly at Xu Qing. “Either cooperate or die.”

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered dangerously. But then, the huge black tumor in the network of red striations suddenly started twitching. Astonishingly, a crack spread out, and then opened up. It looked like a huge eye opening up.

When the eye opened, a turbid gaze emerged, dropping down... to land on Xu Qing. All of a sudden, the dark red light in the sky seemed to become viscous, and the entire world started to tremble and distort. Chanting spread out through heaven and earth.

Xu Qing shivered. The gaze that had settled on him seemed corporeal, and it was like he could hear the sounds of blood flowing, bones snapping, and the scream of the butterfly’s discarnate spirit being incinerated. In an instant, the husk of the butterfly shriveled up. It couldn’t sustain the force of the gaze, and it exploded. A boom rang out.

Xu Qing's true body was revealed. freewebnovel.com

At that instant, a sound like that of a fetal heartbeat rang out from inside the black tumor. It was so loud that it caused the rocky surfaces of the mountain to tremble. An immense pressure was about to descend from the tumor, except, right then, all of the mountains and trees seemed to have found an opportunity to fight back. The lands trembled, the mountains shook, and numerous branches shot up toward the sky.

The black tumor hesitated, and then a howl echoed out from nowhere. The eye had no choice but to close, and focus completely on defending against the attack.

Heaven and earth once again went back to fighting each other.

Meanwhile, the dwarf’s gaze sharpened as hē apparently received a transmitted message. Hīs eyes glowed as the 360 ancient corpses all around hīm opened their eyes and looked at Xu Qing.

“You’re not a god. You’re a cultivator! Don’t tell me that you’re... the very same cultivator that God Emperor Death Departure listed as wanted for the kidnapping of Her Grace Starryeyes??”

Atop the black lotus, the eyes of the dwarf glowed with an increasingly intense golden color. Hē had not been born as a god. Granted, hīs species had produced a True God, but they were not Godfolk in the most accurate sense. Rather, they had worked hard to produce gods.

That was just how things worked according to the rules of the Fourth Star Ring. The ringsource that gods needed could be extracted from the star ring itself, but there was an even better way to get it. It could be extracted from the faith of worshipers.

If a god wanted to get strong, that god needed believers that could make offerings and sacrifices. That was how gods could actually invade countless worlds. The more slaves thēy had, the more worship thēy could get from the masses!

That was the case with the butterfly Xu Qing had possessed. Everdoom Netherfly had no blood relation to the scaled oxen. But the scaled oxen worshiped the butterfly, and that was the foundation of hīs cultivation. In fact, it wasn’t just the scaled oxen on that one planet who worshiped hīm. There were other species on other minor worlds who also offered such worship. As long as hē didn’t perish, and had the good fortune to eventually step into the True God level, then all species who worshiped hīm would benefit as a result.

At that point, the scaled oxen as well as all of the other species who worshiped hīm would be able to add the word True to their species name. They would also be able to expand their territory and become powerful rulers of all the surrounding lands. And yet, substructurally speaking, those species weren’t gods.

They worshiped their True God and had the word True in their species name, which meant that it was easier for them to gather god power and godliness. By getting the blessing of their True God to ignite their godfire, then they could become a god.

Those newly born gods would be considered followers of the original True God, and could go out to find thēir own worshipers. It was like a tree sending out more and more roots in all directions.

The True Radiants were a good example. They were not the only species that worshiped this specific True God. However, after having the word True added to their species name, their sphere of influence expanded beyond the nebula. And at their peak, they had controlled many, many universes.

A species like that might seem glorious, but in reality, they were one of the most lowly types of Godfolk in the Fourth Star Ring. There was more progress they could make.... As time passed, if every member of the species could change their blood into that of the gods, then they would truly be Godfolk.

The vast majority of Godfolk in the Fourth Star Ring were one of those two varieties. As for the latter, if they could proliferate and produce multiple True Gods, or perhaps even a God Lord, then they could consolidate all of their worshipers into one unified species! And then... the personhood of their species as a whole would advance. They would become an imperial clan!

However, that was extremely difficult to do, and over the countless years that had passed, only a few species had ever done that.

The dwarf, who was a postheaven god, had guessed that Xu Qing was the very person declared wanted by God Emperor Death Departure. As a result, hīs eyes shone with golden light, and hīs heart was pounding. Hē was fully aware that this was likely the most amazing good fortune and destined opportunity that hē had ever encountered in life!

After all, any reward given by God Emperor Death Departure would be astounding. Even just providing clues would bring a hundred portions of ringsource. And capturing this person alive... would bring the weapon of a God Lord!

Therefore, the dwarf sliced hīs hand through the air overhead, and then spoke in a thunderous godly voice.

“All subordinate gods present have a new mission. Immediately attack and capture this cultivator!”

His words caused wild colors to flash in heaven and earth. All of the gods working with the trees and mountains looked up, then shot straight toward Xu Qing.

Up above, the handful of Altar Gods seated cross-legged around the tumor looked down at Xu Qing. However, none of thēm moved a muscle. The True God wouldn’t permit it!

The dwarf didn’t care. Although helping the True God was still important, comparatively speaking... if hē could get that reward from God Emperor Death Departure, the weapon of a God Lord, then for hīm to become a True God wasn’t out of the question! After all, coming from a species that had a True God provided inherent advantages. That wasn’t to mention that there were plenty of Altar Gods to offer support. Therefore, as long as hē captured this person quickly, there would still be time to offer help to the True God.

Having reached this point in hīs train of thought, the dwarf leaped off of the black lotus, bringing the 360 corpses along. Peak Altar God power raged as hē closed in on Xu Qing.

Withering corruption spread out in all directions as the corpses all opened their mouths and howled in gruish voices. It turned into a wind of corpses that filled the area. This was none other than hīs godly authority. The power of withering and a wind of death. It was... a voice that demanded life. It all combined into a terrifying dirge of death. The melody became like a physical object that shot toward Xu Qing.

Xu Qing’s eyes flashed with cold light. He knew that, being in the Fourth Star Ring, avoiding detection was a matter of luck. And therefore, he had been prepared for it to happen at any time.

Actually, being exposed in this situation is better than it happening outside. That said, my main goal in this fight is going to be to escape.

Eyes narrowing, he suddenly shifted, causing himself to become a blur. Instantly, time seemed to become chaos around him, as though it were flowing differently than the surrounding world. At the same time, the area around the dwarf distorted, causing hīs dirge of death to suddenly become distorted.

As the god magic was broken, an iron skewer flew out of the distorted aspects of time. Immortal energy glittered in heaven and earth, along with the chiming sound of a bell. Instantly, all magical techniques in the area lurched to a halt.

The dwarf, who had been charging right toward Xu Qing, looked astonished. Hē could clearly sense hīmself suddenly losing connection to the godly aura within.

The iron skewer shot with astonishing speed toward hīm. An intense sensation of deadly crisis erupted within hīm.

As the crisis hit, the dwarf bit hīs tongue off and spat it out. As the severed tongue sprayed golden god blood, it grew larger in gruish fashion until it turned into a huge tumor. Apparently, it was able to call out to the tumor of the True God up in the dome of heaven. The two connected.

In that manner, the dwarf was able to borrow True God power and send it erupting out. The tongue-turned-tumor then opened like an eye. The gaze locked onto the incoming iron skewer, wrapping around it and isolating it. The gaze also landed on Xu Qing’s distortions of time, causing the distortions to fade into nothing. Xu Qing was revealed.

By this point, the dwarf’s godly aura was restored. Eyes blazing with killing intent, hē let loose hīs trump card. The 360 corpses around hīm erupted into flames.

What was more, the air beneath Xu Qing’s feet filled with dozens of golden rifts! Out of them emerged 36 three-eyed god statues, which were formed from the 360 corpses. The moment thēir feet touched the air outside, a crisp sound rang out like breaking glass. Vertical eyes opened on thēir foreheads, out of which poured dark golden light, like a corrupting waterfall heading right toward Xu Qing. Wherever it passed, everything became as solid as amber.

Xu Qing’s black robe fluttered as the godlight fell toward him. Then he extended his right hand and pushed out. Instantly, the canon of space converged, and the scattered fragments of time around him merged, forming space-time canon. A space-time tempest instantly erupted.

It was a heaven-shaking, earth-shattering tempest that shot up to meet the dwarf’s descending godlight. Within the tempest were innumerable immortal sealing marks. And they all erupted!

A massive boom echoed out in the world. Godlight shattered. The 36 god statues exploded. The thick black fog roiled, and the dwarf’s face fell as hē began to retreat at top speed.

In the blink of an eye, Xu Qing appeared right behind hīm. Reaching out, he put his hand on top of the dwarf’s head.

Simultaneously, the iron skewer, which had been halted in place by the gaze of the tumor, glittered brightly. The bell chimed again, and the iron skewer broke free, becoming a blinding streak that shot through the air. It stabbed right into the pit of the dwarf’s stomach, pierced all the way through, and then appeared next to Xu Qing.

However, Xu Qing was actually frowning.

The dwarf god in front of him was trembling and transforming into a black lotus. The lotus shattered; it was a case of death substitution!

Off in the distance, the dwarf god formed anew, eyes glittering with lingering fear. Truth be told, hē was not surprised by how things were going. Hē knew full well that if God Emperor Death Departure had marked someone as wanted, and that person could evade the divine will inspections of many True Gods, then he wasn’t going to be a weakling.

“But this is the god kingdom of a True God!”

As the dwarf’s words rang out, nine burning clumps of flesh appeared above Xu Qing’s head. Merging into a cage, they dropped toward him.

Meanwhile, the host of other gods had finally arrived, and were launching all sorts of god magics at him. And yet, even as those attacks closed in, the cage of nine lumps of flesh surrounded him.

Xu Qing vanished, having become millions upon millions of blood-red butterflies that flew out in every direction. On the wings of the bizarre red butterflies were countless designs that looked like eyes. And every beat of the butterflies’ wings caused a god magic to be sucked into the eyes.

Even more bizarre was that the moment Xu Qing transformed into millions upon millions of butterflies, something happened to the eyes of many of the gods below. Masses of blood butterfly larvae appeared there! And then, after only three heartbeats of time passed, the gods began to scream and howl as the larva formed hives, out of which flew numerous blood butterflies.

This was a god magic that Xu Qing had learned from Everdoom Netherfly. However, when being unleashed by Xu Qing, it had a range far more terrifying than the butterfly god had ever been capable of.

Red butterflies fluttered everywhere, with about half of them flying toward the nine burning clumps of flesh, while the others headed toward the host of gods. Those who were only in the Godfire level scattered in terror. And yet, Xu Qing suddenly appeared right behind a female god.

Reaching out with his right hand, he stabbed his fingers into hēr spine. And with his left hand, he grabbed hēr godsource and extracted a glowing orb that was hēr memories. He crushed it open and absorbed it. This god had blue skin with black marks like a spiderweb under the surface. Shē didn’t have much ringsource, so it hardly took a moment to absorb it all. It rushed into Xu Qing, whereupon the god withered into a desiccated corpse.

Very impure ringsource. And not much of it.

Having sampled the ringsource of Goddess Starryeyes, other ringsource... wasn’t very impressive to Xu Qing. He had a very refined palette now....

Waving his hand, he tossed aside the corpse. At the same time, dozens of other corpses dropped from the sky. They fell from the red butterflies that were manifestations of Xu Qing!

After absorbing the ringsource, the butterflies converged, turning into Xu Qing’s true form, hovering in midair. He looked around expressionlessly. Then he reached out, grabbed a god that was hiding, and dragged the god out.

This god was made of crystals. Before the god could speak, Xu Qing shattered the crystals into a host of fragments. Each fragment reflected the terrified faces of the other gods.

One of them was the unsightly face of the dwarf.

“There’s still time to start the teleportation and let me out,” Xu Qing said.

Xu Qing had a clear goal here, and it wasn’t to kill everyone. It was to escape.

If this True Radiant dwarf wanted to avoid fighting, all it would take was a teleportation. Although Xu Qing usually preferred to wipe out all his enemies, after a bit of consideration, he had to admit that getting out of here was more important. After all, his original plan had been to figure out the best way to get back to the Fifth Star Ring.

There was another reason. In this world, though the True God of these True Radiants was in the middle of assimilating, hē was occasionally lucid. Whenever that happened, it was very unfavorable for Xu Qing, and put him in a lot of danger. In fact, during his earlier attacks, he had attempted to use spatial manipulation magic to carry out his own teleportation. Unfortunately, he had been stymied.

The only way to leave was for this dwarf to open the way. Unfortunately, given the dwarf’s relationship to the True God, Xu Qing wasn’t confident that he could make his escape even if he managed to capture and puppetize the dwarf.

Getting his opponent to back away from the fight seemed like the perfect way to achieve his aim. Therefore, he made sure his words didn’t just target the dwarf, but also... the black tumor in the dome of heaven! Xu Qing had learned long ago that living beings were all different. Some were wise, some were foolish. And everyone had their own perspective and view of things.

Up above, the black tumor wriggled briefly, and then, a vortex appeared alongside it. The vortex pulsed with the spatial aura of the outside....

It was the exit!

As it turned out, the one being that was most interested in preventing a chaotic battle was actually the True Radiant’s True God! Although Xu Qing could be valuable to hīm, the people hē had brought here weren’t even close to being finished with thēir work. So in the end, it made sense to let Xu Qing leave. That would remove many variables, and let hīm focus on the work at hand.

“Ancestral God!” the dwarf blurted anxiously. Hē, of course, did not want Xu Qing to leave, because to hīm, Xu Qing... was too valuable!

Xu Qing’s eyes flitted back and forth. He had suspicions about whether or not this exit was legitimate. However, given the circumstances, he finally decided to grit his teeth and shoot toward it. But then... even as Xu Qing’s incredible speed brought him right toward the exit vortex, something dramatic happened!

The mountains rumbled, and the trees swayed as the local god unleashed an eruption of godly might. The result was that a huge tempest covered the entire exit. Then the exit crumbled out of existence.

As shock waves rolled out, Xu Qing fell back, his expression grim. At the same time, the fluctuations turned into a voice spoken via divine will.

“Young cultivator friend, that exit is a trick! Hē was trying to harm you! If you help me crush this enemy god, then I’ll help you escape!”

No one wanted Xu Qing to leave more than the True Radiants’ True God.

But as for who wanted Xu Qing to stay... the one who desired that the most wasn’t the dwarf. Rather... it was the god below that the True Radiants’ True God had been fighting for years, and was on the verge of being devoured. The chaotic situation at hand was the perfect opportunity for hīm. With Xu Qing here, it was now possible that hē could turn defeat into victory! That was why hē had stopped Xu Qing and also gone all out against the True Radiants’ True God.

The entire world devolved into chaos. The blood rain fell harder. The rumbling grew more intense.

And then a raspy voice spoke from within the blood rain. “Look, hē’s trying to prevent you from leaving. Help me crush hīm and I’ll open the exit for you again!”

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. The world trembled as more divine will converged.

“Hē’s lying to you. If you step into that exit, you’re dead beyond the shadow of a doubt. Hē has the upper hand in this fight right now, so there’s no way hē wants anyone on the outside to realize what’s going on. After all, you’re only one minor variable. But if people find out about this situation... there could be a lot more variables!”

I hereby swear an oath on my true name, ensuring that I can’t go back on my word. If you don’t believe me, then just ask hīm if hē’ll swear on hīs true name!”

Both of those things were uttered simultaneously by the two gods. And the god below didn’t swear on his true name!

Eyes flashing, the dwarf looked at Xu Qing and urgently said, “Fellow Daoist, I was being rash earlier. There’s no need for us to fight to the death. If you help us, we will abide by the promise of our True God!”

With that, hē looked up into the dome of heaven, bowed, and said, “Ancestral God, please release the Altar Gods. Give me the power to help this immortal cultivator to crush the enemy god. In doing so... we can prevent anything unexpected from happening!”

There was a hidden meaning to hīs words. If the Altar Gods joined the action, then their side would have the upper hand in both offense and defense, and would be in an almost invincible position.

The black tumor up above twitched, and then the handful of Altar Gods connected to it opened thēir eyes. Thēir divine will was returned to thēm as the connection to the black tumor was severed. And then thēy shot downward. It seemed like they really were going to help Xu Qing to crush the True God below.

Most of the Altar Gods weren’t particularly noteworthy. But there were three that had attracted Xu Qing’s attention earlier.

One of them was an evil eye with the pupil of a bronze bell covered in rust. Another looked like an emaciated old woman. And the third was a tree, half of which was covered in blooming crabapples, while the other half was charred and withered.

Xu Qing looked at them with glittering eyes. He had the weapon of an Immortal Lord, but to use it required tapping into the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring. Given that he was in the Fourth Star Ring, doing that... would definitely blow his cover. It was time to make a decision, so that’s what he did....

“Fine, all of you, come with me!”

Xu Qing shot down toward the mushroom umbrellas growing on the withered trees! freewebnovel.com

The mushroom umbrellas, big and small, were covered in crystals. And inside of those crystals was the same thing: an empty minor world. However, the reality was that, though it seemed to fully exist, it was actually in a state between illusion and reality. Normally speaking, there was no way to enter it!

But Xu Qing shot directly toward the minor world and went right inside! This had nothing to do with his canon. Apparently... the minor worlds had opened up on their own!

Xu Qing’s face remained as expressionless as ever.

“This minor world is the core of the enemy god. Normally speaking, we can’t get inside of it. But now it’s open.... All of you follow me in and wipe out everything! If an opportunity presents itself to capture that cultivator alive, do it. Otherwise... kill him!”

“You can see that I’m telling the truth. So you’re getting anxious!” The ground trembled. Hīs entire goal was to get hīs opponent anxious. That was when the flaws would be exposed.

In the minor world, the sky looked wrinkled, and the lands looked withered. There was no life. There were only ruins that attested to past glory.

Lightning crashed through the sky, and within it was Xu Qing. As soon as he appeared, a wind kicked up.

As it touched him, an image appeared to him. The image depicted the map of a world that had been shattered into millions upon millions of pieces and then put back together into what looked like a complete god kingdom.

The spot where Xu Qing was currently located was identified as just one small part of it! And there was something indescribable calling out to him, coming from a location among all those millions upon millions of pieces that actually wasn’t too far from him!

The moment he sensed it, his gaze hardened. Hidden within him was the Sageheaven Pagoda, which was his ticket to getting back to the Ninth Star Ring. And it was vibrating. The reason for that reaction wasn’t because of the Sageheaven Pagoda itself. Nor was it the sageheaven god vine that was wrapped around it, sleeping....

It was something that Xu Qing had placed into the pagoda after coming to the Fifth Star Ring, because it had been exhausted so thoroughly it needed to sleep. It was the little golden rat! Because of that call, the rat was waking up!

As soon as it started waking, grumbling sounds echoed in Xu Qing’s mind. Xu Qing’s pupils constricted, and then his eyes lit up. A seemingly preposterous idea then occurred to him. Struggling to control his breathing, he came to a decision. Then he shot forward toward the source of the call!

Unfortunately, as soon as he started moving, numerous gods descended. Every single one caused the call to weaken, until there were so many gods that the call disappeared altogether. The god kingdom that had been shattered into millions upon millions of pieces was thrown into complete chaos.

As a result, Xu Qing couldn’t accurately find what he was looking for! His eyes flashed. Obviously... the god below wanted him to kill all of the gods that had come to help the True Radiants’ True God.

This god wanted to make a deal with him.

Coldness filled Xu Qing’s heart. But in the end, he said, “Deal!”

Those gods looked like an eye, an old woman, and a half-blooming half-withering tree! Thēir godly authority surged around thēm.

One was some star ring hemp. The other was the chronoflitter aura of the golden rats. Without those two things, the portal couldn’t be used.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. Years ago at the outer sea of the Revered Ancient mainland, I ran into the Immortal Paragon as he was chasing down a golden rat.... That was when he told me to go to the Fifth Star Ring.
