The True Radiants’ True God wants to devour and assimilate me, and is about to succeed. But I have a secret magic that you could use to devour that True God. It would boost your ringsource, and would let me turn defeat into victory!”

Xu Qing stopped and looked up into the canopy of heaven. Looking very calm, he said, “Considering you let me in here, you obviously knew all along that karma would play out this way in your god kingdom. In that case, is this deal of yours your idea? Or is it... someone else’s idea? I’m very interested to know whether you are... a god or an immortal!”

***

Very far away from the Fourth Star Ring was the distant Ninth Star Ring. The vast expanse of the starry sky there, right in the middle, was the Revered Ancient mainland! The pressure of that ancient immortal in the starry sky grew stronger constantly, leaving all living beings feeling very anxious.

Beneath the surface of Revered Ancient was a vast subterranean location that was tightly sealed by ancient immortals. It was where the Brilliant Heaven Godfolk were. In that remote location was a dilapidated temple.

There was no statue of a god in the temple, but in one corner, a head lay there facing upward, unleashing a torrent of curses.

“All I did was steal the corpse of a peak Altar God! Because of that you fools chased me all this time? You people just wait!”

The head ground its teeth. Then, a very wild-looking old rat appeared. It had almost no fur left, as it burrowed out of nowhere next to the head. There, it made a few lazy squeaking sounds.

The head rolled into a different position so that it could look right at the rat. The head looked surprised. “Say what now? You sense a teleportation occurring very far away?”

Xu Qing stood in the teleportation portal made of star ring hemp. He had all of the requirements, including the star ring hemp from the Immortal Paragon, and the aura of the little golden rat.

With a mere thought, he could begin the teleportation. But instead, he continued to look up into the canopy of heaven. He was waiting for an answer to the question he had just asked.

A moment later, an ancient voice echoed out into the minor world, tinged with a faint bit of confusion.

“I don’t know either.... Years ago, I perished. When I returned, my recollections of the past were that of a god, but at the same time, I had scattered memories of a cultivator.

“Those two types of memories intersect, and thus, I often feel confused. Within that confusion is a voice that occasionally echoes out when the two types of memories clash. The voice tells me that there are clues left behind in my memories, and that one day, he’ll be able to use those clues to do something. Therefore, he says not to obsess over what I am. I should just walk the path in front of me until, one day, I will meet a cultivator who has a resonance with my memories.

“When you entered that pocket realm out there, I sensed the resonance with the clues. I understood... that you are the person I’ve been waiting for. As for the question you asked, I really have no way to answer it. Maybe I’m a god. Or maybe... I’m a cultivator.

“Furthermore, I have no way to prove what I’m saying is true. Whether you trust me or not... well, that’s up to you. I’m not hiding anything from you. If I impart to you the secret magic that can absorb the True Radiants’ True God, it will cause a stir in the pocket realm, and that will bring the risk that forces on the outside realize what’s happening. But the secret magic is real. Its absorption powers are real.”

Xu Qing looked down at the teleportation portal for a short time. “Transfer the secret magic to me.”

Up above, numerous bolts of lightning appeared, which converged into a jade slip that descended to Xu Qing.

He scanned it, whereupon a secret magic called the Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation poured into his mind. Xu Qing’s eyes immediately narrowed. The first part of the name was definitely a shock to him.

The voice of the True God then echoed out again. “This secret magic comes from the cultivator memories within me. Only someone with immortal energy can use it.”

“Do the memories contain the cultivator’s name?” Xu Qing asked.

“....” A long moment passed before the True God replied, “Unfortunately, no.”

Within Xu Qing’s mind, the Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation formed a dense network of magical symbols. After studying them with divine will, his eyes glittered with silver light. The air behind him vibrated as a towering immortal embryo materialized. Then the magical symbols of the Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation became silver and spread over the surface of the immortal embryo, converging on its right hand.

The immortal embryo lifted that hand and shoved it upward to the sky! The sky shattered as the huge hand punched a hole right through it.

Instantly, the pocket realm was revealed, complete with its raging war between heaven and earth. The mountains erupted. The trees shot toward the sky. Blood rain fell in torrents. The huge black tumor twitched violently. What was more, all of the magical mushrooms began to shine with silver light. The light spread out to fill the entire pocket realm as a majestic silver hand formed. freewebnovel.com

It was none other than the hand of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo! And it sped directly toward the black tumor! The silver magical symbols rushed out of the hand, becoming a silver river. And because the black tumor was so involved in the intense fight with the True God below, īt was quickly covered over.

The silver river... ravenously devoured the tumor! In the blink of an eye, a terrifying torrent of ringsource poured through the silver symbols and into the immortal embryo. An instant later, Xu Qing was assimilating all of the ringsource!

And thus, that ringsource was converted into immortal energy that nourished his immortal embryo! His cultivation base began to rise, reaching the very border of late Quasi-Immortal....

The black tumor began to writhe violently, sending out the mighty pressure of a True God, along with an astounding godly voice.

“How impudent!” The voice shook the pocket realm with such intensity, that rifts opened up everywhere. At the same time, a slit appeared on the black tumor, which opened to reveal a golden eye!

Īt had no emotions. A cultivator or a postheaven god in this situation would be enraged, but right now, īt was simply apathetic. However, a lack of emotions didn’t equate to irrationality. Īt knew that if, during the process of absorbing the True God below, Xu Qing plundered īts own foundation, then īts future would be in jeopardy, and īt could very well die.

Normally speaking, a Quasi-Immortal cultivator couldn’t possibly steal from īt. The real reason... other than the secret magic being used, was that... īts enemy was behind it. The True God below struggled and fought back, and was going all out at the last minute.

As Xu Qing assimilated the ringsource, the mountain ranges became like a blade made of a spine, which slashed up and stabbed into the canopy of heaven with an ear-shattering boom. The trees burned themselves to bolster Xu Qing’s silver hand. Their golden light suppressed the godly might of the enemy god, making Xu Qing’s work easier.

At that moment of crisis, the tumor twitched, causing īts outer layer of skin to crumble and burn, as it was converting into a terrifying power. That power then sought to drive away Xu Qing and his power of absorption!

Though the True God below was able to block much of that power, it was still so terrifying that as soon as it hit the hand of Xu Qing’s immortal embryo, the hand shattered. The ringsource of a True God sprayed everywhere.

Within the minor world, Xu Qing’s entire majestic immortal embryo also suffered the effects, and exploded. Within the spell formation, Xu Qing coughed up a mouthful of silver blood, within which was some of the ringsource he had not fully absorbed. At the same time, he suffered a backlash thanks to the sudden interruption to his cultivation base breakthrough.

Of course, Xu Qing was a vicious individual. His eyes flashed, and before the blood could even land on the ground, it turned into a blood mist that he quickly inhaled. Blue veins bulged out all over him as the power of the immortal embryo once again surged. The immortal embryo appeared again and then forcefully thrust its hand up again!

The silver hand appeared again outside. Silver magical symbols flowed as it once more began to drain the black tumor!

This time, the absorption played out differently. The extent and the strength far surpassed the previous attempt. And that was because, this time, Xu Qing... didn’t assimilate it!

Normally speaking, the process would be to absorb and assimilate it at the same time, turning it into nourishing immortal energy. The entire process could be considered a complete cycle. But after what just happened, Xu Qing knew that expending the effort to assimilate the ringsource would take time away from absorbing it.

Eyes flashing with cold light, he decided to forgo the assimilation, and instead use himself as a vessel to simply contain the ringsource.

There would be some downsides. For one, there was a limit to how much Xu Qing could contain. After all, this was a peak True God. And if the True God could be considered an ocean, then Xu Qing was like a lake. The second downside was that a lot of the ringsource would be wasted, and what he took into himself wouldn’t be very pure.

But Xu Qing couldn’t worry about those things right now. He had an opportunity to enjoy a big meal right now, and he would swallow however much he could. And after he finished with the meal, he would try to take some to-go as well!

And thus, he viciously absorbed the ringsource! He quickly reached capacity, and yet continued working. What he could fit inside, he fit inside. And what he couldn’t fit inside, he kept outside!

Up in the sky, a whole section of the black tumor already looked shriveled up. Though it was small compared to the tumor as a whole, it was obvious that īt couldn’t fight back much thanks to being locked in combat with the True God below. What was more, that missing section further weakened īt, so that the attacks of the True God below were even more effective. After all, the two True Gods were fairly evenly matched to begin with.

The biggest factor in the black tumor’s loss of momentum was the fact that Xu Qing couldn’t contain all the ringsource, and was letting much of it drain. It was like a deflating balloon!

As a result, the black tumor was in incredible danger. At that critical moment, the tumor shivered, then ignited part of ītself, causing a loud cracking sound to ring out. Īt was trying to rip open the spatial barriers of the pocket realm to allow the energy inside to spread on the outside. Not only would that create an exit, but also, it would alert forces on the outside of what was happening.

Īt didn’t want to resort to this action unless there was absolutely no other option available. After all, it would introduce a host of other variables. But given what was going on, there didn’t seem to be any other option. Those variables were the key to resolving the crisis.

However... just as īt was preparing to rip open the pocket realm.... The silver magical symbols in the area collapsed on their own. The silver hand also vanished, as well as the immortal embryo in the minor world.

Xu Qing had taken the initiative to stop absorbing the ringsource. Without any hesitation, he activated the teleportation portal and vanished!

He left!

He had worked out a deal with the True God below, but given his personality, he wasn’t going to simply trust the other party completely.

From the earliest moment, he had not intended to actually help that True God. He only had one goal. And that was... to take the unbalanced situation and return it to a state of balance! That way, neither party would be able to target him.

“He left?” The black tumor abandoned the plan to rip open the pocket realm.

And then the True God below erupted with full force. Heaven and earth once again went back to fighting. Everything shook inside the pocket realm as the teleportation portal made of star ring hemp slowly dissipated.

But then, in the moment before it was completely and utterly gone....

A finger-sized blue worm with the face of a person burrowed out of the teleportation light. Once it was in the open, the star ring hemp completely faded into nothing, leaving behind no trace of its existence.

The blue worm looked around the area, stunned. “What freaking place is this?”

The human face on the worm looked confused.... If Xu Qing were present, he would definitely be both shocked and delighted. The worm was Erniu! Although Erniu was initially flabbergasted, it only took a moment for his nose to twitch. Then he turned to look in a specific direction, his eyes shining brightly.

That’s the aura of Altar God flesh! Holy crap! What is this place...?

Erniu excitedly blurred into motion. Burrowing out of the minor world, he quickly arrived... at the spot where Xu Qing had contended with those gods. He looked around at all the god corpses, which included quite a few Altar Gods. There was even a peak Altar God....

Erniu was shivering in elation, and he felt the impulse to rush forward.

Has luck finally smiled on me? The moment I show up, I’m presented with so much stuff to eat? Back in that damned Brilliant Heaven place, I got chased down just for stealing one Altar God. But here... thēy’re everywhere! And nobody else is around! I hit the motherlode!

Erniu raced forward. However, he still felt there was something suspicious going on, so he kept his guard up.

These gods haven’t been dead long. I wonder who killed thēm? Whoever did it has a really ruthless way of doing things!

Dark green starlight flowed through a rift in space-time, becoming like moonlight glimmering on an endless black glacier. As the light went on, it spread out over the entire glacier until it was like the canopy of heaven over a world. Beneath that canopy was a temple that had existed for countless years, which was emanating a faint, mysterious light. Other than that, everything was dark.

It was impossible to see anything within the gloom. However, it was possible to hear hair-raising cries. There were also sounds like chewing and the snapping of bones, as well as disgusting swallowing sounds that would cause one’s hair to stand on end.

As for the mysterious light, it was only around the temple, which was illuminated hazily. From a distance, it looked like a candle burning in the night.

The temple was deep underneath the frozen glacier. Innumerable years had passed in which no one disturbed it. Deep within the temple were twelve badly damaged statues of gods. Thēy were circled around a red altar, atop which... was a bronze door, standing upright.

The bronze door opened silently, and a figure slowly emerged from the darkness beyond. He wore a black robe, had violet hair, was tall and slender, and had a mesmerizing face. As he looked around with a vigilant expression, his entire person pulsed with a terrifying aura. He was... Xu Qing, who had just experienced a teleportation via the star ring hemp!

Where am I...?

He immediately sent his divine will out to scan the area. He was ready for anything. Unfortunately, he had no idea where he was. All his divine will revealed to him was that this place was extremely ancient and full of intense pressure! His cultivation base, his divine will, and everything else about him was under immense pressure. He couldn’t even fly.

Xu Qing’s brow furrowed. Thankfully, though his divine will was severely limited, he could sense the twelve damaged statues surrounding the altar. Thēy were gruish in appearance, yet were also indescribably holy. Thēy were covered in deep slash marks, like growth rings left behind by the claws of some terrifying entity.

Considering how large thēy were, and how large everything else was in this place, Xu Qing felt like he had come to a kingdom of giants. He seemed insignificant.

Is this a temple?

His eyes narrowed as he studied his surroundings more closely. However, he didn’t identify anything unusual. Eventually, he stepped onto the altar. When his shoes touched the blood-red tiles, a red liquid oozed out from beneath his feet. It floated about gruishly, as if it were blood that was waking up.

Xu Qing’s eyes flashed, but he kept walking. He wanted to get out of this temple and have a look around to determine where he was.

Soon, the temple filled with a sound like footsteps on a watery surface. It sounded empty and bizarre. And then, the footsteps suddenly stopped.

Xu Qing stood in a crumbling corridor that led toward the outside. He looked up.

Perhaps it was his arrival, or perhaps it was the breeze that came with him. But either way, the dust on the wall shifted. It almost was as if time was passing as the dust revealed the red surface of the wall, and the ancient symbols on it. The designs depicted a god whose skin had been flayed off, reclining on the horizon, hīs bones having turned into mountains, and hīs blood flowing toward a bronze planet. Surrounding the god were hosts of greedy blue eyes.

After a while, Xu Qing looked away. The sense of unfamiliarity and suspicion regarding this place were getting stronger.

Just where exactly am I?

He turned and looked in the direction of the end of the corridor. Before long, the footsteps echoed out again within the silent temple. The sound went on for the time it takes an incense stick to burn....

Outside, it was dark, with only that mysterious light creating hazy illumination around the temple. Eventually, the main door opened.

Rumbling sounds echoed out into the dark surrounding world. The chewing sounds stopped. And then... pairs of blue eyes suddenly appeared out in the darkness, all of them looking toward the temple.

At the same time, mysterious light erupted from the temple, like the last flash of light before sunset, or the passage of a bolt of lightning. As a result, Xu Qing could see everything clearly as he stepped outside!

There were corpses everywhere! There were never-ending god corpses! Thēy included all types of Godfolk. Thēy came from a host of different time periods! The vast majority were little more than skeletons with some scrap of flesh on thēm. Thēy were piled up everywhere, as far as the eye could see.

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted at the sight of it. He had never seen the corpses of so many gods in one place, not even on the battlefield.

What struck him most deeply was that among the innumerable god corpses were... a host of living creatures. Thēy were everywhere, and thēy were extremely gruish![1]

Each one had a gray, skeletal body with a rib cage of twelve rib bones in total, divided asymmetrically on the left and right side of the body. The ribs on the left had a sticky violet membrane stretching between each bone, which would inflate when it breathed in. When the membrane stretched thin, it was possible to see the flesh of gods inside being digested.

On the right, the rib bones were crystallized, and would occasionally reveal the protruding faces of agonized gods. Those faces created an endless, tormented flow toward the tumorized head, a cycle that would repeat every few breaths.

Although each creature had different facial features, they all had blue eyes. As for the limbs, they were extremely skinny and covered with bone spurs, while the spine on the back seemed to be growing upside down. Bone spurs protruded from the skin at the neck, and they glowed with blue light. Astonishingly, at the end of each spur was a shriveled finger. As Xu Qing watched, the fingers would writhe and sway along with the movement of the spurs.

Xu Qing looked at all of this with glittering eyes. He felt a sense of danger, but at the same time, there was something familiar about all this.

I feel like I’ve seen these gruish things before....

Before Xu Qing could think much about it, the strange creatures suddenly let loose shrill cries. A piercing sound wave swept out in all directions, along with a surge of greed. It turned into a wind.

And then countless gruish creatures began to rush in Xu Qing’s direction. A sense of deadly crisis erupted within him.

Xu Qing didn’t hesitate for a moment. His immortal embryo glittered as it materialized behind him and then rushed forth to meet the incoming gruish creatures. Wherever it passed, the gruish creatures shivered and then howled as their bodies exploded. However, they would form anew only moments later. They seemed to be eternally indestructible.

There were some who looked mostly like the others, except that they had blue patches of ice on them, and they were far more deadly than the others. Seeing that, Xu Qing waved his hand, and his iron skewer flew out and joined the effort.

His canon of parallelism appeared, causing different versions of himself to emerge from overlapping space-time. Like his true form, they unleashed explosive immortal might, becoming shooting stars that shot in various directions.

The sound of slaughter drifted out across the glacier. freewebnovel.com

About an hour later, as the dark green moonlight shone out over the glacier, a loud cracking sound rang out, and the glacier began to split apart in one area.

Xu Qing shot out from within. Blood oozed out of the corners of his mouth, and he looked to be in bad shape. Behind him were a host of space-time reflections that were slowly fading away. He could now sense that he was able to fly, and so he shot up into the air and pushed down behind him with his hand.

The sheets of ice trembled, then collapsed, closing the opening. On the other side were a host of those gruish beasts. Leading thēm was a tall figure whose body was twenty percent blue. Hē had one arm that was almost entirely covered with blue, as if it was completely made of ice! Hē looked at Xu Qing with greed, but did not try to give chase.

Xu Qing looked down at that tall being, a scowl on his face.

The gruish beings in the glacier had ordinary battle prowess. It was their eternally indestructible characteristics and endless numbers, coupled with the fact that he couldn’t fly, which had made things so difficult. But even with all that, he normally wouldn’t have ended up in such bad shape.

What got him really broken-down were the creatures with the blue ice patches. The more ice they had, the more deadly they were. And that was especially true of the one with the ice hand covered with bone spurs.

That being filled Xu Qing with an intense sensation of danger! Only by relying on his space-time clones had he been able to fight his way through and eventually get out of the glacier.

Seeing that they weren’t chasing him, he breathed a sigh of relief. But at the same time, he still felt like all of this was familiar, especially that huge figure looking at him from the other side of the opening.

I’ve seen something like it before.... Eldest Brother!

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted as he realized where that sensation of familiarity came from! That blue hand of ice with the bone spurs was very similar to the one which would come out of Erniu’s chest when he went all out.[2]

Godfiend?

Xu Qing’s heart pounded as the opening leading into the glacier closed, becoming nothing but a crater. The sight of the tall, blue figure was cut off.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed as many thoughts ran through his head. Then he sent his divine will around him to check his surroundings. Astonishingly, he was on top of a massive black glacier that pulsed with intense mutagen. Within that mutagen was endless death.

Before he could thoroughly inspect his surroundings, a strange sensation of fear rose up within him. He looked off into the distance. The clouds in the sky rippled as a golden meteor shot forth, heading in his direction.

Is that...? He looked closely at the meteor. Soon, he could make out clearly what it was! It was not a meteor. It was... the massive corpse of a god! Though the god was dead, the aura indicated it was a True God! This....

His eyes narrowed as a voice spoke into his mind via divine will. It was a voice full of astonishment and disbelief! It was the voice of the goddess Starryeyes!

“This is the primeval motherworld!” [3]

***

Outside of the glacier world was the space-time rift. And in the vast expanse of this universe’s starry sky, the corpse of a god floated along. Responding to the direction given, the corpse flew into the rift.

Two people were seated inside the corpse. They were none other than Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix!

Opening her eyes, Spirit Phoenix quietly said, “The primeval motherworld of the Fourth Star Ring. We’re almost there. Husband... have you come to a decision?”

Next to her, Young Lord Aurora slowly opened his eyes. “The Immortal Paragon came up with this plan. Call it my predestined fate....”

1. The author goes back and forth between using the divine pronoun for these creatures and the non-gender-specific “it” pronoun usually used for animals or inanimate objects. This feels intentional to me, as if the author intends for these creatures to seem “similar” to gods, but not an actual Godfolk species. Therefore, I will do the same. Occasionally they will have the divine pronoun applied, but not always. ☜

2. The blue hand has come up quite a few times in the past, for instance in chapters 573.2 and 1022. There are other instances, those are just the first two I pulled up. ☜

3. The characters, and later context, imply that this motherworld is a planet. That said, description makes it unclear if it’s a ‘spherical’ planet or a ‘flat earth’ type of thing. ☜

When Xu Qing heard the voice of Goddess Starryeyes, he scowled, lifted his right hand, and made a grasping gesture. In that manner, he dragged Starryeyes out by the neck and placed hēr on the black glacier in front of him. Then he loosened his grip so shē could speak.

“Tell me everything you know,” he said. “Very accurately.”

His cold gaze coupled with everything shē had experienced after being captured, plus what shē had gone through with Starfire, ensured that Starryeyes’ defenses had all crumbled. Shē knew that hiding things wouldn’t benefit hēr at all.

After a moment of thought, shē said, “Everything here matches the description of a very secret location. It’s... the Fourth Star Ring’s primeval motherworld.” freewebnovel.com

“Continue,” Xu Qing said tranquilly.

“Supposedly,” shē continued, “the primeval motherworld is the place where the very first god was born in the Fourth Star Ring. Legend has it that before that primeval god, the Fourth Star Ring didn’t have gods at all. It was only because of hīm that gods came to be here.”

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered.

His gaze caused Starryeyes to shiver. After a brief moment of hesitation, shē continued, “It’s a very old story. I heard about it from my father. And not all the gods in the Fourth Star Ring accept it as truth. I guess you can say that the story of the primeval motherworld is just one of the stories that explain the origin of the gods.”

“Tell me some things you know to be true,” Xu Qing said coldly.

Starryeyes nodded. “There’s one thing that’s certain. When gods develop the godrot, and thēir bodies wither, thēy’ll sense a call from the motherworld. At that point, thēy will float through the starry sky, following a prescribed trajectory until thēy arrive here and land on the motherworld. That journey cannot be detected or perceived, so even after countless years have passed, very few gods know the actual location of the motherworld. Only the dead come here.”

“Godrot?” Xu Qing asked.

Starryeyes seemed hesitant to explain what were obviously secrets of the gods, but in the end, shē didn’t hold back. “Gods under the level of True God are not undying. It’s only after becoming a True God that one acquires a true name and becomes undying. However, that undying aspect refers only to the true name, not the god’s body. The bodies of all gods, True Gods or not, will eventually develop godrot after enough time passes.

“It ends in complete withering.... When thēy sense the call of the motherworld, thēy come here and die. Those gods that don’t have a true name become nutrients. As for those who do have true names, well, the motherworld is like a womb where they can develop a new god body.

“Then, by combining that new body with the true name, thēy can be resurrected. It’s a slow process, but it’s just one of the ways the natural laws governing the return of True Gods works.”

Hearing this, Xu Qing frowned. “That doesn’t conform to my previous understanding of this subject!”

Starryeyes quickly explained, “It’s because there are two additional ways for gods to be resurrected. The first way is for a god to return to the body thēy died in. The other is to be summoned by a God Lord. But those two methods only work on gods who have not developed godrot. For example, maybe thēy died in battle.... For the godrotten, the only option is to answer the call of the motherworld.”

Xu Qing looked thoughtful. This was the first time he had heard any information like this. But thinking back to instances in which he watched True Gods reviving, he realized that all of them had been killed in battle. That said, he still wasn’t sure how trustworthy this information was, so he checked with Starfire.

Unfortunately, Starfire was a postheaven god, and was not yet a True God. In contrast, Starryeyes was nobility. In the end, there was no way for Starfire to answer the question.

After some thought, Xu Qing pointed down at the black glacier with his left hand. “What are those gruish things underneath the glacier?”

“They’re sourcefiends...” Starryeyes replied immediately. “Sourcefiends are beings unique to the motherworld. They devour the corpses of gods, as they’re a part of the motherworld itself. They are born here and die here. And ultimately, they become elements in the new god bodies that form.”

Eyes narrowing, Xu Qing thought for a moment, then asked, “Can the sourcefiends leave the motherworld?”

Starryeyes shook hēr head to indicate the answer was no. “At least, I’ve never heard of that happening. Based on my understanding of the motherworld, there has never been a sourcefiend seen anywhere but here.”

“Is the Fourth Star Ring the only place that has a motherworld?” he asked. “Or do all the other thirty-six higher star rings have them?”

“They all do,” Starryeyes said quietly. Shē wasn’t holding anything back. These matters were secrets that few under the True God level knew about. In contrast, upon reaching the True God level, the information would become apparent to that god, as it was contained in thēir blood. Given that Starryeyes’ father was a god emperor, it made sense that shē would know all the details.

“How do we leave here?” Xu Qing asked, looking at hēr coldly.

Shē shivered and shook hēr head. “I don’t know.... I just know that living beings shouldn’t be able to come here....”

There was one thing shē didn’t ask, and that was why Xu Qing would come to a place like this.

Xu Qing frowned and was about to ask another followup question. But then something shocking happened.

Starryeyes, perhaps because of just spending time in this place, was starting to wither and rot.

At the same time, Starfire spoke into Xu Qing’s mind, sounding alarmed. “Young Lord, my body is weakening, and my godsource is fading away!!”

Apparently, Starryeyes had also sensed the change in hēr, as shē started trembling in terror. “This is the primeval motherworld! It can break down and absorb all living things!”

Xu Qing checked himself, but didn’t notice anything unusual. Looking at the terrified Starryeyes, he said, “Are you sure there’s no way to leave?”

Shē trembled as shē searched hēr memories. Unfortunately, shē really didn’t know any way to leave.

Xu Qing waved his hand to put the goddess away. Then he scanned the area, all while simultaneously checking his ringsource and analyzing the information he had learned.

The primeval motherworld. It’s supposedly the place where gods were first born in the Fourth Star Ring. Gods who develop godrot all come back here....

Living beings can’t come here.... Then why would the Immortal Paragon arrange for me to be teleported here? Also... the so-called sourcefiends look very similar to whatever Erniu has inside of him. If Erniu really does have a sourcefiend in him....

Xu Qing had long speculated about Erniu’s secrets. But even to this point he didn’t have much concrete information to work with. However, now wasn’t the time to ponder that. Xu Qing looked up into the dome of heaven.

Regardless of why the Immortal Paragon sent me here, the most important thing to do right now is figure out a way to leave. I tried the bronze door in the temple, but I couldn’t use it to leave. In that case, I guess I need to check the canopy of heaven. Maybe that’s where I’ll find a way out.

With that thought in mind, he flew up into the sky. Moving with astonishing speed, he went higher and higher.

Time passed.

Unfortunately, heaven here was massive, and no matter how Xu Qing climbed, he never got more than halfway up. It was like there was no end. At a certain point, he stopped, hovered there, and looked down. The black glacier was still beneath him, and it seemed to stretch forever. When Xu Qing saw that happening, his heart sank.

Given the speed I’m capable of, I should have been able to fly through an entire universe at this point. But I’m still only halfway up!

Xu Qing could sense that Starfire and Starryeyes were both getting weaker and weaker. He didn’t care much about Starryeyes. But he did care about Starfire, so he sent hēr some of his own ringsource to help.

It doesn’t matter how high I get. As long as I’m in this location, thēy will keep getting weaker.

After some consideration, he kept moving at top speed. Not much time passed before he stopped, his pupils constricting.

A hair-raising sensation had struck him, like a mountain-toppling, sea-draining force assailing him. At the same time, a cold, prickling sensation filled him. It was as if every scrap of his flesh and blood, as well as all aspects of his divine will, were screaming that he was in danger. It was coming from the boundless sky above him. Apparently, if he kept going up, something unimaginably terrifying would happen.

I can’t keep going!

Reeling, he dropped down. After going back down to a certain elevation, the terrifying sensation vanished.

Unfortunately, he couldn’t actually relax, as a new danger suddenly manifested. After bolstering Starryeyes and Starfire, Xu Qing realized that his own ringsource was starting to disappear. That caused his expression to darken.

It wasn’t happening very quickly, and he still had plenty in the stockpile from the black tumor. But nothing he did to try to stop it from happening had any effect.

When Starfire realized what was happening, shē got extremely nervous. “Young Lord, it looks like it’s speeding up. If things keep going on like this....”

“I know,” he replied. With that, he blurred into motion, heading down toward the glacier so fast that a sonic boom echoed out in all directions.

He was moving in the direction of the True God corpse that he had seen falling earlier. It didn’t take very long before he reached the spot. There, embedded halfway into the ground, was the huge god corpse.

Despite being embedded in the ground, it hadn’t shattered the glacier. It was almost as if it had melted into it. Down beneath, there were hordes of sourcefiends already feeding on the corpse.

Without any hesitation, Xu Qing touched the corpse. Silver light flashed in his eyes. Gradually, a feeble stream of ringsource emerged from the corpse and poured in to replenish both himself and Starfire. He was yet again using the Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation!

“Oh, I see...” he said, his eyes glittering.

The Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation is a very tyrannical secret magic. It’s strong enough to assimilate the ringsource of a True God!

Xu Qing looked off into the distance, and the fog clouding his mind began to clear. He stopped using the secret magic and instead tried an ordinary collection technique on the corpse. The result was just as he had expected. It didn’t work at all.

So that’s how it is. If I want to collect from a True God, then I either have to rely on the power of the Aurora heaven beyond heaven to collect from the god imprisoned there, or I have to target lower-level gods like Starryeyes. Of those two, the first was half-returned, and thus not complete, while the other is seriously injured, and has dropped in cultivation level.

As for this god corpse, the ringsource is fading after death. The sourcefiends are devouring it, and the motherworld is absorbing it.... That’s why ordinary collection techniques don’t work at all. I can only use the domineering Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation to succeed.

With it, I can counteract the effects of this locale that drains ringsource. And that means I can actually stay here safely. Except, there’s no way the Immortal Paragon just wants me to come here, absorb god corpses, and improve my cultivation level!

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. From what he could tell, the Immortal Paragon was the type of person who crafted plans within plans within plans.

I’m probably just one part of the overall plan. Or maybe I’m just here to help! Perhaps my presence here is the mere foundation for something else....

In other words, I probably don’t need to sit around trying to figure out what the Immortal Paragon is planning. I should just wait and see. The truth about his plan will probably be revealed unexpectedly at some point. Unfortunately, I am not fond of arrangements like that!

Xu Qing didn’t like it when his fate was manipulated by others, even if it was the Immortal Paragon himself.

That said, when he assessed the situation honestly, he had to admit that after coming to the Fifth Star Ring from the Revered Ancient mainland, everything he had done had been his own choice. But at the same time, it seemed that the Immortal Paragon had been watching over him, ensuring that he never ran into too much trouble to handle. He had long come to sense that.

Sighing, he focused on absorbing the ringsource, keeping some for himself and giving some to Starfire. After taking enough to counteract the effects of his surroundings, he settled cross-legged to focus on building another stockpile.

A few days later, the god corpse had sunk all the way down into the glacier. As the sourcefiends looked on with their blue eyes, Xu Qing flew up and then sped along over the surface of the primeval motherworld.

The ringsource I’ve taken so far is enough to keep Starfire and I going for a number of days. Going forward, I need to explore this place a bit more. Naturally speaking, the ideal outcome would be to find an exit. As for the Immortal Paragon’s plan... I guess I’ll consider it as a debt owed. Until the plan is revealed, I’ll just focus on my cultivation.

With that decision made, he sent some ringsource to Starryeyes. After all... he didn’t want the goddess to die. That wouldn’t do any good. As far as Xu Qing was concerned, if shē was going to die, it needed to benefit him in some way.

And thus, half a month went by.

There was no division between day and night on the primeval motherworld. But there was occasional dark-green moonlight that allowed Xu Qing to track time according to the timekeeping standards of the Revered Ancient mainland.

During the time that passed, he saw a lot of god corpses fall from the sky. Most of them crumbled in the process of falling, turning into ashes. Some, those who were Altar Gods or higher, didn’t completely crumble, and landed on the glacier as mostly intact corpses that slowly sank down.

Seems Starryeyes wasn’t lying after all.... Gods under the True God level who develop the godrot come back here and become nutrients. Only True Gods land as intact corpses. Seems to me that ‘primeval motherworld’ isn’t the best description of this place. Calling it a ‘corpseworld’ would make more sense. It’s like hell itself.

Xu Qing looked up as a Godfire god crumbled into ashes. Beneath the glacier underfoot were countless sourcefiends staring at him. And amidst the hordes of sourcefiends was a temple that the moonlight barely reached.

Xu Qing looked down at the glacier, his eyes glittering coldly. During the half month that had passed, he hadn’t just explored the topside of the glacier. He had also gone down below, where he had found a total of three additional temples. All of them, without exception, were surrounded by endless corpses and innumerable sourcefiends.

Xu Qing had not held back any ringsource. He had unleashed all his battle prowess to fight his way through them. Inside each of the three temples, he had found a bronze door. Unfortunately, no matter what efforts he made, the bronze doors were as useless as the door in the temple he had arrived in.

Apparently, the doors in the temples lead the way into this location, but are not exits to the outside.

Xu Qing had also come to a conclusion about the sourcefiends. There’s a definite connection between the temples and the sourcefiends.

Unfortunately, he wasn’t sure of the specifics. Contemplating such things, he flew up into the air. He needed to find some more fallen god corpses to replenish the ringsource he had used and also bolster Starfire. He had grown used to this process over the last half month. Though he hadn’t found any True God corpses like the very first one he’d encountered, there were other corpses he could make use of, though most were in bad shape.

The ringsource those gods provided wasn’t as amazing as that of the True God, which had provided enough in one shot to keep him going for days. But after absorbing from multiple corpses, he would get what he needed to continue exploring.

Days passed. Xu Qing would replenish his ringsource, then widen his search of the primeval motherworld. Unfortunately, nothing atop the glacier changed. It was always black, and it always went on forever.

Other than the sourcefiends under the glacier and the god corpses falling from above, he didn’t see anything. He was the only living being in the world, flying along endlessly alone. He was slowly getting numb to it all. But then... on one particular day, he stopped in place and looked off into the distance, his eyes glittering.

“Is that...?”

Shockingly, a great distance away on the glacier, he had spotted a massive crevice! It was like a gigantic, ghastly canyon. This was the first unusual terrain feature he had encountered in this place!

His spirits lifted, and he raced along like a shooting star to appear right above the canyon! Looking down at it, he realized it resembled a wound. And it was so long and deep that his senses couldn’t penetrate it. But there was something even more shocking.... freewebnovel.com

The opposing walls of the valley, from top to bottom, were covered with innumerable bronze doors. Some of the doors were sealed with ice. Others were half-exposed. Yet others were completely out in the open.

If that were all there were to it, Xu Qing wouldn’t have been so taken aback. But what really caused his pupils to constrict was that there were sourcefiends seated cross-legged around all of the exposed doors. These sourcefiends were different from the ones he had seen. Thēy didn’t just have blue arms. Thēy were completely blue from head to toe, and thēy looked almost exactly like the one inside his Eldest Brother.

Wait, no. The one in Eldest Brother is a dark blue color. These ones... thēy’re light blue!

Xu Qing’s guard went up. Having fought many sourcefiends, he knew what thēy were like and how difficult thēy could be to deal with. But this was his first time seeing any that were pure blue. And there were a lot of thēm. It seemed that just as he caught sight of thēm, quite a few of thēm looked over at him with blue eyes.

Xu Qing didn’t make any sudden moves. Similarly, the sourcefiends didn’t move either. Thēy just looked at him. Xu Qing slowly backed up, and the sourcefiends looked away from him.

Thēy’re not coming out....

Given everything he had experienced so far in this place, Xu Qing was certain that the valley... would be an extremely dangerous location to enter.

But why are thēy all sitting there by those bronze doors?

He frowned, then settled cross-legged in midair to study the sourcefiends. A few days later, something happened in the valley that dispelled much of his confusion. One of the bronze doors at the very bottom of the valley slowly opened. Godly chanting drifted out from inside.

“Kan Shan... Kan Shan....”

The godly voice seemed to contain the power of the star ring, and it stirred the local mutagen, causing it to converge in the form of a god talisman. It floated out of the door! And it shot right toward the nearest sourcefiend!

The god talisman seemed infinitely ancient, and it contained unimaginable mysteries. But all it took was one glance at it for Xu Qing’s heart to start pounding. He immediately backed up. As for the sourcefiend, īts eyes became more intensely blue, and then īt let loose a raging howl. It was as if the god talisman was a tribulation īt had to face, and thus, īt howled maniacally as the talisman approached.

As Xu Qing watched, the talisman and the sourcefiend collided. Next, golden light shone from the god talisman, while the sourcefiend shone with a blue glow. It looked like the two were trying to devour each other.

But the convergence of the blue and gold was like boiling water meeting a snowflake. The blue glittered, but in the end, couldn’t fight back, and was wiped out by the golden light from the god talisman. And then... it was as if the god talisman sucked all the life out of the sourcefiend. In the middle of the god talisman, bones appeared, then meridians and veins, and then flesh....

It became a god body! It surged with endless life force! A new god had been born!

The aura of a True God surged from the god body. And before the body could awaken, the bronze door sucked the body in. It vanished completely.

Xu Qing watched the whole thing happen, his heart pounding the entire time.

This is how new gods are reconstructed in this place! The reconstruction process requires a carrier in the form of a sourcefiend of blue ice. What came floating out of the door... was a true name!! The true name is imprinted and transferred to a new god. And the sourcefiend can’t do anything about it. It’s like predestination!

Xu Qing’s heart was racing.

Does that mean that I came out of that bronze door in the same manner as a true name?

He wasn’t sure. But as he looked at the sourcefiends and the bronze doors, he couldn’t help but think of his Eldest Brother!

It seems more than ever that Eldest Brother... is very unique! Whenever he goes all out, a sourcefiend comes out of his chest. It almost seems like he and the sourcefiend are occupying one body! What’s more, Eldest Brother certainly does have undying characteristics!

***

A god fell from the sky off in the distance. The body had been on quite a journey. As the corpse fell to the ground, it didn’t break apart. It was the corpse of a True God!

When Xu Qing spotted it, he settled his thoughts. His eyes glittered. Assimilating damaged gods was very limiting. It was nothing like dealing with the corpse of a True God! Xu Qing blurred into motion toward the corpse.

***

Inside that very corpse, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix opened her eyes.

“Husband, we’ve arrived.”

Young Lord Aurora opened his eyes and looked around calmly. He was about to speak, when all of a sudden a strange expression overtook the calmness on his face. “Hmm?”

Xu Qing sped through the air over the black glacier. He looked like a hungry wolf!

During the time that passed, he had not found any way of leaving the primeval motherworld. And despite his contingency plans working so far, the constant drain on his ringsource was a source of great anxiety. After all, he had to worry about Starfire as well. And only a few days earlier... he had started to contemplate whether or not it would be worth it to give up on Starryeyes.

Draining those mangled corpses only brought in a meager amount of ringsource. And as time went on, the draining effect of the planet only increased. Over the past month, he had been searching for an exit while at the same time searching for intact corpses! freewebnovel.com

Unfortunately, the only intact corpses were those of True Gods, and such corpses didn’t fall very often. And when they did fall, they would sink down through the glacier in a matter of days. The result was that finding one was like fishing a needle from the sea.

It really came down to getting lucky. In fact, during the past month, Xu Qing had only encountered two. One was that very first one he had found, and the other was this one. That was why he felt such a sense of urgency.

Luck is on my side this time. This corpse fell pretty close to me, and I was able to rush over to it immediately. It should have a good amount of ringsource. With the Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation, I’ll be able to collect quite a bit from it.

Xu Qing’s mind was spinning with all the possibilities. An hour later... he caught sight of a massive corpse with green skin and black crystals growing all over it. Despite being dead, the corpse still sent immense pressure out in all directions, causing the air to ripple and distort.

Down beneath the glacier, hordes of sourcefiends were gathering in anticipation of the corpse sinking down.

Xu Qing stopped in midair and studied the area. After confirming that the corpse really was dead, he shot through the distortions to arrive atop the corpse. He landed on the chest. Given his experience harvesting the mangled god corpses, he knew that the chest was where the most ringsource would be gathered.

Without a moment of hesitation, he unleashed the Dark Serenity God-Assimilating Incantation and put his hand down onto the surface of the chest. Assimilation via direct contact was the most efficient! His eyes glittered as the process started. Streams of ringsource immediately began to come out of the chest and into him.

His eyes lit up.

It’s good I got here so quickly. The planet hasn’t taken much of the ringsource!

Xu Qing was in very high spirits as he rapidly assimilated as much ringsource as possible, not forgetting to send some to Starfire as well, who reacted with an exclamation of joy and satisfaction.

The sourcefiends below the glacier were getting visibly antsy. Although it wasn’t possible to hear their calls, it was clear that they were instinctively angry at having their food stolen. In fact, some of them launched up into the air and smashed into the underside of the glacier.

Xu Qing completely ignored them, and focused fully on the assimilation effort. As the process went on, the spot where he was touching the skin of the god went from green to white. And it started to sink down.

When that happened, Xu Qing knew it was time to switch to another spot. However, that was when something completely unexpected happened!

A hand shot out from the white, sunken portion of the chest. There was no way for Xu Qing to avoid it! And before he could do anything, it latched onto his wrist!

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted. He had studied the area and the corpse thoroughly before beginning, and had confirmed that the corpse was indeed dead. How could he not be caught surprised? His immortal embryo appeared behind him, and his cultivation base roared to life. Starfire, startled, held nothing back to help him.

But then... a gentle ringsource flowed out of the hand and into Xu Qing. The hand loosened its grip. Uncertain of what was going on, Xu Qing backed away. That was when a familiar voice drifted out.

“How long have you been this hungry?”

Xu Qing’s jaw nearly dropped as he looked at the sunken area of the god’s chest. Two familiar figures emerged. One was a man, the other was a woman. The woman was smiling. Her oval face shone with a pearly luster, and her eyes were slightly upturned with full under-eyes, making her seem unusually gentle and friendly. The man, meanwhile, wore a black robe with silver embroidery. He stood tall, but was relaxed, with an enigmatic smile on his face as he looked Xu Qing up and down.

Xu Qing stared at them in astonishment. It was an expression rarely seen on his face. He really could not imagine why these two people would appear as he was assimilating a corpse.

“You two....”

In reaction to his facial expression, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix cast an annoyed glance at Young Lord Aurora. “Why did you have to go and grab our young friend’s arm like that??”

Young Lord Aurora chuckled. “I guess I was just too excited to see an old buddy. I hope I didn’t startle you too much, Xu Qing.”

Xu Qing took a deep breath, and his eyes lit up with understanding. This must be why the Immortal Paragon had arranged for him to come here! He quickly clasped hands and bowed.

“Well met, Seniors!”

“Are you kidding me?” Young Lord Aurora said, his eyebrows shooting up. “You got the Aurora Immortal Palace, and the entire heaven beyond heaven. Yet you’re still addressing us as Seniors? Are we strangers or something?”

Young Lord Aurora’s eyes glittered much like they had when he was an imp back in the immortal palace. Spirit Phoenix laughed softly. After coming to the Fourth Star Ring, her husband had mostly acted very serious, and definitely not like this. She knew it was all because of Xu Qing.

Smiling, she said, “Oh, you! Why don’t you just come out and say it. You want lil’ bro Xu to call you big brother, don’t you?”

Young Lord Aurora smiled enigmatically.

Xu Qing blinked a few times and thought back to all the scenes that played out in the Aurora Immortal Palace. Given that, he had every reason to comply.

“Big Brother.”

Young Lord Aurora laughed heartily. He didn’t ask Xu Qing what he was doing here. Instead, he flicked his sleeve, causing the god corpse to collapse into a host of crystals that were packed with ringsource. He sent them flying over to Xu Qing.

“Let’s go,” he said. “Your big brother is going to bring you along to do something dramatic.”

With that, Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix flew up into the air, taking Xu Qing along with them. They headed... in the direction of the valley. Hearing their familiar voices, and seeing them in person, left Xu Qing feeling very moved. All of a sudden, he realized that this was a feeling he had experienced with someone else many times in the past.

I wonder how Eldest Brother is doing right now...?

Taking a deep breath, he put such thoughts aside and focused on keeping up with Young Lord Aurora and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. The three of them shot through the dark green sky and its dappled moonlight. Soon enough, the dark green moonlight merged into the black, cold wind. Snowflakes flew with the wind, piercing through the sky, before eventually reaching that huge valley. That was where the three of them stopped.

“This is the place,” Young Lord Aurora said, looking down into it.

The valley started in the extreme north and zig-zagged across the primeval motherworld. It looked almost like a massive, ghastly wound that cut down to the bone. The countless bronze doors Xu Qing had seen earlier responded to Young Lord Aurora’s gaze. They started trembling, and the sourcefiends outside of them all looked up and stared at the three of them. But it was a bit different from what Xu Qing had experienced before....

The sourcefiends looked scared. And what was even more terrifying was that they were making sounds like those animals would make when they were feeling threatened.

Xu Qing felt an instant sense of unease. He looked at Young Lord Aurora.

Young Lord Aurora hovered in midair, his black robe not moving at all despite the cold wind. A moment later, he plucked an alcohol flagon off his waist, lifted it, and took a drink. Then he splashed some alcohol out of it. Astonishingly, the alcohol seemed to contain the reflection of countless heavenly bodies.

Young Lord Aurora lifted his pale right hand and pushed it toward the glacier on one side of the canyon. The glacier trembled as though a giant invisible hand had grabbed it.

“But from my perspective, if you consider this planet to be the mother of the gods, then that means that very first god must have cut open hīs mother’s belly and crawled out. And this is the wound left behind afterward.”

As Young Lord Aurora spoke, he lifted his left hand toward the glacier on the other side of the valley. Then he shoved both of his hands to either side with great force. Heaven and earth trembled violently.

A cracking sound rang out from the depths of the valley, so loud it would make one’s teeth ache. At the same time, the glacier on either side of the valley began to move, almost like a scab being ripped away from a wound. All of the bronze doors in the valley started shaking. A mist as black as ink poured out from the valley. At the same time, the sourcefiends howled and, seemingly driven by instinct, shot out of the valley along with the mist. They headed directly toward Young Lord Aurora!

“You mere vehicles dare to make such a ruckus?”

A vertical red eye appeared on Young Lord Aurora’s forehead, which erupted with massive force. Rumbling sounds echoed out as the mist from the valley was shredded into nothing. The sourcefiends within it howled in anguish from the pressure, and all scattered. Some of them were even ripped to shreds.

Xu Qing was shaken deeply.

It was a given that Young Lord Aurora was strong. After all, he was the grandson of the Immortal Paragon and was the son of an Immortal Lord. He had an extraordinary background and his shocking talent, and even though he had been sealed in the immortal palace for a long time, he still controlled the palace and everything in it that entire time.

He had developed the many worlds there, and had the destined opportunities necessary to become a Summer Immortal that entire time. And there was little need to mention the fact that, although Immortal Lord Aurora had perished, he had done it all for his son. Beyond all that, after the seal was broken, Young Lord Aurora was working to carry out this unknown plan created by the Immortal Paragon....

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly. Peak Summer Immortal!

“Before your big brother came here,” Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix said softly, “we secretly passed through the fringes of the battlefield in the Fourth Star Ring. While we were there, he had the opportunity to attack and kill the commander of the gods’ eastern army.”

Her words struck Xu Qing like a tempest. After all, it suddenly made the events back on the Fifth Star Ring battlefield much clearer. Xu Qing had previously speculated that the grindstone of flesh and blood was serving as a lamp to attract attention. It had been a distraction to allow someone to assassinate the commander of the eastern army in the Fourth Star Ring!![1]

Because of that, Goddess Starryeyes came in person to use hēr bloodline innate ability to bring back that assassinated officer more quickly. The death of the commander, the return of Spirit Jade, and the arrival of Starryeyes was the second step. The deal they made was another lantern. So was my escape and the bounty the gods put on my head. All of it... was to distract the gods in the Fourth Star Ring! Plans within plans, getting more complicated the entire time!

And the entire point of everything... was to hide the fact... that Young Lord Aurora was coming here!

Xu Qing’s mind spun as all the puzzle pieces clicked together.

Just what I would expect of a plan put in place by the Immortal Paragon....

Xu Qing took a deep breath. He looked at Young Lord Aurora, then looked over his shoulder at Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. “So what’s going to happen now?”

She looked at her husband as he started walking toward the valley. “Your big brother is going to peel the skin off this primeval motherworld.”

Peel the skin off! Xu Qing had experienced a lot of things in life, and had witnessed all sorts of freakish and gruish things. But the words he had just heard still struck him to the core with astonishment. His eyes shone. What style....

Xu Qing reeled, but at the same time, his eyes were shining. It was just like the time back in the Aurora Immortal Palace when he first met Young Lord Aurora. It was also like the path he had walked when he first formed his space-time and realized the direction he needed to pursue.

As Young Lord Aurora continued walking, he said, “Xu Qing, this is your path. I’m just borrowing it for the moment. After you achieve your dao, you’ll be the only person who can use it!”

As he passed, the sourcefiends lost their height and became flat, and like talisman paper from the Yellow Springs, they floated about. The sourcefiends could offer no resistance. They could not block his way. They could do nothing other than allow Young Lord Aurora to continue to walk into their lands!

In the world below the glacier, heaven had previously been the glacier itself. As Young Lord Aurora descended, both of his hands pushed out in either direction. An aurora spread out from him, turning into a sea of light that spread out below, dispelling the haze and revealing all of the lands.

Those lands were actually... a dull purple layer of flesh-like rock! In fact, close examination would reveal that the rock was actually covered with a membrane that was very much like an epidermis! Slender tentacles spread up from it like grass reaching toward the stars! And at the end of every single one of those tentacles was a golden eye. All of the eyes were staring directly at Young Lord Aurora! This was the true skin of the primeval motherworld!

Xu Qing’s eyes shone as he stepped forth alongside Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. At the same time, Young Lord Aurora thrust his hands out, with fingers curved like clawed hooks as he shoved them toward the rock! Then he viciously yanked upward!

A thunderous groan echoed out from the depths of the ground. Hands trembling, Young Lord Aurora began to rip up the planet’s skin, bringing broken ice chunks with it. This was peeling the skin!!

The ripping sound was like a furious roar. A fountain of blood filled with planetary rubble erupted, shooting up! It was like a blood rain, except instead of falling from the sky it was rising into it! It turned into sky-obscuring, sun-blocking red clouds that spread out to replace heaven!

At the same time, as the land was lifted up, the millions upon millions of golden eyes glared furiously, sending innumerable golden gazes shooting like arrows toward Young Lord Aurora. As they neared, a black vortex sprang into being in the blood eye on his forehead, and it devoured all of the gazes.

Next, he ripped the planetary skin upward! An intense ripping sound echoed out as two chunks of the skin rose higher! From a distance, it looked like an inverted 八 character.

The area involved grew larger and larger, and the ripping grew louder. Higher and higher it went, until finally it formed a relatively intact piece of skin! There it was in the dome of heaven. Wild colors flashed.

And then Young Lord Aurora said, “Seal the heavens. The fetal membrane becomes a world.”

The terrifying planetary skin writhed as it fused with the void, turning into an amber-colored fetal membrane! The gigantic embryonic skin was now the canopy of heaven in the primeval motherworld. The dark green moonlight native to the planet hit the membrane like a physical force, causing ripples to spread out. However, the light did not pierce it.

Looking up from below, the fetal membrane gave a sensation of being made of flesh and blood, complete with veins and arteries that formed a star chart. And the drops of blood flowing within were the rivers of stars. At the same time, it reflected the writhing of the flesh and blood that made the lands below.

Xu Qing was shaken to the core. The heaven of the primeval motherworld really had been changed!

Light from outside was obscured, and the world was cast into an eternal blood-colored evening. The motherworld had really been skinned like a huge beast. As for the land, it was made of dark red muscle covered with horrifying blood vessels that leaked viscous ringsource. The motherworld seemed to be twitching deep inside, causing the lands to quake. It was almost as if some ancient entity were inside, slowly waking up.

Xu Qing took a deep breath, his heart pounding as he watched Young Lord Aurora skin the planet.

When the young lord walked forward on the exposed flesh, his shoes were covered with sticky fluid. Surrounding him were 30,000-meter-tall waves of blood that sprayed out from the conglomeration of flesh. That provided the backdrop!

The motherworld seemed to call out in sadness. As countless sourcefiends crawled about in the blood, their cries joined in. It was a sound of unending grief and terror.

As for Young Lord Aurora, he seemed to be taking some measurements. Ultimately, they led him to a certain location.

“This is the place.” Reaching up to his forehead, he pushed his fingers down and then viciously dragged them out. A massive sword appeared, shining with silver light that drove away the color of blood. It was... the sword of the Immortal Paragon!

Young Lord Aurora didn’t hesitate for a moment. He stabbed the sword viciously down into the flesh below, then began to slash the sword forward.

The entire planet issued a scream of agony. More blood gushed out. The new wound spread rapidly, until... the planetary core was revealed! It was the planetary uterus that the primeval motherworld had used when that first god was born.

“Is he...?” Xu Qing said, his mind spinning as a seemingly insane notion occurred to him.

“You guessed it...” said Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix. “Your big brother has picked this spot... to reach godly ascension!”

Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix’s words were like a sharp blade that sliced through all of the fog and confirmed that Xu Qing’s preposterous speculation was actually correct! In this very spot where the first god had been born in the Fourth Star Ring, Young Lord Aurora would attempt godly ascension! It was a level of daring unheard of in either modern times or ancient!

Yet even as the fog dispelled, uncertainties occurred to Xu Qing. He had witnessed cultivators changing their dao to that of the gods, and it was not an easy task.

That was why the Immortal Paragon ultimately chose to seal my husband in the Aurora Immortal Palace!

When Xu Qing heard that, he immediately understood why Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix had said that only Immortal Lord Aurora or his son could accomplish this task! It was because... the higher the cultivation base of a cultivator, the more difficult it would become to change the course of one’s life. For example, Empress Summer Departure had only been an Imperial Sovereign, yet even still, had required multiple ceremonies.

Young Lord Aurora had a peak Summer Immortal cultivation base. For him to change his dao would require an almost infinitely difficult ceremony. And yet, the infinite... now had a solid foundation. And that foundation was this location. The primeval motherworld!

This was where the Fourth Star Ring’s first god had been born, and it met all the requirements. The personhood available... was sufficient!

However... though the requirements were met and the personhood was sufficient, there was still one more thing that would be required for a peak Summer Immortal to change daos. And that was a godspark! It was said that a single spark could set a prairie on fire, and the godspark... was exactly like that!

Of course, an ordinary spark wouldn’t be enough. That was why no other cultivator could do such a thing. But Immortal Lord Aurora and his son were different!

The Immortal Paragon of the Fifth Star Ring had been infected by the godbane thanks to the God Paragon. After that, he was contaminated. That was the power that was unleashed when the God Paragon’s godhood was shattered. It became a boundless godly might that formed a curse. Not even someone on the level of the Immortal Paragon was strong enough to get rid of it. It stayed behind as a sealing mark. The Immortal Paragon eventually figured out a way to get rid of the mark by passing it down through his descendants until it was eventually gone.

Immortal Lord Aurora lived a life of grief and pain. And he... didn’t want his son to experience the same thing, so he ended his own life. He succeeded by raising Young Lord Aurora in a sealed environment. However, though it was technically a success, it wasn’t a complete success, considering what happened afterward.

And now, Young Lord Aurora had selected the Fourth Star Ring’s primeval motherworld as the place to use the remnant of the godbane to change his dao and achieve godly ascension!

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered brightly. “He’s not just aiming for godly ascension in general. He’s going to become... a God Lord! With the personhood of the primeval motherworld to become a God Lord... if he succeeds, Young Lord Aurora will be able to command the destiny aura of the Fourth Star Ring. He’ll be deeply connected to it! And after that....”

Xu Qing struggled to control his breathing as he realized what would come afterward. He could already guess why he and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix needed to be here....

Young Lord Aurora sat down cross-legged in the naked flesh, his long hair glimmering in the blood-red light shining from above. He was looking at the planetary uterus that he had peeled away.

A sound like a pulse crashed like thunder from inside the flesh, echoing across heaven and earth. It was the pulse of the motherworld! Along with the pulse came an awakening consciousness. It was as if the planet itself was waking up.

When Young Lord Aurora heard the pulse and sensed the awakening, he calmly lifted his right hand, took the Immortal Paragon’s sword, and stabbed it into his own chest! “Blood Contract!”

Thump-thump. Thump-thump!

Eyes glittering, Xu Qing flew down. He settled down cross-legged next to Young Lord Aurora atop the flesh of the primeval motherworld.

“Planetary soul!”

Mi Ming.[1]

When Xu Qing saw that happen, he sensed something within the memory river, which caused a splash as two characters appeared.

At the same time, Young Lord Aurora’s voice echoed in his mind.

Xu Qing!

Terrifying fluctuations were now rolling out from Young Lord Aurora. The entire primeval motherworld was shaking violently as complex striations appeared on it. Young Lord Aurora slowly opened his eyes. In his right eye was visible a shrunken planetary system, while in his left eye was universal lightning. Both were golden. He slowly stood. With the millions and millions of blood vessel tentacles writhing about, it made a sight both gruish and holy.

He had become hē!

A peak True God!

Xu Qing had seen many, many gods. He had even seen a few True Gods. However... he had never seen anything like Young Lord Aurora as hē stood there on the primeval motherworld, emanating such mightiness.

The mutagen was extremely strong and terrifyingly active, causing all surrounding things to ripple and distort. Hīs godly will was like a sharp blade that caused heavenly bodies to tremble and universes to vibrate. What was more, the holy, golden light emanating off hīm was equally impressive.

At the same time, hīs form was changing! Black crystals spread out across hīs chest, becoming like a suit of scale armor. And upon the crystals were complex and ancient designs. The designs formed a network like a star chart, every part of which pulsed with an astonishing godly will. Astonishingly, if one looked closely, it would become clear that the lines which made the design were actually hīs true name!

From within the design stretched a dense host of blood vessels that connected to the primeval motherworld. As Young Lord Aurora rose to hīs feet, it looked like hē was actually an integral part of the motherworld!

The land of flesh around hīm churned. With the planetary skin to serve as heaven, and blood raining down, all heaven and earth was crimson, serving as the perfect complement to hīm. The anguished howls of the motherworld formed part of the background. As for the rise and fall of the surrounding lands, they corresponded to Young Lord Aurora’s breathing. It was the same with the pulsing of the subterranean meridians.

Taken altogether, everything became hīs terrifying personhood!

It was not merely the personhood of a peak True God. There was also the presence of the true name, the connection to the primeval motherworld, and even more deeply... the spark formed by the godbane! This personhood could step through the doorway of something truly paramount! A personhood like this would have a profound impact on the surrounding world!

Even when just barely sensing it, Xu Qing felt that familiar sensation of his fleshly body being a separate entity that wanted to split away from him. After his cultivation base reached a certain level in the past, he had ceased to ever experience that sensation. But now, in the presence of Young Lord Aurora, he felt his breathing becoming unstable. His body felt like it was being ripped apart, and his eyeballs seemed to swivel of their own accord.

Though he was able to forcefully suppress such effects, the infection of a god that he was experiencing caused something like chanting to explode in his ears. The chanting of a godly voice filled every part of him, turning into distortions and madness that wanted to destroy all life.

At that moment of crisis, Xu Qing unleashed all of the ringsource he had to suppress the abnormalities. Those abnormalities became a destructive, unstoppable tempest that threatened to wipe away all forms of resistance within him.

But then a voice spoke into Xu Qing’s soul. It was a godly voice that came from himself, and from his own true name from earlier.

“Xu Qing.”

The sound caused a tremor to pass through him. His eyes instantly became clear, and all the abnormalities within him instantly calmed down. A strange connection to the Fourth Star Ring appeared with his soul.

He took a deep breath and looked at Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix at his side.

The aura of the Immortal Paragon....

Young Lord Aurora stood on the planetary uterus, black crystals spreading out over hīm, godly might surging and cold apathy filling hīs eyes. Hīs human nature was rapidly fading away, while hīs godly nature was quickly filling hīm up. It seemed just on the verge of completely overwhelming hīm.

Two families are now united in marriage by this covenant that never ends....

And thus, the agreement is confirmed.

Every word seemed to contain life force. It was canon. It was law. And it came from... Immortal Lord Aurora! This item was the marriage contract between Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and Young Lord Aurora!

As soon as it appeared, karma created a pulling force like a powerful anchor. The words on the plaque glittered, full of the blessings of Immortal Lord Aurora. And then the plaque floated through the air toward the young lord. As it neared, a connection sprang into being!

Young Lord Aurora shivered, and the cold apathy that had been flooding hīs eyes suddenly stopped.

Two names flew off of the marriage contract. They were the names of Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and Young Lord Aurora, and as they flew forth and merged into hīm, the coldness and apathy showed signs of melting.

Upon seeing that, Xu Qing waved his hand, causing his immortal embryo to appear. Within it, the Aurora Immortal Palace rose up, turning into his own karma, which in turn provided another anchor. It connected with Young Lord Aurora!

Gods were without emotions! Of course, that was not an absolute. Normally speaking, preheaven gods were all like that, although there were exceptions. For example, Goddess Starryeyes had developed emotions because of unique outside influences.

As for postheaven gods, thēy would usually experience a complete transformation. However, emotions still existed in thēir memories, and whenever thēy recalled the past, it would result in slight fluctuations. However, thēy were little more than fluctuations. The exception was when some gods, before transforming, buried obsessions deep inside. Then, if the fluctuations became strong enough, the importance of an anchor would become manifest.

Anchors were more often used to re-awaken human nature, but even more than that... to affix human nature permanently in place! They could make human nature like a towering reef that would remain no matter what huge waves smashed against it.

Right now, the marriage contract and the Aurora Immortal Palace tugged at Young Lord Aurora, causing the cold apathy in hīs eyes to melt away. Human nature did not disappear.

Looking around, Young Lord Aurora murmured, “So this is what it feels like to transform from being an immortal into a god.”

To hīs eyes, the world looked different now. It was withered, feeble, dirty, and chaotic.... Everything about the past didn’t seem important now. What was precious before became distracting. Even the most important people were like dust. The only thing worth pursuing in life was the elevation of one’s own life force. And anything that got in the way of that should be destroyed. It didn’t matter who the obstructer was. freewebnovel.com

Except... Young Lord Aurora’s gaze fell on Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and Xu Qing. Those two people were like threads connected to hīm, guiding hīs thoughts and becoming exceptions. They were like two burning fires in hīs life, lamps that could lead hīm back home.

“No problem. I’m fine.” Young Lord Aurora smiled at Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix and Xu Qing. It looked as if hē was working hard to rekindle emotion. “I remember. I know what I have to do next.”

Reaching up with hīs crystal-covered right hand, hē made a slashing motion toward the canopy of heaven. Huge rifts opened up in the air, and deep inside of them was primal-chaos that didn’t come from this dimension.

Xu Qing’s pupils constricted as he realized that, on the other side of the rifts were countless chains of karma, crumbling and reforming. Turbulence struck all the natural and magical laws, as if a pair of unseen hands were re-writing the rules of logic that governed the star ring.

“Godhood, assemble!”

At the moment, countless gods shivered within thēir temples. The instinct to prostrate erupted from thēir god souls.
