But then he had run into Xu Qing and Erniu in the Revered Ancient mainland. By that point, the important parts of the plan were already underway. Things fell into place from there.

He needed to do it at a special location: the primeval motherworld, where the first god in the Fourth Star Ring had been born. He needed to do it at a special time: when Immortal Lord Nineshores was leaving office and Immortal Lord Aurora was succeeding him. That was when it could be completed.... That was when a god could be used to create a new Immortal Lord!!

This... has never, ever been done!

Xu Qing was rocked with astonishment as he looked up at the mighty Young Lord Aurora. As everything clicked together, he began to form some speculations about what the Immortal Paragon was planning.

Actually, there is someone who did something like this in the past. I just wasn’t there to witness it.

Xu Qing was thinking about Li Zihua! That was someone who had walked a similar path.[1]

What Young Lord Aurora was doing right here and now was leaving a much more profound effect. That said, there were still many unknown elements.

As these things became clear to Xu Qing, the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring surged forth. The sky had become silver!

It was the color of the destiny aura from the Fifth Star Ring, and it... swept through the space-time memories of the Fourth Star Ring gods, slipping through the cracks to fill the area outside the primeval motherworld. It stained the void, turning everything silver. And as a result, the heaven over the primeval motherworld... was thoroughly transforming.

It became a majestic river of destiny aura that surged forth from the horizon. It came to replace the sun and moon, and also to bolster Young Lord Aurora! Inside of it were projections of all living beings in the Fifth Star Ring. There were illusory cultivators, universes and starry skies, and numerous heavens beyond heaven.

They were all cheering for Aurora! The soundless cheering became like fluorescent fishes swimming through the river, leaving behind streaks filled with immortal sealing marks that drifted toward the young lord.

A huge silver vortex was forming, with him in the middle. Rumbling sounds drifted out, filling the primeval motherworld inside and out. And in that manner, it entered the memories of the host of gods in the Fourth Star Ring.

Shaking began to fill the Fourth Star Ring. The souls of the numerous gods trembled. The statues in the temples shook. Veined lines ripped open throughout the starry sky. Crimson ringsource, like the blood of gods, seeped out of those veins and spread into the sea of stars.

Young Lord Aurora, who was orchestrating all of this, hovered above the primeval motherworld, within the vortex of destiny aura.

“Gods come from heaven,” he said softly. “The dao of immortals comes from the self....”

The innumerable immortal sealing marks in the vortex of destiny aura began to glitter brightly, and to purify the godsource and mutagen coming off Young Lord Aurora. As the purification process proceeded, sounds emerged like the strings of a zither snapping.

The sounds materialized, infecting the godsource and turning into a host of burning godfire lamps. This was the godsource of God Lord Aurora!

The lamps were densely packed and seemed to have no end. But the moment they formed, they started crumbling! In the blink of an eye, millions upon millions of god lamps collapsed into ashes. It was like they had been sliced apart, as though some blade had chopped down, severing the Fourth Star Ring and Young Lord Aurora from each other!

The destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring entered Young Lord Aurora’s spine. That was the godly meridian the Fourth Star Ring had bestowed when he ascended to the level of God Lord. Right now, the power of the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura ripped that spine out, thus severing his resonance with the dao of gods in the Fourth Star Ring. In an instant, all of the godly veins covering Young Lord Aurora went dim.

The moment the scene started to play out, a rumbling like a whimper drifted out from the depths of the Fourth Star Ring. Īt came in the form of the combined wills of all the gods in the star ring. Īt could be called the dao of the gods, and īts call turned into a roar of rage. Īt could not permit something like this to happen!

That roar of rage seemed to contain innumerable godly voices!

“This is not permitted!”

“This is not permitted!”

“This is not permitted!”

As the godly voices descended, through the memories of the gods, the sound entered the primeval motherworld and rushed toward the river of destiny aura from the Fifth Star Ring. The river of destiny aura reacted as if giant hands had squeezed it with great force, turning it into blood-red amber. The transformation started outside of the primeval motherworld, then spread rapidly.

From a distance, it looked like the sky was turning amber, as the effects spread through the river toward Young Lord Aurora’s vicinity. As the vortex of destiny aura solidified, the will calling out to the motherworld caused the planet to start trembling.

A will was waking up! The ground quaked as Young Lord Aurora’s conversion was interrupted!

The young lord’s face distorted, and it was possible to see the previously dimming god veins starting to turn bright again. Astonishingly, within every single vein it was possible to see the godly will of the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods. That godly will was attempting to drive out the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring in one fell swoop.

But how could the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring simply fall back? The amber shattered as the destiny aura made a comeback! It smashed into the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods with unprecedented force. Neither would back down. The dao of gods extended, causing the magical laws of the Fourth Star Ring to reach the various god dynasties.

Instantly, the Fourth Star Ring’s God Lords strode out. Thēy could stand by and watch as Aurora became a god. But now a god was changing into an immortal, and the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods was requiring that thēy interfere.

However, just as the God Lords were about to step onto the primeval motherworld... a host of figures appeared out of nowhere to block their path! Those figures... all pulsed with an aura no weaker than the God Lords, except formed from immortal might.

They were the Immortal Lords of the Fifth Star Ring!

At the same time, an old man in hemp sandals appeared outside the paramount god court. There he stood, his eyes steely, not saying a word. The god court... was as silent as ever.

***

On the primeval motherworld, Young Lord Aurora looked up into the dome of heaven, where it was possible to see gold and silver intersecting.

“Not willing to let go of me?”

He extended his right hand and pushed it down toward the primeval motherworld. That gesture caused the entire planet to tremble. Heaven and earth heaved. Then an illusory river appeared from within the depths of the motherworld.

It was a river filled with true names. Among those countless true names was one in particular that glittered far more prominently than the others! It was the true name Young Lord Aurora had left there.

Mi Ming!

Seek for what is not seen. The sun and moon are the brightness![2]

Years ago, Immortal Lord Aurora had taken away the sun and moon from the Fifth Star Ring and put them into his son’s name. And not long after that... his son took the sun and moon of the Fifth Star Ring and, by means of his true name, put them... in the river that represented the dao of gods in the Fourth Star Ring!

They were buried like a nail! And right now, as he pushed down, that nail... started to explode!

The sun and moon appeared!

It was like the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura opening up a door leading into the depths of the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods! Rumbling sounds echoed out as the destiny aura opened the door of the sun and moon in the river of true names, and rushed inside!

It became a boundless immortal lightning that sent ripples through the entire river of true names! Every bolt of lightning contained materialized destiny aura, as well as heroic spirits of the Fifth Star Ring!

Xu Qing had visited the Heroic Immortal Tombs in the Nineshores heaven beyond heaven, and had paid respects to immortals who had fallen in battle. The mark they left in destiny aura was now made manifest in the lightning.

That lightning shot with deadly force toward the true name! This was how the sun and moon would truly return!

The Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods rippled and distorted as a dramatic transformation took place. One grew strong while the other weakened! The destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring surged with great intensity!

The solidified amber cracked, and the destiny aura vortex around Young Lord Aurora began spinning again! The conversion from god to immortal proceeded. Millions upon millions of god lamps began to go out. Streams of godsource emerged from Young Lord Aurora, splitting away from him. And the black crystals that had covered him started to fade away. His godly aura became weak, while the might of an Immortal Lord grew strong upon him.

What was more, as the destiny aura poured into his spine, an incredible transformation hit Young Lord Aurora. His god bones shattered, section by section. In their place, new bones grew, as sparkling and translucent as crystal. The new bones were covered with immortal script, and close examination would reveal that it was a shrunken star chart of the Fifth Star Ring.

These were star ring bones! Only paragons had such bones! Only an Immortal Paragon or a God Paragon would have a star chart of the star ring on their bones when they broke through. But right now, it was happening inside of Young Lord Aurora!

However, the method being employed was different. The Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura was the flame, while the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods was the kindling. With a paramount godspark, the power of two star rings could be used for the forging! In other words, power from two star rings was converging on him!

Of course, most of the extracted power came from the Fourth Star Ring! Howls of agony from the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods echoed through the starry sky. The Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods was experiencing an unprecedented catastrophe. The destiny aura from the Fifth Star Ring was infecting īt inside and out!

Young Lord Aurora was creating another huge problem, as he was detaching and shredding īts natural laws. As a result, īt was struggling in an unheard-of fashion!

Outside of the primeval motherworld, an enormous starry door that pulsed with ancient time suddenly opened up. As it did, an indescribable aura emerged. It seemed like the aura of a god, but there was something different about it. Apparently, it was even more ancient!

After the starry door opened, a host of ancient statues were revealed, all of them surrounded by gray fog. They came from an era far removed from the current one. Perhaps it was better to say that their time had been stretched out so long it surpassed that of the first god to have been born on the primeval motherworld.

What was more, if one peered further into the starry door, it would be possible to see that, beyond the congregated statues, there existed the crumbling remains of an ancient planet. It wasn’t possible to see anything clearly beyond that. There was only a symbol growing larger and larger. The symbol glittered with gray light and something indescribably mysterious. Neither gods nor cultivators had seen any symbol like it before!

After appearing, it pieced together a dilapidated iron chain and then began moving toward the primeval motherworld. Wherever it passed, the starry sky couldn’t stand up to the force, and collapsed. Soon, the empty memories where the primeval motherworld existed couldn’t hold on any longer... and they started to crumble! The God Lords and Immortal Lords who had been locked in combat were all stunned.

Having been pushed to the ultimate limit, this was what the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods chose to do to seek salvation! Īt had opened this unknown door.

Up to this point, the paramount god temple in the Fourth Star Ring had not reacted, not even to Young Lord Aurora becoming a god or transforming back into an immortal. No orders had been issued. But now, it suddenly lit up with boundless godlight.

Out from the godlight strode the God Paragon!

“The Living God Umbilical Cord, the endless end... has finally been opened!”

The God Paragon. There was no more ultimate and paramount entity in the Fourth Star Ring. After a long moment of silence, hē finally appeared, walking slowly out of the god court.

The light in the starry sky started rippling. Countless red lightning bolts appeared, weaving together in the void to create a staircase underfoot. And thus, hē slowly walked forth.

Every step hē took caused cracks to spread out through the starry sky, like shattered porcelain. And within each of the cracks were illusory images. Some images depicted living beings slowly growing younger. Enormous trees turned into seeds, and middle-aged creatures turned into embryos. Some images depicted the starry sky starting to wither until it was destroyed in a dazzling flash of light. The scenes created a clear impression of hīs majestic status.

The entire Fourth Star Ring was affected. Some weak life forms exploded like blooming lotuses, with their brain matter becoming prismatic bridges that led to heaven. Some temples emitted deafening rumbling sounds as the paramount godliness surging into them caused instant transformations, making them transparent, and ultimately causing them to become sparkling manifestations of godly qualities. Even the cycles of day and night and the orbits of heavenly bodies became crystallized.

What was more, within the depths of the spatial rifts were ancient living entities whose tentacles curled toward the god court and trembled excitedly. All of the God Lords were currently bowing thēir heads in the direction of the god court. All were offering worship! All gods’ eyes were focused on the same thing!

This most paramount of entities stepped forward, something that the vast majority of living beings couldn’t even perceive due to the limits of their own form, until hē was fully manifest in the starry sky.

Astonishingly, it was a body made of three trillion dao projections! The outer layer was formed from a flow of galactic debris, collapsing from inside to out to create the shining outline of a person, but at the same time, revealing the shape of millions upon millions of heavenly bodies exploding. Any who attempted to look directly at the face of this entity would see endlessly shrinking nebulae whose every fold and crease seemed to be filled with the birth and destruction of reincarnation.

Raw power seemed to leak out of the dimensional rifts. It would occasionally turn into stellar fragments that drifted into the mortal world of the various gods, where it became godly light that spread for millions upon millions of kilometers. As the light shone, the wind on all the planets stopped moving. Countless clouds became like black glass inset with gold. At the same time, the god weapons of all the various gods suddenly began to leak a dark gold liquid!

Howls of anguish echoed out. God weapons that would never decay for all eternity were now crumbling thanks to the godly might weighing down on them.

This was the God Paragon! And the godly voice that echoed into the star ring was like a godly divination that could influence all living beings.

“The Living God Umbilical Cord, the endless end... has finally been opened! This path is hidden deep within the dao of gods....”

The voice did not echo into the ears of the host of gods. Rather, it was in thēir very marrow, where it vibrated like tolling bells! That was because the presence of a godly divination made many spoken words meaningless.

All living beings, and in fact, all gods, found that a transformation to natural law was being imprinted into their souls. And then... they started to collapse. It was because eight of the words that had just been uttered were actually taboo! And all of the external influences at play were not intentional on the part of the God Paragon.

They were merely the side-effects of hīm showing up at the last moment. They were ripples flowing out from hīm, and the effects of the words hē had spoken. The entire Fourth Star Ring seemed on the way to transforming into something very bizarre.

Both True Gods and God Lords... even the being in the coffin in the forbidden region... were struck speechless. The chains with the god talismans on them simply hung quietly.

From beginning to end, the God Paragon’s attention was focused solely on the Immortal Paragon, who stood there in his hemp sandals.

“I didn’t do anything to stop you,” the God Paragon said. “So now... are you going to stop me?”

The Immortal Paragon’s eyes glittered vaguely as he sensed the starry door outside the primeval motherworld. Finally... he shook his head.

The God Paragon said nothing further. Hē lifted hīs left hand. Hīs palm no longer contained a sun and moon, nor did it contain primal-chaos. Instead, it contained something that surpassed the material, and was called the ‘existential conception.’

Countless circular rings of light within it constantly brightened and faded over and over again. Every ring of light contained images of different civilizations rising and falling. This was something that only an entity with personhood equal to hīs could understand. It was... paramount godhood!

With a look at hīs palm, hē slowly clenched hīs left hand into a fist and took a step forward. That single step taken by hīs majestic form caused hīm to appear outside of the primeval motherworld. There, hē didn’t bother to even look at the motherworld. Instead... hē looked at the starry door and the gray world within it.

Hē did not hesitate, as this was an opportunity hē had waited countless years for. Hē stepped into the starry door!

Hē... was seeking the path to Living God!

When hīs majestic form and terrifying personhood entered the starry door, the door began to rumble loudly, as if it couldn’t sustain the force.

The Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods also struggled. But it did no good, because the door... was already open! The God Paragon forced hīs way inside, and then charged into the depths of the fog in that gray world!

As for the starry door itself, the violent intrusion caused it to crumble to pieces. A rumbling boom echoed out, and the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods moaned in grief.

The dao of gods deteriorated! Earlier, a chain of symbols had stretched from the starry door to the outside. As the door collapsed, so did the chain. However, the section that was on the outside... fell down toward the primeval motherworld.

The chain fell down through the void. The Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura couldn’t stop it, and within moments, it appeared within the primeval motherworld’s dome of heaven. It looked like a huge snake that could devour worlds as it shot directly toward Young Lord Aurora!

This was an unexpected turn of events! The mighty pressure of the chain caused the entire primeval motherworld to tremble. The dome of heaven split, and both Xu Qing and Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix were shaken to the core.

This was not godly might, nor was it the dao of immortals. This was something much older, and it surpassed the limits of perception. It was like a tribulation.

Young Lord Aurora was in great danger, but his eyes shone with determination. “The dao of immortals is life, the dao of gods is death... I guess I’ll just borrow your power to get rid of this godhood even faster!”

Suddenly, he lifted his right hand and stabbed his fingers into his own eyes. Grabbing the golden light there, he dragged it out and severed it! Blood poured out of his eye sockets.

Without any hesitation, he took advantage of the dao bones forming within him to... bring back his personal canon that he had developed as a youth. It was the mirror canon!

By using that personal canon, he was replacing his lost eyes. An instant later, his eyes once again shone with radiance and light! His eyes had been restored!

The pupils were like mirrors, reflecting everything within the river of destiny aura above. It made it seem like the river was within him! And it caused the river of destiny aura to flow through him! Rumbling sounds echoed out as the power of destiny aura from outside and inside overlapped!

A heaven-shaking, earth-shattering mightiness erupted from Young Lord Aurora as he fused with the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura.

“Xu Qing, I have a gift for you. Do you dare take it?”

Xu Qing’s eyes glittered in response to the suggestion. He could guess exactly what kind of gift Young Lord Aurora was talking about!

There was only one gift that Young Lord Aurora could give after changing from god to immortal, and it was something he couldn’t allow to infect him! It was... the godly authority of fate that he had stolen from the Fourth Star Ring’s God Paragon when he rose to the level of God Lord!

Xu Qing now had further speculations about why the Immortal Paragon had sent him here! His heart was pounding, and he had trouble breathing steadily.

Voice full of determination, he said, “Of course I dare!”

Most people wouldn’t dare to trifle with Eminent Desolation’s karma. But Xu Qing had long since developed deep karma with Eminent Desolation. After all, his god clone was made from Eminent Desolation’s flesh and blood. Granted, he’d had help. His Eldest Brother had taken him along to steal the blood, and his Master had acquired the flesh somehow. But facts were facts, and the reality was that taking this godly authority wouldn’t change much.

With that thought in mind, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered even more brightly.

Up in the sky, Young Lord Aurora heard Xu Qing’s response and laughed heartily. Reaching up with his right hand, he made a grasping gesture, and the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura responded to both the internal and external connection to him. Within his palm formed... a blade made of destiny aura!

As his dao bones trembled with power, he used the synergy between God Lord and Immortal Lord, as well as the godbane serving as godspark, to wield the blade of destiny aura toward the incoming chain of symbols.... He slashed it toward the chain!

As the blade descended, cracks appeared on the thread it contained from the fate of the Fourth Star Ring. The light of future and past connected into a blood-red tapestry. The Fifth Star Ring destiny aura trembled, and by extension, all living beings shook.

With those two things bolstering it, the blade... hit the chain. A deafening boom rang out. Cracks spread out on the surface of the primeval motherworld, and waves surged across the sea of memories.

The chain shook!

Young Lord Aurora also shook. He staggered backward as if millions upon millions of universes were exploding inside him. Gaping wounds opened up all over his fleshly body, and god blood turned into crimson crystals that scattered everywhere.

Within those crystals were reflections of the moment he changed from immortal to god. When the crystals hit the destiny aura or the chain, they melted, turning into liquid primal-chaos that formed the foundation of the dao of immortals.

The liquid flowed into Young Lord Aurora’s dantian region, and the godhood that had been crumbling suddenly started forming again. Then, countless threads swept out to connect to Young Lord Aurora.

They were resisting the outside force! The threads were karma!

“Still not enough!!”

A mix of golden and silver blood sprayed out of Young Lord Aurora’s mouth, but his eyes shone with vicious determination. Within his pupils appeared a black and a white fish, swirling around in a yin-yang symbol.

In his left eye were the karma threads encircling the godhood, which bolstered the crumbling magical laws of the Fourth Star Ring. In his right eye was a vortex of neonatal immortal origin, reflecting all the living beings of the Fifth Star Ring.

And then Young Lord Aurora shot up toward the descending chain of symbols!

Above the primeval motherworld, the chain of symbols glittered with gray light. It was a light that could eradicate all things, be they gods or cultivators, godly authority or canon, natural laws or magical laws. All things were at a much lower level than it.

Apparently, this light from the Living God Umbilical Cord could crush all logic in the thirty-six higher star rings. As such, fighting against it with upward momentum would require using overwhelming force to whittle it down. And only something with equal levels of power could face it as an equal.

That was why Young Lord Aurora’s blade formed from the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura had been incapable of breaking it, and had only given it a slight pause. Young Lord Aurora deserved his reputation as being a consummate chosen. The moment he saw the chain of symbols falling toward him again, he had come up with a method to fight it.

To truly fight it... he needed to use the godhood within him! After all, that godhood was Eminent Desolation’s authority of fate that the God Paragon had once tried to steal. Because Eminent Desolation was half a step into the Living God level, that godhood was the only thing that could equal the chain of symbols, or perhaps even surpass it.

Meeting the force of the chain of symbols with godhood like that was the best choice. Furthermore, Young Lord Aurora... didn’t just want to rely on that godhood alone to fight back. He wanted to take the opportunity provided by the clash between the godhood and the chain to actually sever the connection between himself and the godhood. That connection came in the form of karma threads between himself and Eminent Desolation!

As the power of gods and immortals swirled in his eyes, he shot up into the air and unleashed unheard-of force. He was the vessel to channel the Fourth Star Ring and the Fifth Star Ring, sending out explosive power to form a long blade that was a mixture of gold and silver.

He made another attack against the Living God Umbilical Cord’s chain of symbols!

Heaven and earth shook. The starry sky filled with rumbling sounds. The primeval motherworld and everything around it vibrated violently. A terrifying tempest swept out in all directions.

The Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods moaned in agony again. The Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura surged with intensity.

The chain of symbols slowed down to a stop yet again. The gray light within it had been significantly reduced by the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods and the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura, but there was still some left. It flowed down the length of the blade.

When it entered Young Lord Aurora, it became pure destruction that raged forth with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. Young Lord Aurora shivered from head to toe, and blood oozed out of his eyes, ears, nose, and mouth. However, his eyes remained as vicious as before.

Golden light shone from the godhood within him, racing to slam into the invading gray light.

They collided. The shock of it caused the karma threads connecting the godhood and Young Lord Aurora to shiver. And then a few of them snapped.

At that critical moment, Young Lord Aurora didn’t hesitate to slash the blade out again. Heaven and earth shook as the blade light swept forth from Young Lord Aurora. He then launched a third, fourth, and a fifth attack! Each slash of the blade caused the chain to shake, and rocked the godhood, causing further breakage among the karma threads.

After nine blade attacks, madness began to rise within Young Lord Aurora. He then stretched out his left hand, releasing an explosion of golden light. He waved as right hand, sending out intense silver light.

Reaching out, he grabbed the chain of symbols. Expression distorting viciously, he let loose a howl that echoed through both the Fourth and the Fifth Star Rings. The godhood within him thrummed violently as a flame emerged from it, which surged through Young Lord Aurora’s arms and into the chain of symbols!

The chain burst into flames. However, it didn’t melt immediately. It just flickered as the flames slowly ate away at it.

As that happened, the threads connecting Young Lord Aurora to the godhood seemed on the verge of being fully destroyed.

And then, a tipping point was reached between the godhood and the symbols. Both sides went completely insane! The godhood rumbled as it shrank down, until it was a finger-nail sized fragment. Despite its size, though, its terrifying mightiness surpassed anything from before. It was as if fighting the chain of symbols had purified the godhood! The impurities had been extruded, leaving behind only the purest of half-step Living God Eminent Desolation’s paramount godhood!

At the same time, the karma threads connecting the godhood to Young Lord Aurora were unable to repair themselves. They were about half gone! Visible on the surface of the severed threads were images of Young Lord Aurora becoming a God Lord. Just like his godliness, they were fading away.

As for the chain of symbols, it had been worn down to such a degree that it couldn’t fight back any longer.... The chain of symbols burst into flames! It was visibly being burned up! As every part of it started crumbling into ashes, an astonishing sound emerged that resembled a musical instrument being played.

Meanwhile, Young Lord Aurora was surrounded by a sound like that of a rushing river. It was the flow of a new immortal origin. The terrifying immortal power of an Immortal Lord swept through the star chart of the Fifth Star Ring that existed on his dao bones, spreading out and filling the bones with silver light.

That influenced Young Lord Aurora’s form, causing him to revert from a godly appearance to that of a cultivator! It was as if human nature were flourishing within him, while godly nature was retreating. His hair changed from golden to white, eventually turning into flowing silver like a silver river. The aura of an immortal rose within him.

The dome of heaven trembled, and the dao of gods wailed. The destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring grew more robust. That was when Young Lord Aurora did something that no one could possibly have predicted. He lifted his right hand, which surged with the Fifth Star Ring’s destiny aura, and then he... pointed at Xu Qing!

“Xu Qing, you are the master of the Aurora Immortal Palace and heaven beyond heaven. You should benefit from the nourishment of the destiny aura from this beginning of an epoch. You are also a true monarch, so you have the right to be blessed by destiny aura! Furthermore, you have provided immense assistance both to the Fifth Star Ring and to me.

“On this day, I will give you two gifts. Consider this... the first gift!

“I, Mi Ming, having become an Immortal Lord and having taken office in the Fifth Star Ring, hereby issue an imperial decree! Fifth Star Ring destiny aura: go!”

Mi Ming’s words were a paramount imperial decree, and they caused the Fifth Star Ring destiny aura in the area to surge. As it did, one portion of the destiny aura became like a dragon rushing toward Xu Qing.

As it neared, Xu Qing’s heart raced. The destiny aura issued a draconic roar, and then... it entered Xu Qing!

Xu Qing’s cultivation base went wild! The nourishment of destiny aura brought pure ringsource. It contained the will of all living beings, like the approval of natural and magical laws. And it was backed by Mi Ming’s status. It was completely legitimate and just! And it was an amazing destined opportunity!

Rumbling sounds erupted from inside Xu Qing as the blessing caused his cultivation base to smash right through mid Quasi-Immortal and into... late Quasi-Immortal!

A shocking aura swept out of him. The moment Xu Qing had gained enlightenment of his ninth extreme, the canon of parallelism, he had earned the qualification to become a peak Quasi-Immortal.

The only thing he had been missing was ringsource! That was the main reason he had been so intent on finding more ringsource. What was unfortunate was that he needed a staggering amount of ringsource. His ability to absorb it was also an issue, and thus, his progress had been slow.

But now, this destined opportunity provided what he had been missing. In one shot, he was greatly bolstered. And the blessing of the destiny aura ensured that he had no trouble absorbing the ringsource.

An instant later, Xu Qing’s aura surged again. Astonishingly, he advanced from late Quasi-Immortal into the great circle! This was also called... peak Quasi-Immortal!

And there was still more to come! He pushed past the limit of that cultivation level, rising higher, to a level no one had reached in the past. Terrifying pressure erupted from Xu Qing, pushing out with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force that could crush everything.

This was energy that, from ancient times until now, surpassed anything a peak Quasi-Immortal could do. In fact, there were even some Summer Immortals whose auras could not compare to this! This was what happened when Xu Qing... unleashed everything he had accumulated!

A dazzling silver light shone! That was the color of the Summer Immortals, and it flowed around him, gathering in his eyes until they were pure silver!

He had silver eyes and violet hair.... His cultivation base was not that of an immortal, and yet, it already surpassed that of an immortal!

All he lacked was the tenth extreme! It was canon turning into law! All Xu Qing had to do was gain enlightenment, and his cultivation base would break through, and he would step into the ranks of the Summer Immortals!

And he had already determined that when that day came, he would return to Revered Ancient! The good fortune caused his heart to swell.

Taking a deep breath, he sensed the terrifying fluctuations within him. He knew what path he would follow going forward. Looking up at Young Lord Aurora, he clasped hands and bowed very deeply!

Young Lord Aurora looked down, his eyes twinkling with joy at the sight of Xu Qing’s breakthrough. He laughed heartily. And then, having no reservations whatsoever, he... cut the final karma thread connecting him to godhood! It was no longer connected to him.

The aura of an Immortal Lord erupted with no hindrances. The Fourth Star Ring trembled, and the Fifth Star Ring cheered with joy!

He was now completely back to being human! Hē had thoroughly returned to being he! He had transformed from immortal to god, become a God Lord, and then switched back to the dao of immortals.

In that manner, the Fifth Star Ring... got a new Immortal Lord!

Immortal Lord Mi Ming!

At the same time, though it seemed like his connection to the Fourth Star Ring had been completely severed, the reality was that it still existed. His name, which contained both the sun and moon, would forever be part of the river of true names there.

As a result, Immortal Lord Mi Ming would be like a nail plunged deeply into the natural laws of the Fourth Star Ring! It wasn’t something that could easily be tampered with. It was as if he had left his canon behind there for all eternity.

He was the first person in the Fifth Star Ring to have the blessing of that star ring’s destiny aura, while at the same time, capable of stirring the dao of gods in the Fourth Star Ring.

He... was the most powerful Immortal Lord in two star rings! It was no exaggeration to say that he was half a step into the Immortal Paragon level!

In countless universes in the Fourth Star Ring, living beings trembled. Even gods shook in the depths of their god souls.

Only a day had passed since Young Lord Aurora arrived on the primeval motherworld. But the events which had played out were astonishing. They were like an unrivaled tempest, the effects of which spread through the entire Fourth Star Ring. Temples collapsed. Gods withered. God kingdoms fell into ruin. Even god dynasties were swept up in the violence. The very foundation of the Fourth Star Ring was shaken!

That wasn’t even to mention that Young Lord Aurora’s true name was now forever a part of the Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods, bringing with it the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring. That made the blow to the foundation even greater.

It was easy to imagine what would happen going forward. The Fourth Star Ring’s dao of gods wouldn’t be as pure. The resurrection ability of the gods would be obstructed. And even more terrifying... immortal energy could very well appear within the Fourth Star Ring! The gods would then feel pressure to survive both from inside and outside.

And there was another critical point. That was... that the God Paragon had abandoned the Fourth Star Ring and just left! Hē had given up on all the other gods in the Fourth Star Ring. Hē had taken advantage of thēir crisis, ensuring that hē would face no repercussions for choosing to enter the Living God Umbilical Cord.

Those actions were a huge blow to the gods of the Fourth Star Ring. Moans of grief swept out from the dao of gods and into the souls of all gods left behind in the Fourth Star Ring. It remained in place for a long time before fading away.

It was quite a contrast to the Fifth Star Ring. The destiny aura seethed as Young Lord Aurora achieved his breakthrough and returned. However poorly the Fourth Star Ring was faring because of the invasion, the living beings of the Fifth Star Ring were benefiting. In fact, the effects were more pronounced as the destiny aura grew stronger. Cheering filled the star ring.

Because of this incident, it was correct to say that the war was about ninety percent over. The end was in sight.

And the results... were astounding! Whether in terms of absolute power levels, or from the perspective of the star rings overall, there was no doubt that the Fourth Star Ring would have trouble turning things around. In fact, the Fourth Star Ring seemed to be doomed to have its fate devoured.

Now thēy were facing a countdown! That was because the Immortal Paragon had issued new orders. The Immortal Lords who had entered the Fourth Star Ring were to go all out to fight the God Lords.

With the wave of a hand, the Immortal Paragon opened up a host of huge teleportation portals all over the Fourth Star Ring. Armies of cultivators poured out of them and attacked the Fourth Star Ring forces! What seemed to be a very one-sided battle began to rage.

Standing there on the primeval motherworld, Young Lord Aurora could sense what was happening. Seeing that matters had essentially been decided, he reached up and plunged his hand into his own chest.

Grabbing the godhood that was now cut free of karma threads, he dragged it out. Silver blood sprayed out as the godhood... emerged from Young Lord Aurora. The moment he pulled it out, heaven and earth trembled, and a will of fate appeared clearly on the godhood.

Young Lord Aurora had no desire to keep it. He knew that the karma was not something he could sustain. According to the Immortal Paragon... there were only two people in existence who could bear that karma.

One of them was Xu Qing. The other had supposedly been set to arrive in the middle of the breakthrough process, at least according to the Immortal Paragon’s plan. But for some unknown reason, that second person was nowhere to be seen.

“Ah whatever....” Young Lord Aurora looked at Xu Qing. “Xu Qing, this thing has benefits and detriments! You surely understand its background. As long as that being has not perished, no god or human in the higher star rings can truly own it.

“Regardless, you can consider it a precious treasure! You can make your own decision about whether or not... to take this second gift!”

Xu Qing looked at the godhood in Young Lord Aurora’s hands. He could sense the strong connection between himself and it. Put precisely, it was actually connected to his god clone.

Therefore, he didn’t hesitate. He nodded.

Young Lord Aurora waved his hand, sending the godhood toward Xu Qing in a blur of prismatic light.

Xu Qing caught it. The moment he did, his mind spun, and he could clearly sense the fluctuations of the godhood. And he could sense the incomparably terrifying power within it. It was as if... he was holding an entire star ring in his hand.

“My god clone back in Revered Ancient should be able to contain this godhood....” Xu Qing took a deep breath and put the godhood away. Then he looked around. He knew that his time in this place was coming to an end.

“In that case,” Young Lord Aurora said softly, “do you want to fight in the war here in the Fourth Star Ring? Or would you like to come with me? Or is there somewhere else you’d like to go? I can send you wherever you want.”

Xu Qing thought for a moment. “I want to go back to the eastern theater in the Fifth Star Ring.”

He had not forgotten about the Fifth Ring Immortal Pill that Immortal Lord Deepgloom had promised to give him. He was now a peak Quasi-Immortal, but he lacked enlightenment of canon. That said... he still wanted that Fifth Ring Immortal Pill. He wanted to give it to Plumdark.

Young Lord Aurora waved his hand, causing ripples to spread through the void. Destiny aura converged, creating a vortex.

Young Lord Aurora smiled. “In that case, see you in the Fifth Star Ring.”

Xu Qing nodded. He bowed to Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix, then looked around wistfully one last time. Many images floated up in his mind, but in the end, he suppressed them all, leaving behind only his fixation on becoming a Summer Immortal. With that, he shot into the vortex. He disappeared inside, leaving the primeval motherworld.

After he was gone, Young Lord Aurora looked at Spirit Phoenix. He smiled warmly. “Sorry I put you through so much anxiety....”

Eyes puffy and red, Immortal Fairy Spirit Phoenix floated up to Young Lord Aurora’s side. “We have one more thing to do. Then we can settle down.”

Smiling faintly, Young Lord Aurora clasped her hand and turned. Together, they disappeared into the void.

***

Elsewhere in the Fourth Star Ring, the pocket realm Xu Qing had visited was now nothing but ruins. When Young Lord Aurora achieved his breakthrough and changed his dao, this place had been affected just like the rest of the star ring.

It was little more than rubble. The sky had been torn open, and looked like it wouldn’t stay intact much longer.

Two corpses could be seen on the ground. One was a black tumor, rotting and full of filth. The other was the local god who actually looked human. Hē was not rotting, but rather, was slowly dissipating as if by some process of purification. As the corpse dissipated, someone crawled out from inside.

Sheesh, I barely got half full! Why’s it dissipating all of a sudden? Well, I am a badass. I risked everything to unleash my Heaven-Devouring Earth-Consuming Reverse-Ancient Super-God Incantation. At least I got to eat a bit before this thing dissipated.

Hmmmphh! It’s not like I didn’t notice that teleportation portal pop into being next to me all of a sudden. It was very enticing, as if it was trying to lure me inside. It was obvious what was happening. This god knew it didn’t want me eating it, so it was trying to trick me into leaving! But I, Erniu, am not that kind of person! I cannot be fooled, fool!

His clothes were in tatters, and he looked very bedraggled. He was none other than Erniu. Despite looking to be in bad condition, his belly bulged out as if he had just eaten a big meal.

After crawling out into the open, he looked around. When he saw the world around him, his jaw nearly dropped. He even gasped in surprise.

What happened out here? The aura is in chaos! Why does it seem like a war broke out...? What’s going on...? Holy crap! Did I miss something? Did something incredible happen?

A moment later, Erniu’s eyes sparkled, and he slapped his thigh excitedly.

If a war broke out in this damned place, that would be a good thing! That would mean gods died! Don’t tell me that I’ve finally experienced some heaven-defying good luck! Can I finally get full?

Erniu licked his lips in anticipation.

The eastern theater of the Fifth Star Ring was very far away from Xu Qing, and it was currently very empty. Roughly seventy percent of the cultivator army had been ordered by the Immortal Paragon to invade the Fourth Star Ring for the final battle.

Those left behind were tasked with the important mission of maintaining planets that were designated as supply depots. There were many such planets stretching between the eastern theater and the Fourth Star Ring. Just about every other universe had at least one.

Their purpose was to provide supplies to the front lines and also offer healing services to injured members of the army. They were so full of immortal energy that they were almost like immortal towers. And they weren’t just on the side of the Fifth Star Ring. They extended through the various theaters all the way into the Fourth Star Ring.

The cultivator army pushed the front lines deeper and deeper into the Fourth Star Ring, and the supply depot planets went with them, going deeper and branching out as necessary. It made sense considering that the battlefield encompassed countless universes, and the cultivators’ goal was complete domination of enemy territory. Given that, it couldn’t be understated how important logistics were. And thus, these planets were like game pieces on a game board, which the cultivators put in place to stabilize the battlefield.

In the middle section of the Fifth Star Ring’s eastern theater, there was a supply depot planet that was pure yellow. It hung in space surrounded by rings of rubble, atop which many cultivators were stationed.

The planet’s surface was covered with mountain ranges and vast deserts filled with yellow sand, each grain of which could provide a baptism of immortal energy. There were many cultivators on the surface as well, all of them tasked with various duties relating to logistics.

This was a very important planet, as it was the very first supply depot planet that had been put into service at the beginning of the full-scale war. It was the starting point of the chain of supply depot planets that ultimately stretched into the Fourth Star Ring.

This planet also had a lot of teleportation portals. There were big ones and small ones, and they operated nonstop day and night, funneling massive amounts of supplies out of the Fifth Star Ring and to the front lines. That was the primary mission of this supply depot planet.

Because the planet was so important, the teleportation portals there were connected to subsequent supply depot planets. However, given the wartime situation, they only performed outgoing teleportations, and would not accept returning teleportations. Wounded cultivators had to abide by that arrangement, and could only seek treatment on other supply depot planets. freewebnovel.com

In order to ensure the defenses were as strong as possible, there was a huge contingent from the army stationed there, and Immortal Lord Deepgloom had even left a clone in charge. All such arrangements were to ensure that supplies could get to the front lines safely.

As countless cultivators hurried about their work, a strange rumbling suddenly filled the air and multi-colored light flowed through the dome of heaven.

Large numbers of cultivators shivered and sent their divine will out to check what was happening. The streams of divine will soon came to focus on the source of the strange phenomenon.

It was a teleportation portal! And it was lighting up!

The fluctuations were noticed first by the cultivators in charge of that portal. Except, they hadn’t activated the portal. And this wasn’t a case of the portal being used to send supplies out. Instead....

After checking the incoming teleportation, one of the cultivators said, “It’s coming from the Fourth Star Ring. There’s a living person coming through, on the order of... an Immortal Lord!”

The information was immediately relayed up the chain of command. Even as the unusual event was reported, the glow from the teleportation portal grew brighter, becoming a dazzling display that shook all the lands in sight.

Then a massive vortex appeared in the sky. As countless people looked on, a figure materialized there. He wore a black daoist robe, and had violet hair. His eyes were silver. The terrifying aura that he emitted, even in the midst of teleportation, caused heaven and earth to tremble. The converged divine will from all the cultivators also shook.

He was none other than Xu Qing! As he stepped out of the vortex, winds screamed and the air vibrated. The unique immortal starlight of the Fifth Star Ring spread over him like tide waters.

As he hovered in the air, the empyrean winds caused his robe to flap. Stellar debris whipped about around him like a silver river.

He was the center of all attention! The destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring swirled around him, converging into a violet energy. It was almost like he was being welcomed back by the destiny aura itself.

The feeling of the familiar immortal starlight, destiny aura, and immortal will left Xu Qing feeling a bit dazed. He hadn’t been gone for very long, but so much had happened that he felt like a lifetime had passed.

Back when things went awry between Immortal Lord Deepgloom and God Lord Death Departure, Xu Qing had been a mid Quasi-Immortal. He had fled for his life, explored the primeval motherworld, helped Young Lord Aurora change his dao, and upgraded his own cultivation base. Now... he was a peak Quasi-Immortal! That type of change in cultivation base was huge.

As Xu Qing thought back to everything, he couldn’t help but sigh in his heart.

At the moment, bells were tolling on this, the original supply depot planet. They interrupted Xu Qing’s thoughts. As the bells tolled, some of the cultivators assigned to the area appeared outside the teleportation portal. They included men and women, and they were from different universes in the Fifth Star Ring. But all of them instantly recognized who Xu Qing was.

“It’s Xu Qing!”

All of them were visibly shaken, and they quickly clasped hands and bowed to him.

“We offer respectful greetings, True Monarch!”

Voices rang out in all directions, and they were full of deep respect! After all, everyone had been made aware of the events on the primeval motherworld almost in real time. It had been sent to everyone through the destiny aura.

Xu Qing looked around, then suddenly shifted his gaze up. Clasping hands, he bowed at the waist. As he did, nine crimson suns appeared through the clouds as Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s clone revealed himself. Magnificent dao reverberations filled the sky.

“Xu Qing!” he said.

A pill appeared in front of Xu Qing that swirled with nine-colored light. Within it was a vortex made of millions upon millions of pieces of stellar rubble, as well as an aura very close to that of a Summer Immortal.

“Fifth Star Ring Immortal Pill,” Xu Qing murmured. This pill was the main reason he had come back.

The Fifth Star Ring Immortal Pill could only be used by someone who had been blessed with destiny aura. If he wanted to give it to another person, it would require that person to be connected to the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring. However... Xu Qing could get around that. Because he had Fifth Star Ring destiny aura, he could share the pill’s potent medicinal effects with someone else.

There were other considerations. After he got back to Revered Ancient and gave it to someone else to use, he wanted to see if the Revered Ancient destiny aura could produce similar effects. With such thoughts in mind, he reached out and took the Fifth Star Ring Immortal Pill.

Meanwhile, Immortal Lord Deepgloom’s clone noted the silver glow in Xu Qing’s pupils.

“Normally speaking, this pill would be a gift given to you much later. But the karma of the Aurora Epoch caused the timeline to advance.”

Xu Qing nodded. “Many thanks, Immortal Lord! If there are no other matters at hand, your humble servant would like to leave the eastern theater and return to the heaven beyond heaven to seek enlightenment and attempt a breakthrough.”

Immortal Lord Deepgloom looked deeply at Xu Qing. “I suggest that you stay here for a while to rest and recuperate. After all... an old friend of yours would like to see you.”

Xu Qing could think of a number of people he might be referring to, but wasn’t sure which one. “Immortal Lord, which old friend wants to see me?”

“Immortal Lord Dark Alchemist! He has countless incarnations, which he sends out to all the star rings to seek the will of the dao. He has sent incarnations to the Ninth Star Ring as well. You probably knew him as... Grandmaster Bai. At the moment, he’s on the battlefield in the Fourth Star Ring, where he’s hoping to confirm something for you.”[1]

When Immortal Lord Deepgloom said ‘Grandmaster Bai,’ the name hit Xu Qing with the power to dry up rivers and drain seas. He suddenly found it difficult to keep his breathing steady.

Deep inside, Xu Qing was both sentimental and loyal. Whether it was Sergeant Thunder, Grandmaster Bai, or his Master, there were certain people who held a place in his heart that could never be replaced. All of sudden, he found himself thinking back to what Grandmaster Bai had said to him when they parted, so long ago.

“The world is a tavern for living beings. And the timescape is an old guest. As long as we don’t die, we’ll meet again....”

The voice drifted through his memories, and images popped up in his mind. He thought back to learning about plants and vegetation in the scavenger basecamp. He thought about the sorrow he felt when he visited the grave in the Violet Lands. He thought about that mysterious old man with the medicinal decocting pot that he had seen in the Aurora Immortal Palace.

“We’ll meet again...” Xu Qing murmured.

He chose to wait for Grandmaster Bai. At the same time, he worked on stabilizing his cultivation base to make sure he was in a peak state. He also tried to organize his scattered thoughts regarding the tenth extreme.

Time passed. Before he knew it, it was a month later.

Although Grandmaster Bai did not return during that time, there was a piece of news that excited the whole Fifth Star Ring. It was a report about the war!

The Fifth Star Ring’s army was smashing through the gods like a boulder crushing a drinking glass. Forty percent of the Fourth Star Ring was already occupied, and resources had been seized from countless universes.

After being abandoned by the God Paragon, the God Lords of the Fourth Star Ring were put into a deadly situation. Five of them had chosen to leave and go to other star rings. Three were confirmed to have perished! Of those three, two were slain by Immortal Lord Mi Ming, who suddenly appeared on the battlefield without any warning! The remainder were still trying to fight back, but were clearly in a hopeless situation.

As for God Lord Death Departure, he ended up losing in a fight to Immortal Lord Deepgloom, but used an innate ability to escape, and was now at large.

What was more, the Immortal Paragon had issued a new imperial decree! Immortal Lord Mi Ming was in command during this epoch, and as such, he would take over for Immortal Lord Deepgloom to lead the war effort.

It was an era belonging to cultivators... and the war would only bring further glory and honor!

1. Immortal Lord Dark Alchemist’s name contains the same character ‘dark’ that we see in Dark Serenity or Plumdark. The second character in the name is the word for a medicinal pot. I considered a variety of options, eliminating Dark Pot almost immediately lol, and ultimately (for a variety of reasons) settled on this option for the translation choice. ☜

A new era really had begun the moment Immortal Lord Nineshores stepped down.

Immortal Lord Mi Ming’s rise to prominence had already been transmitted back to the Fifth Star Ring by means of destiny aura. He carried on the legacy of his father Aurora, taking command of the Fifth Star Ring and becoming its leader. He now had incredibly high status.

And now... his performance on the battlefield in the Fourth Star Ring was outstanding. He had killed two God Lords and had taken control over the army! It caused a swell in destiny aura, and filled innumerable Fifth Star Ring cultivators with extreme excitement. Cheering could be heard on all of the supply depot planets.

At the same time, Xu Qing’s status also increased. He was the master of the Aurora heaven beyond heaven, and he had a very special relationship with Mi Ming. He had helped Mi Ming to change his dao to that of the gods, then back to that of an immortal. What was more, he had been the subject of Mi Ming’s very first imperial decree as an Immortal Lord, and had been blessed by destiny aura.

As a result, everyone in the Fifth Star Ring had heard the story... of Xu Qing, the person who Immortal Lord Mi Ming viewed as a younger brother.

True Monarch Xu Qing was going to be an extremely important person in the epoch to come in the Fifth Star Ring. The status, position, and destiny aura involved... left people who had gotten into conflicts with Xu Qing, whether directly or indirectly, shaking in fear.

One person who felt especially uneasy was Li Mengtu’s Master, Poison Monarch! He was also in the Fourth Star Ring at the moment. He had just finished a fight to the death with a True God, and he had won. He was currently seated cross-legged on a gray asteroid.[1]

Seated cross-legged around him were his subordinates. If Xu Qing were present, he would recognize those subordinates. They were the very same squadron that he had clashed with early on. There were fewer of them now. All the survivors were injured in some way, and they looked exhausted.

None of them were speaking any more than Poison Monarch was speaking. Occasionally, some of them looked like they wanted to say something to Poison Monarch, but in the end, none did.[2]

Poison Monarch didn’t look back at them. However, given the level of his cultivation base, he knew exactly what was going on. He felt just as bitter as them.

In the past, he had been able to avoid coming to the front lines. But orders had come through just a few days ago from the Fourth Star Ring, ordering him into service. The orders didn’t come directly from Immortal Lord Mi Ming. But they came from the Tower of War Affairs, so he couldn’t ignore them. Someone there had arranged for him and some of his subordinates to come to the Fourth Star Ring to carry out a specific mission.

Poison Monarch had speculations about who had issued the orders. Not that it mattered. In the end, there would always be someone willing to suck up to important people, and then use war powers to achieve their own ends.

You sucked up to Xu Qing, didn’t you...?

Poison Monarch’s bitterness grew deeper. If he had been assigned to ordinary war duty, he wouldn’t have been so bitter. But he had been given a very brutal mission.

He had been ordered to kill nine True Gods as strong as himself! In the days that had passed since he started the mission, he had only killed one![3]

A lot of people know about my history with Xu Qing.... Is that why this is happening? I had hoped to take his dao to benefit myself. It didn’t work, but the karma was sown. And now... I’m facing the backlash.

When Poison Monarch thought about the past, he felt a sense of defiance, but at the same time, got the feeling this was all fate. He felt like he had watched Xu Qing just get stronger and stronger, until now, when someone had sucked up to him to launch an attack on Poison Monarch himself. Having reached this point in his train of thought, Poison Monarch sighed.

The clone I sent should be arriving right about now. Hopefully, he can resolve this karma.

Shaking his head, he looked in the direction of the Fifth Star Ring.

***

In the Fifth Star Ring, a dilapidated figure had just appeared outside the yellow supply depot planet where Xu Qing was staying. He was an old man surrounded by a dark green cloud of poison. His facial features were exactly the same as Poison Monarch, and his aura matched as well.

He was a clone sent by Poison Monarch. Clearly he had run into stiff opposition on his way here, as he was severely injured. Within the cloud of dark green poison, he looked withered, and his canon emanated a sense of rot. His left arm had been severed at the shoulder, and the flesh around the wound wriggled.

The clone looked hesitantly at the supply depot planet, then gritted his teeth and flew forward. He had made contact with a friend on the planet ahead of time, but still had to go through a screening process. It was several hours later before he arrived at a stargazing tower in the southeast.

The tower was a pagoda made from a meteorite, constructed atop a mountain, and the area was full of strong immortal energy. This was where Xu Qing was staying.

Upon arriving, his friend stopped in place, and even took a step back. “You’re on your own from this point forward, Poison Monarch.”

The friend was an army officer stationed on the planet. After hearing about the matter between Poison Monarch and Xu Qing, and given that he owed a favor, he had helped out. But he wasn’t willing to do more than escort Poison Monarch to this location.

Poison Monarch nodded in response. And with that, he made his way up toward the stargazing tower. He stopped about 300 meters away from the pagoda. Without the slightest hesitation, he bowed deeply and said, “I’m an old friend. May I have an audience with the True Monarch?”

Despite how his voice rang out, there was no response from the pagoda.

A short time passed. Poison Monarch’s clone sighed. Then he produced a palm-sized bronze doll, held it out in front of him, and put it on the ground. The bronze doll looked exactly like Poison Monarch, and it even had a dark green heart pumping in its chest cavity.

Poison Monarch looked at the doll with determination in his eyes. Then used the nail of his finger to slash open his neck. Blood sprayed out, sizzling through the air before landing on the doll. The doll started moving. At the same time, the clone started to fade away.

Bowing once more to the tower, he said, “My true form is in the Fourth Star Ring, on a mission to kill nine True Gods as strong as myself. Because of that, I can’t come in person. In my stead, I’ve sent this tribulation-substitution doll. Activate the doll, and my true form will be teleported into your presence to fight for you. Whether I live or die, it will resolve the karma I sowed by trying to take your dao.”

As the voice echoed out, the clone disappeared. There was never any response from the tower. Off in the distance, the officer who had escorted Poison Monarch to this location sighed, bowed, and then left.

Sometime later... the bronze doll blurred and disappeared. When it reappeared, it was inside the tower in Xu Qing’s hand. He looked expressionlessly at it for a time.

If I use this, the karma will be resolved. If I don’t, the karma will remain. Everything depends on your fate.

***

Back in the Fourth Star Ring, Poison Monarch’s true form grunted. About fifty percent of the karma threads connecting him to Xu Qing had already snapped. Upon sensing that, Poison Monarch sighed again. He had always looked like an old farmer, but now, he looked even older than before.

I should never have made a move on him in the first place. I should never have coveted his dao....

1. Poison Monarch was introduced in chapter 1120. He was mentioned in quite a few other chapters as well, sometimes as Poison Monarch or sometimes just as Li Mengtu’s Master. I believe the last time he was mentioned by name was in chapter 1246. ☜

2. The main clash occurred in chapter 1205, although the people involved were introduced a few chapters before that in 1201. ☜

3. To provide some context, chapter 1202 gave some broader information about what it means to kill True Gods. When Xu Qing visited the Heroic Immortal Tombs, one of the stone steles had an epitaph in which the buried hero mentioned being proud of having killed seven True Gods, while another lamented about not being able to kill any. So being ordered to kill nine is obviously a very difficult task. ☜

Xu Qing had not forgotten about the situation with Poison Monarch, no matter what events had played out recently. That was just Xu Qing’s personality. Originally, he had planned to gain enlightenment of the tenth extreme, and thoroughly step into the Summer Immortal level. And then, before he left the Fifth Star Ring... he had planned to kill Poison Monarch!

Although it was true that Poison Monarch had failed to take Xu Qing’s dao, the fact remained that karma had been sown. But then the man had sent a clone to him, and had offered him the bronze doll.... Xu Qing looked at the doll in his palm.

Before picking it up, he had inspected it thoroughly. Now, he used destiny aura to seal it before putting it away.

Right now, the most important thing is my reunion with Grandmaster Bai....

Putting aside the issue of Poison Monarch, Xu Qing looked up into the starry sky above. Just barely... he could sense something stirring in his mind.

He’s coming....

Xu Qing stood and walked out of the stargazing tower. The starry sky above seemed to spin as a ray of light descended from beyond heaven. It was like a starry river pouring down, sending ripples through the surrounding nebulae. The light eventually reached the surface of the planet, becoming like a waterfall. It looked almost like an ink painting came to life.

The faint aroma of plants and vegetation spread out, filled with canon and magical laws. Along with it came a sound like an ethereal zither, playing an ancient melody that resembled the rustle of young plants growing. It was profound and extraordinary to the extreme. Then a figure appeared within the ink painting.

He stepped out. He was an old man. He wore a robe as white as the moon, embroidered with decorations that resembled plants and vegetation. Tied to his waist was a medicinal decocting pot. He had chiseled features, but at the same time, the way his eyebrows framed his eyes made him seem very compassionate.

His eyes were as profound as deep pools of water, and his pupils were like vortexes made of stellar nebulae. Occasionally, they would flicker with starlight, as though a river of stars existed deep inside. He was surrounded by lingering violet energy that seemed like the materialization of a spirit meridian that had existed since the beginning of heaven and earth.

He was smiling as he looked down at Xu Qing.

“You’ve grown up.” His voice was as clear as spring waters flowing over jade.

The voice caused endless memories to stir within Xu Qing. Images of the past flitted through his mind. Xu Qing’s eyes were red as he clasped hands and bowed.

“Teacher....”

The simple form of address, and all the memories, contained emotions that made Grandmaster Bai’s gaze seem even more kind and gentle than before.

“Let’s take a walk,” Grandmaster Bai said softly. He waved his hand, and starlight descended, making a path that stretched out between them.

Xu Qing took a deep breath. Heart brimming with respect, he stepped onto the starry path and walked up to Grandmaster Bai. Then, they went into the starry sky together. After leaving the supply depot planet, they strolled through the boundless universe.

“Tell me everything that happened after you joined Seven Blood Eyes,” Grandmaster Bai said.

Xu Qing nodded as he thought back to the past. “Well, after I got into Seven Blood Eyes, I became a disciple of the Seventh Peak....”

Xu Qing’s story became like images reflected in Grandmaster Bai’s eyes. He talked about the Grand Competition at the Merfolk Isles, and the Seazombie war, and the migration to the Revered Ancient mainland.... Eventually he joined the swordsages... and of course, there was everything that happened in Sea-Sealing County. Then there was Crimson Mother, Empress Summer Departure, and Grand Emperor Swordsage....

***

Grandmaster Bai led the way through the starry sky. Xu Qing walked to his right, half a pace behind him.

It was just like years ago in the scavenger basecamp. Back then, Xu Qing had been called the Kid. In the hopes of finding a lifespan flower for Sergeant Thunder, he had sought help from Grandmaster Bai. Eventually, he started eavesdropping on lessons outside the tent, which was how he started learning about plants and vegetation. Eventually, he had been called into the tent, and his formal education had begun.

Something similar was happening now. As they traversed the starry sky, green lotuses seemed to bloom beneath Grandmaster Bai’s feet. Every universe they passed through, every planet they encountered, flourished with greenery. There were some desolate planets where plants began to sprout in the cracked and parched soil. New life was being born.

Xu Qing wasn’t even sure how much time passed as he recounted everything he had experienced in Revered Ancient.

Finally, Grandmaster Bai sighed. “In the past, the Ninth Star Ring wasn’t very special compared to other star rings.... But then Eminent Desolation failed to rise to the Living God level. Hē was the first one to ever return from the Living God Umbilical Cord, and afterward, hē went to the Ninth Star Ring. That was where hē stayed, at the Revered Ancient mainland.

“From that moment on, entities with paramount personhood from all the star rings focused on Revered Ancient. No one knows why Eminent Desolation went there.

“In the past, God Paragons from other star rings went to the Ninth Star Ring in the hopes of finding out more about Eminent Desolation. However, anyone who got close had a difficult time avoiding death.... Though some did find destined opportunities, few could escape the resulting karma. The God Paragon of the Fourth Star Ring is a good example.... Apparently, only paragons native to the Ninth Star Ring, if they’re very careful, have a chance at success.[1]

“Some time ago, the Immortal Paragon entrusted me with a mission. By means of a special transmigration magic devoid of any unusual powers, I was transformed into a mortal, born on one of the islands off the coast of Revered Ancient. I did not have any memories of the past, and I could not take a single step off the island. It was only after I died that I recovered my memories of the past.

“Because of Eminent Desolation, Revered Ancient... is an inauspicious place. Are you sure... that you want to go back? If you want to stay here in the Fifth Star Ring, you’ll definitely become an Immortal Lord before long.” Grandmaster Bai looked at Xu Qing.

Xu Qing was silent for a long moment. “I have to go back, Teacher.”

Grandmaster Bai seemed like a wise old man who had come to understand the mortal world, as he said nothing. His face did seem slightly more wrinkled than before. However, the wrinkles didn’t come from the passage of time. They were like mountains and rivers that secretly contained something profound and ancient.

Eventually, he shook his head. “Before coming to see you, I confirmed something for you in the Fourth Star Ring. That... is where you can reach immortal ascension!”

Those words shook Xu Qing to the core.

Grandmaster Bai stopped in place in the starry sky. As soon as he did, all of the heavenly bodies in the surrounding universe seemed to respond to a call, and changed their orbits. As they swirled through the starry sky, they converged in front of Grandmaster Bai and Xu Qing in a specific sequence. It transformed into a majestic star chart that resembled a medicinal decocting pot!

Grandmaster Bai inclined his head in the direction of the Fourth Star Ring.

“Xu Qing,” he said softly, “I want to impart some knowledge to you. It has nothing to do with plants and vegetation. It has to do with the ‘beyond.’ The thirty-six higher star rings, and all the God Paragons therein, are considered ‘within.’ What thēy are pursuing... is in the beyond.[2]

“It’s not necessarily important to understand what the term means exactly. But you need to remember it... on that future day when you acquire the destined opportunity to rise from Immortal Lord to Immortal Paragon.

“As for right now.... If you want to gain enlightenment of a higher level of canon, you need to go to the Fourth Star Ring! You already ran into the god of pain, and descended into an illusion. In that illusion, you broke through, and lived a life of pain.

“Although it was an illusion, and false, it did contain some truth. And thus, why not go experience it for real? Let the reality really happen! Make the illusions truly false!”

Grandmaster Bai waved his sleeve, and the countless heavenly bodies within the decocting pot star chart shifted. They unleashed dazzling starlight, then converged into the shape of a very unique bridge. It led right into the Fourth Star Ring!

The bridge was made from starlight and spirit plants. It was difficult to tell if it was material or illusory, and was a true manifestation of the mysteries and majesty of nature. It was different from the god of pain’s illusion that contained truth, yet it did the same thing.

“Go,” Grandmaster Bai said. “I hope that when you return... you are a Summer Immortal!”

As Grandmaster Bai spoke, the special bridge shone with dazzling light.

Xu Qing took in the scene, his mind spinning. Memories of that illusory life he had lived filled his mind. A moment later, his eyes shone with determination.

After bowing to Grandmaster Bai, he walked onto the bridge. Striding atop the starlight and spirit plants, he headed in the direction of the Fourth Star Ring! As the bridge shimmered, Xu Qing slowly made his way off into the distance. The star chart spun, pulsing with a magnificent energy and immortal fire.

A moment later, Grandmaster Bai appeared atop the star chart, where he settled down cross-legged. Given the destiny aura he could utilize, and his cultivation level, he was doing everything possible to help Xu Qing on this journey. That was the karma of their relationship as teacher and student, which had begun back in Revered Ancient.

Off to the side, ripples spread through the void as an old man wearing hemp sandals appeared. He walked over to Grandmaster Bai and looked at Xu Qing disappearing in the distance. Perched on his shoulder was a golden rat who was munching on a sunflower seed.

Grandmaster Bai didn’t turn to look at him. He just coolly said, “So, Immortal Paragon, did you put that certain item in place like you were supposed to?”

The Immortal Paragon sighed. “You know I’m the Immortal Paragon, right?” he said. “What’s with the attitude?”

“You owe him!” Grandmaster Bai said calmly.

The Immortal Paragon shook his head. He had known Grandmaster Bai for many years, so he was obviously familiar with his personality. He also knew full well... that although Grandmaster Bai was an Immortal Lord, the truth was that he could have become an Immortal Paragon any time he wished. But for some unknown reason, he had held back from taking that final step.

Ignoring Grandmaster Bai’s tone, the Immortal Paragon sat down next to him. “I put it in place. I don’t want to be involved in the karma, but as you know, I couldn’t just let that thing go.”

Grandmaster Bai said nothing in response.

A short time passed, and then the Immortal Paragon continued, “You know, Xu Qing is getting help from you, and he’ll have that certain item from me. But that doesn’t mean he’s guaranteed to succeed. His canon is different from that of most other people.... Advancing it further will involve pushing it to the ‘statute’ level of Immortal Lords. That’s a big gap to cross, so it’s going to be extremely difficult. What will you do if he fails?”

The Immortal Paragon looked at Grandmaster Bai.

Grandmaster Bai said nothing for a long moment. “He won’t fail.”

The Immortal Paragon continued to look at him for a long moment. “Is he what Eminent Desolation is looking for? Or could it be... that he is actually a transmigrated version of Eminent Desolation??”

His words seemed to make the surrounding universe stop moving.

“You’ve been to Revered Ancient,” Grandmaster Bai said calmly. “If what you suggest is true, wouldn’t you be able to see it, given the level of your cultivation base? So what are you asking me for?”

1. Quick note here about “paragons.” I chose to use the word because it shares the character that I translated as ‘paragon’ in I Shall Seal the Heavens. However, that doesn’t necessarily mean that the paragons in this book are the same as the paragons in that book. Of course, I’m not definitively saying they aren’t the same. I’m just saying that the same character/word does not in itself definitely make a connection. In this paragraph, he uses that character in isolation when he talks about “paragons native to the Ninth Star Ring.” I think that was intentional. It seems to me that the implication is that it could be an Immortal Paragon or a God Paragon native to the Ninth Star Ring. When used in conjunction with Immortal/God, I’ll capitalized paragon as part of the name of the cultivation level, but when used in a standalone way, I won’t capitalize it. ☜

2. Yes, the ‘beyond’ mentioned here is a reference to the title of the novel. ☜

The war still raged in the Fourth Star Ring.

At the moment, a relatively small-scale battle had broken out in one of the large universes there. On the cultivator side was the Spiritheaven Legion from the Fifth Star Ring’s western theater, who were responsible for establishing order in this place, the Manythousands Universe.

They were fighting some Godfolk who were native to the Manythousands Universe. In the past, those gods had been very powerful and influential, with more than ten True Gods. But the main forces from the Fifth Star Ring had killed almost all of those True Gods, thus throwing the rest of the gods into chaos. There were now only a few lingering resistance fighters who had somehow escaped in the chaos.

But the Spiritheaven Legion had tracked them down, and were now attempting to wipe them out. Unfortunately... though the Fifth Star Ring had the upper hand in the war, that didn’t mean that they won every single battle. Unexpected things still happened. That said, those unexpected events usually happened on a small scale, so the overall war wasn’t affected.

Right now, an unexpected situation had developed in this cleanup effort. These Godfolk actually had two True Gods hidden within thēir ranks! Unfortunately, the Spiritheaven Legion only had a single Summer Immortal, and thus, the presence of two True Gods put them in a bad position. Both sides were suffering from heavy casualties.

Of the roughly 100,000 cultivators that made up the army, most were injured in some way. The Summer Immortal leader was doing her best against the two True Gods, but was reaching the limits of exhaustion.

What was worse, the gods had sealed the area with special warding spells that prevented any shock waves from escaping the battlefield. Similarly, divine will was blocked off. As a result, the cultivators couldn’t send distress messages. If the gods won, it wouldn’t change the war situation overall. Eventually, other cultivator forces would arrive and wipe them out.

But the Spiritheaven Legion... were fighting for their lives.

I’m not going to make it out of this... thought the Summer Immortal. She wore a suit of dao armor, and was very pretty. At the same time, she was clearly a valiant, formidable, and accomplished killer.
