She was not from the older generation of Summer Immortals, but rather, had achieved her breakthrough only about a hundred years in the past. Her dao armor was in tatters, and her face was pale. Her injuries were quite serious, and she was completely pinned down by the two True Gods.

The two True Gods were extremely gruish.

One of them was 30,000 meters tall, and resembled a huge snake. Astonishingly, īts body was made of a host of god skulls, making īt seem like it was an emissary of death. Every move īt made caused mutagen to spread out in all directions, and īt pulsed with a godhood of death.

The other god was a wriggling ball of flesh covered in a slimy fluid. The slime īt produced was extremely poisonous, and rained down into the starry sky until it formed a spinning vortex. Within the vortex was a sea of black plum flowers with human faces on them. It was a truly horrendous sight.

The bleeding Summer Immortal unleashed her canon, allowing her to just barely defend herself against the two True Gods. She also managed to back up a bit. Her subordinates were in a desperate situation, and the gods were fighting like mad. The universe was completely locked down by the gods’ magic. However, her eyes shone with determination.

She lifted her right hand, and her cultivation base ignited, sending out pressure that could exterminate gods. The power of a Summer Immortal surged. Shock waves rolled through the universe, and the starry sky trembled.

The two True Gods quickly backed away. Thēy were not in peak condition either. Although thēy had escaped with thēir lives before, thēy had both sustained serious injuries.

As the gods fell back, the Summer Immortal didn’t hesitate for an instant. Silver light surrounded her as she severed her own right arm, then ignited the flesh and blood to refine the bone within it. Then she poured all of her Summer Immortal power into that bone, including all of her canon, causing it to become a silver crescent moon that sliced through the void in front of her.

She was going all out, infusing her own bone with canon in the hopes of creating an opening that would allow her to send out a call for help. That... was their only hope.

The bone, transformed into a silver crescent moon, was just on the verge of slicing out into the open. But then, the True God made of skulls flashed into motion and appeared right in front of it.

With a grim, ruthless expression, the god opened īts mouth and devoured the silver moon. Rumbling sounds filled the god, and then countless skulls shattered. However, īt refused to vomit up the crescent moon. By sacrificing īts own body, īt destroyed the canon in the silver moon, and foiled the Summer Immortal’s plan to call for help.

Seeing that, she sighed inwardly and prepared to take further decisive action. But then....

The fragrance of plants and vegetation suddenly filled the universe.

All of the cultivators noticed instantly. So did the gods, whose hearts pounded in fear. The two True Gods were stunned, and the Summer Immortal looked into the void toward the source of it. Ripples flowed out, causing all obstacles and warding spells to become incredibly weak. Many even collapsed. Then, a bridge made of starlight and spirit plants appeared, descending toward the universe.

The scene caused an instant stir among all living beings present on the battlefield. Given the fact that the bridge was emanating a very strong immortal energy, the cultivators were obviously excited.

The gods, meanwhile, were horrified.

What was especially eye-catching... was the person on the bridge. As he strode forward on the bridge, he emanated a terrifying pressure, as well as an astonishing aura. And then his facial features became clear to the cultivators below. Everyone recognized him instantly!

“True Monarch Xu Qing!!”

The Summer Immortal didn’t just recognize him. She could sense the power of an Immortal Lord, and could feel the strong destiny aura that accompanied Xu Qing.

The two True Gods didn’t hesitate for an instant. Thēy immediately fled! Thēy didn’t recognize Xu Qing, but thēy could sense that the person on the bridge was terrifying, and emanated a very fiendish aura. It was the type of aura that someone would develop after slaughtering many, many gods! Although thēy could sense that this person wasn’t a Summer Immortal, that fiendish aura and the bridge made it clear that this was not someone to trifle with. freewebnovel.com

Most importantly of all, thēir warding spells had been broken, revealing thēir position.

As they fled, Xu Qing’s eyes glittered with cold light, and he took a step forward. The bridge extended with him as he walked. The starry sky shattered, and the void trembled.

Terrifying power surged forth, arriving right in front of the True God made of god skulls. The bridge came with it, and it rushed right toward the True God.

The True God’s mind collapsed as an unprecedented sensation of deadly crisis filled īt. The god screamed and tried to fall back. Īt unleashed īts godly authority, even resorting to withering up īts own body and tapping into īts godhood. But no attempt to flee did any good.

It wasn’t because of Xu Qing’s power. It was because Xu Qing was tapping into the disappearing bridge to launch a deadly attack. He was borrowing the might of an Immortal Lord!

Nothing could stop that power from slamming into the True God. Rumbling sounds echoed out as the True God shivered from head to toe, then began collapsing. The god... was destroyed in body and soul!

The bridge, having accomplished its mission of sending Xu Qing to this place, dissipated into motes of silver light.

Xu Qing’s cultivation base erupted, unleashing peak Quasi-Immortal power. Countless overlapping space-times then appeared, turning into innumerable parallel universes. It was like a myriad of immortals appearing and moving in unison.

And they were moving right toward the final True God!

The True God whose form was that of a slimy ball of flesh and blood immediately started writhing in response to the scene that was playing out. The god seemed just on the verge of piercing through the void and making an escape.

But then the Summer Immortal blurred into motion as she pursued the True God. She moved, waving her left hand, and her entire body surged with silver light as she unleashed her Summer Immortal power to foil the god’s escape. The True God lurched to a halt.

“Xu Qing, let’s join forces. We—”

Before the Summer Immortal could finish speaking, Xu Qing waved his hand, causing a fingernail to fly forth. The moment the fingernail appeared, a terrifying force swept out. The starry sky rippled. The void shattered. And though the power was not on the same level as the bridge from before, it still shook everything.

It was the dao weapon![1]

It instantly sucked in the space-time projections behind Xu Qing and combined them, resulting in a beam of light made of both gold and silver. It pierced through the void toward the True God, moving with such incredible speed that it arrived almost instantly.

The True God trembled, īts flesh and blood started collapsing, īts poison vanished, and the sea of plums became part of the void. The same thing happened to īts soul! Īt was killed in spirit and form!

It happened incredibly quickly. Xu Qing attacked with efficient speed, and his aura and the terrifying nature of the fingernail shook heaven and earth.

The Summer Immortal looked at him, stunned. He’s not just some Quasi-Immortal.... He’s obviously a Summer Immortal! And with that dao weapon, ordinary Summer Immortals would have to be very careful around him. He’s obviously just on the verge of a breakthrough. He has everything, even the completed immortal embryo. All he needs to become a mature immortal is an upgrade in canon!

“True Monarch,” she said, “wait for me just one moment!”

The surrounding gods were fleeing like mad. As for the cultivators, they knew that they had just escaped death. After bowing to Xu Qing, they started chasing down and killing the gods.

The Summer Immortal joined in. Without the True God present, it wasn’t hard at all for the Summer Immortal to lead her subordinates and wipe out the surviving gods. After the work was done, the Summer Immortal returned to Xu Qing and bowed to him.

“Many thanks for your assistance!” she said sincerely.

Xu Qing returned her salute, then chatted with her a bit. After coming to understand the latest developments in the Fourth Star Ring, he bid farewell. As he disappeared into the starry sky, the Summer Immortal struggled to clear her mind.

He’s a true monarch, and he has destiny aura. He’s also the younger brother of Immortal Lord Mi Ming.... There could hardly be anyone more respectable than him in the entire Fifth Star Ring! And his battle prowess is astonishing.... The next time I see him, he’ll surely have broken through and become a Summer Immortal.

Having reached this point in her train of thought, her heart suddenly started racing.

It doesn’t seem like he has a daoist partner....

***

Xu Qing had no way of knowing what that female Summer Immortal was thinking. He was currently drifting along through the starry sky of the Fourth Star Ring.

The deeper he went, the more devastation he saw. He saw shattered planets and destroyed god kingdoms. The ravages of war were endless in the Fourth Star Ring. Everything was in decline.

There was hardly any starlight, and none of the golden glow that came from god kingdoms. Roughly half of the entire star ring had descended into utter darkness and gloom. The supply depot planets stretching from the Fifth Star Ring were just about the only thing bringing light into the Fourth Star Ring. The cultivators were starting to wrap things up once and for all.

According to what that Summer Immortal told me, the end stages of the war involved two things. First, the cultivator army is trying to force the gods into picking a spot for the final battle. Second, the supply depot planets are being used as staging areas to purge any resistance fighters. The main army is up on the front lines. Further back... all the work is being done by Corpsedrainers and various defense squadrons.

Xu Qing found himself thinking about Zhou Zhengli and the others.

I can probably track them down by means of the supply depot planets. Reminiscing about his old comrades-in-arms made him smile. I wonder how they’re doing...?

In that manner, time passed. Xu Qing traveled in the Fourth Star Ring looking for the destined opportunity he needed.

He would occasionally run into surviving gods. Given that he was a peak Quasi-Immortal who had battle prowess sufficient to equal a Summer Immortal, the only things he had to worry about were peak True Gods and God Lords.

On one of the supply depot planets, he was finally able to make contact with Zhou Zhengli. After determining his location, he headed there to meet his old comrades-in-arms.

***

Zhou Zhengli and the other Undertakers had just finished a mission and had earned the right to take an extensive leave. They were currently on their way back to their local supply depot planet, where they would then part ways for their time off.

After Xu Qing went missing along with Goddess Starryeyes, Zhou Zhengli and his Undertakers progressed a lot. They had participated in the general offensive against the Fourth Star Ring, and had earned a lot of battle credits. They had continued the Undertaker tradition of draining corpses on the battlefield, all while being proactive in their activities.

All of them had made significant progress with their cultivation base. Every member was a Quasi-Immortal, while Sir Star Ring was already a mid Quasi-Immortal on the verge of a breakthrough to the late level.

Sir Vilespirit and Yuanshan Su were very close to breaking out of early Quasi-Immortal. Hordeslayer and Rampart were in a similar position. Their mood had improved a lot after Xu Qing left. Being so free from worry had led to them feeling very proud of their accomplishments.

Zhou Zhengli was the only one whose cultivation base hadn’t changed much. However, given how deceptive he was, it was hard for anyone to tell the truth of the matter.[2]

After arriving at the supply depot planet, Zhou Zhengli looked around at everyone preparing to leave.

Grinning, he said, “Ladies and gentlemen, I have some news for you. I recently got word from the young lord. He’s currently on the way to this very planet.”

His announcement was met with various reactions.

Sir Vilespirit’s eyes narrowed, and he quickly took steps to rein in the instinctive cruelty that had been building in him lately. Yuanshan Su seemed dazed. Sir Star Ring’s facial expression didn’t change at all, but his eyes glittered.

The biggest reaction came from Hordeslayer and Rampart. The two sword people had been secretly transmitting a conversation in which they were talking about where to go to have fun on their time off. But Zhou Zhengli’s announcement caused their hearts to start pounding. Eventually, everyone went their separate ways.

Zhou Zhengli continued to smile as he watched them go to different parts of the supply depot planet. Inside, he was feeling quite excited. freewebnovel.com

There were two people who were most excited about Xu Qing’s return. They were Zhou Zhengli and Li Mengtu, who had stayed off-planet to work on his cultivation. The two of them were Xu Qing’s earliest followers, and they had benefited the most when Immortal Lord Mi Ming shook the entire Fifth Star Ring.

They had both noticed how Fifth Star Ring cultivators looked up to them more. Virtually all doors were open to them on this supply depot planet. Even the Summer Immortal in charge of the entire planet treated them with respect.

Because of that, Zhou Zhengli couldn’t have been more pleased with the choice he had made years ago.

Zhou Zhengli knew what everyone else was thinking, but he didn’t care. He knew that all of their little plots and schemes were nullified the moment Xu Qing helped Young Lord Aurora. So it was no surprise they had all disappeared the moment they heard Xu Qing was coming back. He laughed softly as he watched them go, then prepared to wait in place so that he was the first to welcome Xu Qing.

Those who left went to do different things.

***

Sir Vilespirit went into seclusion. The broken sword inside of him was trembling. “He’s on the way back. If you want to go forward with that matter we discussed, I don’t care. But... do you really dare?”

In response, the broken sword inside of Sir Vilespirit emitted a flustered and exasperated sensation.

***

The brothers Hordeslayer and Rampart were now in no mood to have fun. Instead, they raced back to their mansion grotto to try to come up with a plan.

“What do we do...? That guy is coming back!”

“We’re finished. Finished! I knew things were just going too well. Our sword bodies are sharper than ever. Once he notices, he’s definitely going to get greedy!”

“This is all your fault! I told you not to eat so much!”

“This is your fault. You were the one who started eating!”

***

Sir Star Ring left the supply depot planet, turning into a bright beam of light that shot through the starry sky to a secret mansion grotto he had constructed. It was located on a shattered planet that had seemed like the perfect place for cultivation. After settling down cross-legged, his eyes shone brightly.

Although the gap between us continues to widen, Xu Qing... I’m not going to allow myself to fall too far behind!

He waved his hand, and a little pile of dust motes appeared in front of him. It was no ordinary dust, as each mote was terrifyingly heavy.

They were motes of heaven’s principle!

Sir Star Ring eyed the motes with anticipation rising within him. He had worked very hard recently, and had come across some destined opportunities that had allowed him to increase his stockpile of heaven’s principle. It was all for his future breakthrough to Summer Immortal.

He planned to walk a different path than Xu Qing. Xu Qing still had not gained enlightenment of the canon that would take him to Summer Immortal. But Sir Star Ring had long known that his canon was heaven’s principle.

I’ve almost assimilated enough by this point. Just a few more days of assimilation, and I should be able to fully fuse with heaven’s principle! At that point, the only thing I’ll lack to break through to Summer Immortal will be a bit of ringsource to nourish my immortal embryo!

With that thought in mind, Sir Star Ring resolutely performed a double-handed incantation gesture, then focused his thoughts inward on the assimilation process.

However, that was when something unexpected happened!

Without any warning whatsoever, the air in the mansion grotto rippled, and a huge mouth appeared. It seemed to be made of pure greed, and resembled a mad dog’s mouth! Before Sir Star Ring could even react, the mouth swallowed the dust of heaven’s principle in one bite!

It was gone, just like that. Not one mote was left behind. Then the mouth vanished! The only thing left behind was the sound of a satisfied burp.

It happened too quickly. Sir Star Ring was initially stunned, and then his eyes filled with rage as he let loose a furious roar. His cultivation base raged!

1. Xu Qing got the dao weapon in chapter 1253 and we saw it in action in 1259. ☜

2. A long time ago during the immortal palace arc, I mentioned that the author eventually described Zhou Zhengli using the same term he used to describe the Seventh Peak traditions from the Seven Blood Eyes days. This is what I was talking about. If you recall, Seventh Peak disciples had the reputation of being ‘deceptive.’ The same term is used here to describe Zhou Zhengli. ☜

Mid Quasi-Immortal cultivation power swept madly through the starry sky in the area, covering entire universes like heavenly tribulation. Rumbling sounds echoed everywhere. The canon of order manifested as chains, which swept through the void and locked down everything.

Sir Star Ring wasn’t holding anything back. Eventually, he sensed a person fleeing through a rift in the void! The person was clearly very adept at getting away unnoticed. Were it not for the fact that Sir Star Ring was very close to late Quasi-Immortal, he probably would not have noticed the clues.

The fleeing person looked very strange. His head was the size of a normal person, and resembled a young man who was neither good-looking nor ugly. His body, though, was that of a five- or six-year-old child. The bulky robe he was wearing made him look almost like a ghost.

As for his aura... it was that of an Imperial Sovereign. That said, he was moving so fast he was like a blur. He was obviously using a secret magic of some sort, and even seemed to have fused with the star ring itself in some way.

Seeing all that caused Sir Star Ring’s eyes to overflow with killing intent. His right hand flashed with an incantation gesture, causing countless lightning bolts and chains of order to shoot toward the fleeing figure. Sir Star Ring himself also gave chase. The killing intent materialized, locking down the entire area!

His eyes were crimson. That heaven’s principle was very important to him for his breakthrough. He had spent blood, sweat, and tears to get it, and had even set up the entire secret mansion grotto in order to prevent anything unexpected from happening. He had set up warding spells all over the shattered planet, and had been careful to maintain them.

How could he ever have imagined that something like this would happen?? That mouth seemingly came out of nowhere. And even more gruish was the fact that Sir Star Ring hadn’t been able to detect it at all.

Sir Star Ring was like an erupting volcano as he chased after the fleeing figure. Where he passed, the starry sky shattered. And soon, his power swept over the thief.

The fleeing figure exploded. However, only a moment later, he formed anew and then started fleeing again.

Sir Star Ring snorted coldly and set his foot down. That step took him right to the thief, where he sent pressure out in all directions. The weight of order erupted, and his immortal embryo’s power surged out.

The strange-looking thief exploded again. This time, he didn’t form anew. Instead, the shattered flesh and blood turned into a host of wriggling blue worms that scattered in different directions. At the same time, they belched out a large volume of mist that distorted the void and upturned natural laws. The multicolored mist seemed corrosive, but Sir Star Ring’s cultivation base was so high that he simply unleashed his canon. The resulting order shattered all the mist.

It also caused all of the worms to explode. However, the moment they exploded, a frigid energy swept out madly in all directions.

The frigid energy wasn’t a sealing ice, but rather, a force of destruction. It destroyed all traces of passage! In other words, it made it seem like his true form was dead, while in fact, he had vanished without a trace.

Sir Star Ring looked around grimly. He had lost track of the thief!

This guy is weak but very gruish....

Sir Star Ring’s eyes were ice-cold. The sensation he got was that this person had carried out countless heists, to the point where it was an ordinary circumstance to have someone trying to chase him down and kill him. Given his extensive experience in that regard, he had a host of gruish techniques to draw on. At the moment, Sir Star Ring knew he had no way to track the person down.

That said, those motes of heaven’s principle are deeply connected to my canon. Special escape methods aside, he’s still just a measly Imperial Sovereign. Assimilating that collection will not be easy to do....

Sir Star Ring chuckled coldly and used his connection to the heaven’s principle to start tracking it down. A few days later, Sir Star Ring could be seen hovering motionless in the starry sky, his eyes closed, but a scowl on his face.

A short time later, the void rippled and Sir Vilespirit stepped out. Looking at Sir Star Ring, he grinned.

“Sir Star Ring. I never thought I would see the day that you asked for my help.”

Sir Star Ring ignored his comment.

Sir Vilespirit raised an eyebrow but said nothing further as the void next to him rippled. Yuanshan Su appeared. Next came Hordeslayer and Rampart, who hadn’t been inclined to show their faces, but in the end, realized that they might need Sir Star Ring’s help later. Next to arrive was Li Mengtu, who was only now returning to the area.

Finally, Zhou Zhengli showed up. “Given your cultivation base, Sir Star Ring, how could an Imperial Sovereign evade you for so long?”

Sir Star Ring opened his eyes and looked at the group. “He’s only an Imperial Sovereign, but he’s very gruish. He seems like a cultivator, but also resembles a god or even a mutant. He has undying characteristics, and can split apart into innumerable clones. I’ve actually wiped him out numerous times, but his flesh and blood just scatters and then comes back to life. What’s more, he’s obviously an expert in being deceptive.

“I’ve been able to sense that my collection of heaven’s principle is on the verge of being assimilated. I suspect that this person seems like an Imperial Sovereign, but is actually an injured True God! That is why I’ve troubled you all to come here. Going forward, I’ll owe all of you a favor!”

Sir Star Ring spoke in a rather stiff manner. He had never asked anyone for help, but at the moment, he was out of options, and time was running out. Meanwhile, his words caused the others’ eyes to glitter with interest.

Zhou Zhengli looked at the surrounding void and smiled. “Not a problem. How exactly would you like us to help?”

“I’ve tracked the thief down to the universe up ahead,” Sir Star Ring replied. “Please, unleash your sealing magics to block all the exits. I’m going to assimilate this universe, and that way, the thief will be unable to escape!”

Li Mengtu nodded. Waving his hand, he unleashed his canon, causing a massive poisonous flower to cover the universe in question. His poison canon was then made manifest in the form of millions of streams of poisonous fog.

Sir Vilespirit grinned and took out his broken sword. Its raging, baleful aura locked down the area. Yuanshan Su, Hordeslayer, and Rampart all used their various canons and Quasi-Immortal might to further seal the area. Last was Zhou Zhengli, whose forehead opened to reveal a third eye, which finished the sealing.

Their combined power caused the universe up ahead to tremble. Then Sir Star Ring sat down cross-legged and performed a double-handed incantation gesture, causing chains of order to snake out and wrap around the universe. He immediately started assimilating it!

Based on his connection to heaven’s principle, he could sense that the thief was getting very anxious.

At the most, it will take a few days to force you out into the open!

***

A figure was fleeing at top speed through the sealed universe. Put precisely, a head was rolling along through it. Occasionally, some motes of heaven’s principle would spill out, though he would quickly swallow them back up.

It went without saying that the head was Erniu. At the moment, he really was starting to get nervous.

What the hell kind of place is this...? Why are there so many strong people around here?? Besides, I’m just borrowing this stuff! Is there really a need to push things this far? Isn’t chasing me for half a month enough, ya fool? You killed me a bunch of times! And yet you’re still coming after me?? This is outright bullying!!

Erniu quickly swallowed some of the heaven’s principle he had spilled. He already had planned a way to escape, but doing so would require giving up the stolen goods. And he wasn’t willing to do that.

This is some precious stuff. It would be a huge waste to give it up!

A crazy look could be seen in Erniu’s eyes, and it was a struggle for him to breathe steadily. After escaping from that pocket realm, he had been careful to stay out of sight. That was especially true after he realized how many powerful experts there were in the area.

His current situation came about because he was just too gluttonous. Having sensed the precious treasure right there, he had taken a big risk and devoured it.

What should I do? Do I... really just throw caution to the wind??

Grinding his teeth, he finally decided that he had no choice but to undo one of his seals. However, that was when a terrifying stream of divine will swept over him. Erniu shivered as a sense of deadly crisis filled him. The divine will made him feel like a tiny rowboat navigating terrifying waves. But then his jaw nearly dropped, and his expression became one of doubt. His eyes widened.

It seems so familiar. Is this... is it... Little Ah Qing??

***

Outside of the universe, the divine will swept through the area, causing Sir Star Ring and the others to shiver. Zhou Zhengli’s eyes lit up, and he shot to his feet and bowed.

“We offer respectful greetings, Young Lord!”

A person approached through the starry sky. He wore a daoist robe and had long, flowing hair. A dao will emanated from him, and he was surrounded by auspicious signs. Every step he took caused the entire starry sky to tremble. He was none other than Xu Qing!

However, he didn’t seem interested in anyone gathered outside of the universe. Instead, he was looking at the universe itself with a very curious and surprised look on his face.

Destiny was a wonderful thing.

The fleeing figure looked familiar. He was bedraggled, with a crazy look on his face. Most important of all was that, despite existing as only a head, he continuously spilled and devoured the motes of heaven’s principle. It was like a cycle....

Xu Qing’s mind was reeling. There was no way he could have ever guessed that he would run into his Eldest Brother like this....

The moment he caught sight of Erniu, he realized what was going on. He immediately thought back to the teleportation portal in that pocket realm.

That teleportation portal needed two specific things to work. It needed star ring hemp, and a golden rat. But I’m not the only person with those two things. Eldest Brother also has two such items.

Then Xu Qing thought about the Immortal Paragon’s plan, and how he used Eminent Desolation’s karma to confound the Fourth Star Ring God Paragon’s omniscience. In other words... Xu Qing wasn’t the only one who could do that. His Eldest Brother could as well.

Then Xu Qing thought about what Young Lord Aurora had said when he gave him Eminent Desolation’s godhood of fate. He had said that someone else should have been present, except that person had never shown up.

The person who didn’t show up was Eldest Brother?

As those thoughts ran through Xu Qing’s head, the Undertakers looked at him.

Li Mengtu was the most familiar with Xu Qing, having been his study partner Zhong Chi in the reflected version of the history of the Aurora Immortal Palace. Those memories would never leave him. In fact, he excitedly stepped forward, bowed, and explained the situation.

“Young Lord, we’re all here at the request of Sir Star Ring. He just got some more motes of heaven’s principle, only for them to be stolen by a mysterious thief. This thief is crafty and extremely talented when it comes to deception. He has a host of gruish magics, to the point where Zhou Zhengli even suspects him of working with a partner!

“Right now, we have the thief locked up in this universe, which we are slowly assimilating. Eventually, the thief will have nowhere to hide. Doing it this way will also reveal whether or not he has an accomplice!”

As Li Mengtu explained these things, a very strange expression appeared on Xu Qing’s face. If there was any accomplice... it would be himself.

He looked at Zhou Zhengli. Zhou Zhengli’s expression flickered.

Everyone else stepped forward to offer greetings.

Sir Vilespirit acted very respectfully and didn’t do anything out of turn. But inside he was trying to figure out what was going on. When he showed up and looked at the universe, his facial expression changed. Why?

Hordeslayer and Rampart weren’t paying any attention at all to Xu Qing’s facial expression. They were focused on themselves. Both were feeling extremely uneasy. Though they were trying very hard not to stand out, they were still terrified of the possibility of Xu Qing waving his hand and turning them into a pair of swords. Unfortunately, no matter how hard they tried, it wasn’t possible to completely suppress their immortal sword instincts, which prompted them to feel very happy that their bonded master had arrived. Their unease just continued to build.

Yuanshan Su looked just as beautiful as ever as she bowed in greeting.

Sir Star Ring bowed as well. Though he had noticed the unusual expression on Xu Qing’s face, he was so focused on chasing down and killing the thief that he didn’t think much about it. His eyes flitted back to the sealed universe, and the thought of his heaven’s principle being stolen caused his killing intent to build.

Suddenly looking very solemn, Zhou Zhengli said, “Young Lord, I actually suspect that this fellow daoist didn’t intentionally steal the heaven’s principle. In fact, there is some evidence that suggests that he cultivates techniques related to order. Perhaps that’s what drew him to the motes of heaven’s principle.”

Thoughtful expressions appeared on the faces of the others present. As for Sir Star Ring, his eyes flashed with cold light as he looked at Zhou Zhengli, then Xu Qing. All of a sudden, bitterness struck him as he realized what was going on.

Zhou Zhengli ignored the look in Sir Star Ring’s eyes. Focusing on Xu Qing, he continued, “As for this talk of an accomplice....”

Xu Qing cleared his throat and waved a finger in the direction of the universe. That action caused something like a storm to kick up in the universe. As it spread, countless heavenly bodies shone with dazzling starlight. The starry sky shivered, and the sealing effects vanished.

Gradually, an asteroid was revealed in the depths of the universe. Atop it was Erniu, a dazed and incredulous look on his face. Of course, because of the cultivation level of Xu Qing and the Undertakers, they could see Erniu, while he could see nothing but a blur.

Upon catching sight of Erniu, Sir Star Ring’s eyes blazed with killing intent.

Xu Qing sighed helplessly. “That’s my Eldest Brother....”

Li Mengtu’s eyes went wide. Zhou Zhengli shivered inwardly. Sir Vilespirit actually gasped. Hordeslayer and Rampart were visibly stunned. Yuanshan Su’s eyes gleamed.

Sir Star Ring, meanwhile, looked from Erniu to Xu Qing. All he could do now was wait to hear Xu Qing’s decision.

Xu Qing was increasingly unsure of what to do. In the beginning, he hadn’t cared much at all about Sir Star Ring. But after all their travels and exploits, they had become comrades in arms. What was more, those motes of heaven’s principle were crucial to Sir Star Ring reaching the Summer Immortal level. At the same time, he knew what his Eldest Brother was like. His Eldest Brother would consider it a loss to not grab something good that he saw.... And if he swallowed something, getting it back was going to be extremely difficult.

After some thought, Xu Qing waved his hand to unleash his canon. Overlapping universes appeared, and from within them spilled numerous motes of heaven’s principle. Given Xu Qing’s cultivation base and level of enlightenment, plus his own research into heaven’s principle, it made this an easy thing to do.

As the motes of heaven’s principle appeared, they shifted from being illusory to material, and they piled up in front of Sir Star Ring. Xu Qing even added in the mote of heaven’s principle he had taken from Sir Star Ring long ago.

“This was all just a misunderstanding,” he said quietly.

Sir Star Ring looked at all of the motes that made up for what he had lost. A thousand thoughts were running through his head. Finally, he bowed deeply to Xu Qing.

“Many thanks!” Then he turned and left, leaving behind only a few words. “I won’t forget how you’ve helped me achieve my dao, and how we’ve become comrades in arms. I know you’re not from the Fifth Star Ring.... When you go back to your home, I’ll come along.”

Xu Qing nodded. Then he looked at Zhou Zhengli and the others. “I’ll be leaving soon,” he said calmly, “so this will be the last time we see each other.”

Li Mengtu’s eyes glittered with anticipation. “I’ll go with you!”

Zhou Zhengli smiled. It went without saying that he had come to understand the situation even before Sir Star Ring did. “Wherever you go, Young Lord, I’ll go also. But for now, we don’t want to disrupt this reunion between you and your Eldest Brother.”

Clasping hands, he turned and left with Li Mengtu.

Yuanshan Su didn’t say anything. Sir Vilespirit felt hesitant. Hordeslayer and Rampart were elated. Taking such thoughts with them, they all left.

After they were all gone, Xu Qing turned his attention back to the universe in front of him. Looking at Erniu there, hopping up and down in excitement, caused a smile to break out on his face. His Eldest Brother was one of the most important people to him.

He stepped forward. That step spanned the starry sky and put him right in front of Erniu.

“Little Ah Qing!!” Erniu cried elatedly. He almost felt like it wasn’t real.

“Eldest Brother....” Xu Qing cleared his throat. He got the feeling that when his Eldest Brother heard about what he was going to do next, it wasn’t going to go over well. But for now, he just smiled and said, “I missed you!”

Erniu was very excited. He had been completely taken aback earlier when he sensed Xu Qing’s aura. And now that Xu Qing was right in front of him, his mind was spinning. He was so ecstatic at being able to reunite that he was too stunned to react. The two hadn’t seen each other for a very long time, so he was understandably shocked.

Finally, he asked a question that he realized sounded stupid as soon as it came out. “Little Ah Qing, what are you doing here? And who were those people who trapped me here?”

Xu Qing thought for a moment before deciding that the simple truth was the best response. “My subordinates.”

Erniu was shocked to the core, and his eyes went wide. Earlier, he had sensed that something was happening outside, but had no way to know the details. But after the big chase he had endured, he knew that his pursuer was terrifying. And upon being trapped he realized that his pursuer had called some friends to help, all of whom were also very strong. And now, he’d come to find out, they were all subordinates of little Ah Qing....

It was such an amazing development that he went right back to being as excited as before. He also sent out his divine will to examine Xu Qing’s cultivation base. When he realized how deep and unreadable it was, he got even more excited. He even had to suppress the urge to gasp!

But then, all of a sudden, he was overwhelmed by the instinct to act like the Eldest Brother. As such, he had to force himself not to ask what place this was, or what status Xu Qing had earned, or what he was doing here. He didn’t want to give Xu Qing any more chances to provoke him. That said, he couldn’t stop himself from wanting to know about Xu Qing’s cultivation base.

“So that’s how it is,” he said in a light tone. “Hahaha.... Ahem. So, little Ah Qing, how much have you been hogging for yourself here? Your cultivation base... seems to have changed a bit.”

Xu Qing blinked a few times. He was, of course, very familiar with his Eldest Brother. “Oh, just a few destined opportunities and a few flashes of enlightenment.”

It was a simple response, but it was profoundly distressing to Erniu. Now he wanted to know what exact destined opportunities and what specific types of enlightenment could lead to such a terrifying advancement in cultivation base.... However, he wasn’t willing to admit defeat. Maintaining his dignity as the Eldest Brother, he stuck his chin up.

“Not bad, I suppose. That said, little Ah Qing, your cultivation base still has some impure elements. You’re going to have to work hard going forward. What’s more... given how long we’ve been apart, you’re obviously unaware of what I’ve been up to.”

Erniu sighed deeply. “As you can tell, I’m only here as a clone. You definitely have no way of even comprehending how powerful my true form is now. Let me tell you, my true form is half a step away from conquering all of Brilliant Heaven! I, your Eldest Brother, am like the sun in the sky over in Brilliant Heaven!”

Erniu suddenly looked very proud.

Meanwhile, a look of astonishment appeared on Xu Qing’s face. It was an expression that left Erniu feeling very pleased.

“But in the end,” Erniu continued, “I missed the days when you were at my side, little Ah Qing. Too much. And thus, I used an amazing divine ability to pierce through the void, to sever the profoundly ancient, and to come here to find you. I want you at my side when I finally reign supreme over all of Brilliant Heaven!”

Erniu suddenly seemed to pulse with great mightiness.

Xu Qing smiled and nodded, then started moving through the starry sky.

Erniu cleared his throat, and then hurried along after Xu Qing in the form of a head. “However, little Ah Qing, do you know the problem with that final half a step I need to take? I need the corpse of a peak Altar God!

“I have to devour the corpse of a peak Altar God to activate the million clones I have buried all over Brilliant Heaven, as well as the ten million magical devices I put in place. And then I can absolutely crush Brilliant Heaven!

“And that is how I’ll save the Revered Ancient mainland! Now, I could have done all of that on my own, little Ah Qing. But then I thought about you. You are my little Junior Brother, after all. Therefore, I decided to give you the chance to do it!”

Erniu looked at Xu Qing, and inside, he was feeling very emotional. “Little Ah Qing, don’t you think it’s fair to trade the corpse of an Altar God for the rulership of Brilliant Heaven??

“Once I conquer the place, I’m going to appoint Master as the crown prince, and you can be a junior prince! Huang Yan will be the divine beast guardian of the kingdom, Second Junior Sister can be the divine beast’s daoist partner, and Third Sib can be the majordomo! I’ll give great honor and riches to all of my fellow apprentices. We—”

Before Erniu could finish speaking, Xu Qing nodded and waved his hand to produce a handful of mutilated corpses. Though they were all in bad shape, they all emitted True God auras.

“Eldest Brother, I don’t have any Altar God corpses....” He was telling the truth.

Erniu stared in shock. The sight of the corpses caused his scalp to tingle. It felt like he was in a dream, and he instinctively gasped.

Voice trembling, he said, “True Gods?”

Xu Qing nodded.

After a long moment of silence, Erniu laughed heartily. Swallowing so he didn’t drool, he tried to seem very nonchalant. Suppressing his hunger, he waved his hand casually.

“I’m kind of burned out on eating measly True Gods. I mean, they have tons of them in Brilliant Heaven. If I have any more, I might just hurl. The reason I mentioned peak Altar Gods just now is that I was worried that you would be too shocked, little Ah Qing. So I lowered my standards a bit. Let me tell you, over in Brilliant Heaven, the gods all treat me very respectfully.”

Meanwhile, Xu Qing suddenly stopped in place and looked off into the distance in the starry sky. Eyes glittering coldly, he stomped his right foot down in front of him.

The spot he was looking at in the starry sky suddenly collapsed. Rifts spread out in all directions, and tempest winds raged. Several gods popped out into the open. Thēy were resistance forces that the passing armies had missed, and thēy had been hiding in the void. Sadly, thēy could not escape Xu Qing’s senses.

The leader of the group was actually a peak Altar God. But when the group caught sight of Xu Qing, thēy were so terrified thēy immediately tried to flee.

Face completely expressionless, Xu Qing pushed his right hand out. Instantly, a terrifying pressure swept out, turning into a crushing force that descended on the void. The starry sky shook. When the force disappeared, nothing was left behind. The rogue gods had been killed in body and soul.

Given Xu Qing’s current battle prowess, killing Altar Gods was as easy as flipping over his hand.

When Erniu saw that happen, a buzzing sound filled his mind. A long moment passed, and then he cleared his throat.

“Not bad. Not bad at all, little Ah Qing. You’re about as strong as I am in Brilliant Heaven. That said, you need to remember that while it’s good to be able to use overwhelming force against the gods, you also need to earn an appropriate status among cultivators. Take that as a little bit of advice from your Eldest Brother, a person who has plentiful experience in that regard.

“Now that you’ve grown up, there are certain things I can finally tell you. In the past, my status was such that I could turn my nose up at the starry sky. Myriad cultivators would prostrate in worship to me. But my feelings then can only be summed up by the idiom one can’t win against the cold when in high places. And that is how I ended up forming my signature power of frigid coldness.”

It was impossible to determine if it was coincidence or not, but... as soon as Erniu finished speaking, some army cultivators from a nearby supply depot planet arrived to check on the fluctuations which had just rolled out from the area. Upon flying over and spotting Xu Qing, the cultivators excitedly bowed in greeting.

Xu Qing felt slightly embarrassed at how his Eldest Brother reacted, with his jaw dropping and eyes going wide. The cultivators were made up mostly of Imperial Sovereigns, but there were also some Quasi-Immortals.

Erniu was so flabbergasted he felt like his mind was blank. However, there was always his dignity as the Eldest Brother to think about. So he quickly gave a hearty laugh and opened his mouth to speak. But then....

The star domain that this particular universe was part of trembled. A terrifying stream of divine will that surpassed the level of a Summer Immortal rushed through the starry sky, filled with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. It came from a spot where the Fourth Star Ring was rippling.

Countless cultivators from the supply depot planet prostrated respectfully.

When Erniu sensed the divine will, his heart and mind reached a peak state of stupefaction.

Xu Qing’s cultivation base had seemed enigmatic and mysterious to him. But this stream of divine will gave him the sensation that its owner could destroy Brilliant Heaven in an instant.

“Th-that... that....” As Erniu trembled, the divine will which had just arrived thrummed with the voice of Immortal Lord Mi Ming.

“Lil’ bro, your sister-in-law told me you like assimilating goddesses. Well, I just captured one. Specifically, the daughter of God Lord Brightwise. Consider this a gift from me.”

A sealed goddess then appeared out of nowhere. The goddess looked human, and exuded a sensation of profound holiness. Hēr cultivation base was at the True God level, and yet, shē had been sealed tightly and offered up as a gift....

A strange expression could be seen on Xu Qing’s face as he clasped hands and bowed.

Erniu, meanwhile, had a blank look on his face as he thought, The daughter of a god, given as a gift?

The voice in the divine will then seemed to laugh. “I was just joking around. This goddess’ innate abilities and godly authority are very unique, and should help you as you seek enlightenment of your canon.”

With that, Immortal Lord Mi Ming’s divine will retracted, leaving behind the goddess.

The entire experience left Erniu feeling like a hole had been punched in his heart cavity, and he couldn’t help but turn to look at Xu Qing. “What exactly is going on here, little Ah Qing! What is this place? Who are you here? And whose divine will was that...? And what’s this ‘canon’ he talked about??”

Xu Qing smiled. He didn’t feel the need to hide things from Erniu. It was just that the situation couldn’t be explained in only a few words. And thus, Xu Qing waved his hand and took all of the things he had done after arriving in the Fifth Star Ring, put it into a sealing mark, and then fused it into Erniu.

Erniu cooperated with the process and let the sealing mark merge into his forehead. The sea of information poured into him. He saw everything. His expression started out blank, then turned into one of surprise. Then it changed several times, until finally all the information was there.

“When I arrived, the treasures I encountered were all things you didn’t even want!” Erniu beat his chest in frustration. “If I’d known earlier, I would have come with you! If I had, I might already be a Summer Immortal!! I made the wrong damn choice!!”

Erniu was nearly going mad at the thought of how many spectacular destined opportunities he had missed out on. And then he thought about the misery and suffering he had endured after going to Brilliant Heaven, and he could only come to the conclusion that life just wasn’t fair....

Xu Qing could see how Erniu was reacting, so after a moment, he decided to comfort him.

But before he could, Erniu looked up, his eyes crimson. Pulsing with an indescribable energy, he said, “No. I have to do something big here! That’s the only way I can make up for this monumental loss!”

Ignoring the fact that he was right in front of Xu Qing, he ripped open one of his seals, causing his cultivation base to surge. At the same time, he suddenly was able to sense all hidden treasures nearby.

To Xu Qing’s astonishment, Erniu focused on one specific location and then erupted with a crazy laugh.

“Let’s go, little Ah Qing. I’m taking you on a really big job!”

Erniu licked his lips as crazy light burned in his eyes. And then something completely ghastly happened. The body beneath his head had already started to recover a bit. But now, the flesh and blood squirmed and wriggled as the recovery sped up rapidly. Within the space of a few dozen breaths of time, Erniu was back to normal.

And now, he pulsed with an aura that vastly surpassed anything from before. He was no longer in early Imperial Sovereign. He had reached mid Imperial Sovereign!

Xu Qing hadn’t seen his Eldest Brother do this in a long time, so the sight of it brought back many memories.

Eldest Brother’s cultivation base doesn’t improve by practicing cultivation. He progresses by undoing seals! Unfortunately, releasing the seals requires him to pay a price. And the further along he goes, the bigger the price he has to pay....

As Xu Qing considered that, Erniu’s body became whole again, and frigid coldness pulsed out in all directions, along with flickering blue light.

Beneath the flesh and blood, Xu Qing could see that there was a bodily structure inside his Eldest Brother. It was pure blue, and looked like it was made from ice. It was vicious and ancient, and looked very similar to the sourcefiends Xu Qing had encountered on the primeval motherworld. Seeing it caused all of Xu Qing’s speculations about his Eldest Brother to resurface.

There are some differences between Eldest Brother and the sourcefiends I saw. He has lived many past lives, and whenever he dies, his next life takes a different form upon being reborn. That characteristic is actually reminiscent of the gods.

Now that his cultivation base had advanced, Xu Qing was able to pick up on many more clues. And yet, there was still plenty about Erniu that Xu Qing didn’t understand.

I imagine things will become a lot clearer after we get back to Revered Ancient.

Erniu, whose aura and cultivation base were skyrocketing, had eyes that looked even crazier than before.

“You listen to me, little Ah Qing. I can sense that there’s a treasure in that direction!! This is a foreordained invitation! It’s a destined opportunity set by fate! I have a very strong feeling that this treasure is waiting for me specifically! At the same time, it’s also a chance for me to remove several of my seals!

“After we accomplish this big job, little Ah Qing, then you won’t have to rely on strangers to give you goddesses to absorb. Your Eldest Brother will go catch several for you! In fact, I won’t stop at the daughters of gods. If you like the sons of gods, I’ll get them too!”

Erniu suddenly looked very proud. After all, he valued nothing more than his dignity as the Eldest Brother. That dignity had two aspects. The first was that he needed to surpass his Junior Brother, and the other... was that he couldn’t let anyone treat little Ah Qing better than he himself did! That was intolerable!

“Let’s go!” Erniu said, blurring into a streak of light that shot off into the distance.

Grinning, Xu Qing followed. He knew that the Immortal Paragon was the most paramount entity in the Fourth Star Ring, and that the Immortal Lords were all here. Other than the place the God Paragon had left to, there were no places that could harbor major secrets.

At the most, there were a few so-called forbidden regions.

Thanks to all of the things Xu Qing had experienced as he grew, he had come to his own understanding of what ‘forbidden regions’ were.

Normally speaking, forbidden regions are mysterious places with long histories. Because of being cut off from the outside world, they’ve eventually come to be known as forbidden regions. But the degree of danger associated with any given one of them is actually the product of two things: what’s inside, and what’s outside.

Nowadays, everyone knows that forbidden regions are dangerous. But from the perspective of what’s inside the forbidden region, the outside world is just as dangerous. Otherwise, there would be no need to maintain a barrier of isolation.

Of course, there are exceptions... such as the Revered Ancient mainland. But this is the Fourth Star Ring, and there shouldn’t be anything like that here. Since Eldest Brother wants to go explore this place, I might as well just see what happens.[1]

And thus, Xu Qing followed along.

Time passed. This time, it was several months. Although the destination wasn’t necessarily very far away, the star ring was massive, so it took time.

Along the way, they took advantage of teleportation portals on the supply depot planets. As a result, it was only about four months later that they spotted their destination.

From a distance, it was possible to see a majestic rift in the starry sky. It looked like a wound that spanned several universes. The rift was filled with endless mist, and was surrounded by drifting, crimson dust.

This was one of the Fourth Star Ring’s four major forbidden regions. From ancient times until now, hardly anyone had ever been there. Not one god who went inside ever came out.

Erniu eyed the rift, his crazy look getting more and more intense. During their months of travel, he had seen what position Xu Qing occupied among the cultivators here. He had seen countless powerful experts, as well as many fights between cultivators and gods. In terms of goddesses... he had seen two get captured.

The provocation he felt was like a whip slashing against him repeatedly, and it caused him to sink further into craziness. The urge to accomplish a big job was getting stronger and stronger.

Eying the distant rift, he licked his lips and shouted, “It’s there! I can sense that there’s treasure in there, little Ah Qing. A big treasure!!”

Xu Qing said nothing. His gaze pierced through the starry sky, passing through the crimson dust and entering the rift to examine the interior. He could just barely make out an altar. During the journey, he had made certain inquiries and learned a bit about the forbidden regions in the Fourth Star Ring.

This is where the very first God Paragon was sealed up! Hē was killed by the current living God Paragon, and sealed here, imprisoned for all eternity. Furthermore, hē is rejected by the new natural laws woven from the fate in the Fourth Star Ring, and thus can’t leave the place.

Xu Qing’s eyes narrowed. That was the extent of the information he had received, and he knew nothing about what karma could be tied up in it all. There was a God Paragon sealed here, so normally speaking, Xu Qing wouldn’t go inside. But right now....

Xu Qing glanced at Erniu.

I did come to the Fourth Star Ring to look for my own destined opportunity, which is to walk the path of the pain god’s illusion. Although that path of pain didn’t involve coming into this place, I guess... anything is possible.

Xu Qing waved his hand out in front of him. That motion caused all of the terrifying pressure coming out of the rift to be suppressed. The starry sky around the rift became like a mirror that then shattered. Rubble rained down. The crimson dust around the rift was also affected. It was as if some powerful force just peeled it away.

Then Xu Qing lifted his right hand, causing the rubble in the starry sky to converge in a new form. At the same time, the crimson dust parted. Eventually, something like a series of tunnels appeared in front of the two of them.

“Let’s go in, Eldest Brother. Just keep in mind there are some dangerous things inside.”

“....” Erniu looked at the tunnels going through the mist. The sight of Xu Qing shattering the starry sky and making those tunnels left him feeling a bit defeated. That said, he was determined to get stronger. And thus, he... didn’t rush forward. Instead, he stuck close to Xu Qing and nodded. “You lead the way.”

Erniu was no fool. Given the level of Xu Qing’s cultivation base, whatever things he thought were dangerous would definitely be fatal to Erniu. He wasn’t the kind of person who feared death, but if he died, he wanted it to be after he stuffed himself to the gills, not when he was on the way to eat. Although dignity was important to him, his Junior Brother wasn’t a stranger. When he thought about it that way, he felt a bit less defeated.

Xu Qing’s expression was serious as he strode into one of the tunnels and headed toward the rift. Erniu followed. The two of them quickly sped through the tunnel. They ran into a few dangerous situations, but Xu Qing resolved them easily.

A few days later, they were through the crimson mist! The rift was right in front of them.

As Xu Qing looked around, his pupils constricted. In the misty interior of the rift it was possible to see an entire world.

In the middle of that world was a magnificent altar. Astonishingly, the altar was built from a massive pile of god bones. There were also a host of vicious-looking bugs crawling around on the bones. On top of the altar was a bronze coffin! Countless chains filled the interior of the rift, all of which served to secure the coffin tightly in place!

An ancient will and a profoundly wild aura pulsed from the coffin. There was something boundlessly mysterious and majestic about it, as well as something that seemed to tell all living beings... that this place was forbidden!

This forbidden region didn’t just have an altar, a coffin, and some chains. In another part of it was a hulking figure. It was not a cultivator, but rather, a god. Put precisely, it was a corpse. The corpse of a god. Only the top half of the corpse was there.

After looking closely at the corpse, Xu Qing’s mind started spinning. He knew who this was!

God Lord Death Departure!

Based on the war reports he was familiar with, God Lord Death Departure had been seriously injured, and then fled to parts unknown. But here hē was, and hē was... already dead!

While Xu Qing’s mind spun, Erniu pointed into the mist, a crazy, greedy expression on his face. “I can’t see clearly into there, little Ah Qing, but I can sense that the big treasure is there. Can you help me figure out which direction to go in?”

Xu Qing looked like he wanted to say something, but was holding back. Erniu was pointing right toward the corpse....

“What is it?” Erniu asked urgently.

Xu Qing looked at Erniu. “It’s the corpse of a god.”

Erniu seemed disappointed, but he asked, “A god corpse? You mean it’s not a big treasure? What level is the corpse?”

“God Lord...” Xu Qing said softly.

Even as the words left his mouth, Erniu became a string of afterimages that blurred toward the corpse. He was already going completely crazy.

1. To be honest, this entire passage about forbidden regions was very frustrating because I struggled to determine if he was using “forbidden region” in the same sense as the forbidden regions earlier in the story, or if he was using the term in the more generic sense. Considering that he mentions Revered Ancient, it seems to me he is correlating the location here to the forbidden regions from earlier. What makes it more confusing is that he throws in a slightly different term (the one I rendered as forbidden ground) as well. This problem pops up occasionally when he uses a sort of common term with real-life definitions, but assigns a unique fantasy definition to it as well, then feels the need to explain the similarities and/or differences between the different definitions. In any case, I’m going with “forbidden region” for this place because it does seem that he wants to compare the two. At the same time, the forbidden region in this chapter is clearly not something created the way the forbidden regions in the earlier part of the book were created (being looked at by the broken face). They bear the same name but are fundamentally different, although they do have similarities. ☜

Erniu couldn’t see everything in the mist, but he had shocking instincts, and was able to speed along without touching any of the chains. He was like a big rat, scurrying along, going in and out of the chains... and heading right toward the corpse of God Lord Death Departure.

The combined mutagens created a terrifying godly aura in the rift, and as a result, Xu Qing’s skin almost instantly started showing signs of mutation.

Pressure weighed down on him with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. It sought to rip all outsiders to shreds!

Xu Qing quickly released the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring, which bolstered him and relieved some of the pressure. At the same time, his true name glittered within his soul. Back on the primeval motherworld, Young Lord Aurora had given him a destined opportunity for his true name, and now it was coming in handy.

The glittering of the true name dispelled the invading mutagen, and Xu Qing could breathe a sigh of relief. But now he was even more curious about his Eldest Brother’s background. After all, despite the pressure in the area, Erniu was speeding along quite quickly through the mist.

Despite being only an Imperial Sovereign, the glittering light that covered him kept him safe from the mutagen.

Eldest Brother’s background is definitely full of a lot of mysteries. Could he really be a sourcefiend? Based on my experience, only sourcefiends can completely ignore the aura and mutagen of the gods.... Because of being born from gods, the sourcefiends have a deep connection to them.

The strange thing was that, based on what Xu Qing understood about sourcefiends, they couldn’t leave the motherworld.

Could it be that the Revered Ancient mainland... is the primeval motherworld of the Ninth Star Ring?

It was an astonishing possibility. However, it didn’t seem possible that it could be true.

There’s something else strange. If he’s really a sourcefiend from the Ninth Star Ring’s primeval motherworld, then how could Eldest Brother leave...?

Only a moment later, something strange happened. Although it seemed Erniu had picked the correct path, as soon as he neared the corpse... a deep rumbling sound echoed out, and then Erniu exploded into a host of endless blue worms that all had Erniu’s face.

Xu Qing’s gaze hardened, and he was about to rush over.

Except, in the blink of an eye, the worms crazily continued on their way to the corpse. As they neared, the worms started exploding, resulting in a cloud of dust. Erniu’s craziness continued. Blue light shone as the dust turned into a horde of smaller blue worms that kept racing toward the corpse. freewebnovel.com

But then, something very dramatic happened!

Unfortunately, there are immortals everywhere in the Fifth Star Ring, so that’s not a suitable place for my godly authority and conception.

Within that conception within the starry sky, the old God Paragon’s divine will surged. After Eminent Desolation arrived, all karma collapsed. Countless secrets were revealed, including all evidence of external forces. As a result, hīs omniscience was finally able to form a complete sense from all the disparate bits of information within the broken karma. When all the information came together, the God Paragon smiled.

That Immortal Paragon... is a more profound schemer than any god. Just what I would expect of the only immortal to ever become a Paragon in all history!

At first, his scheme included me.... First was to get on the same page as Nan Ke. By borrowing karma, he forced God Paragon Nan Ke to sacrifice everything to enter the Living God Umbilical Cord. Then he got Eminent Desolation to drive me away.... He wanted me to go to the Third Star Ring to pave the way for the next part of his plan.

He knew that I would flee to the Third, because that would be my only shot at surviving. He also knew that I wouldn’t go to the Fifth... because I would definitely die there! Every step of the way. Every turn of events. All of it revolves around the karma tying those two people to Eminent Desolation![1]

The old God Paragon’s divine will within the conception was pulsing. Laughter rang out within the conception.

However, Immortal Paragon, even using Eminent Desolation from a distance will keep the karmic connection to a minimum, are you sure... that I have no other options at hand??

Next, in a development that shocked all observers, something erupted from within the conception. The old God Paragon suddenly shifted directions! The conception turned... and appeared in a different area in the Fourth Star Ring!

It was a spot very close to the Fifth Star Ring! This development astonished everyone in the other star rings.

You think I’m some pawn you can manipulate...?

By some indescribable method, the conception spread over the border, invading the Fifth Star Ring. At that exact moment, the divine will of the old God Paragon echoed throughout the thirty-six higher star rings.

“I am a preheaven god, respected my whole life, a slaughterer of countless hordes, and after becoming a God Paragon, I now ponder the path to Living God....”

The divine will caused all of the God Paragons to tremble inwardly. And then, the old God Paragon in the form of conception truly entered the Fifth Star Ring. Because of hīs arrival, the immortal energy fought fiercely, becoming ripples of rejection. As a result, the conception was forced to change form.

The hidden God Paragon was forced to reveal hīs terrifying form. Hē was an entity covered with countless heavenly bodies, as well as endless writhing tentacles. Stars and planets were born upon hīm, and they also died. It was as if hē was a part of the operation of the star ring itself.

Then hīs voice echoed out again.

“Anyone who plots against me will have a hard time escaping the constant. It was like that with Nan Ke, and as for you....”

The divine will echoed into the minds of the populace of the Fifth Star Ring, hitting them like endless bolts of lightning. Countless living things howled in agony, and endless beings withered. As hīs divine will spread out, hīs physical form became manifest fully, making hīm completely visible there in the Fifth Star Ring.

The destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring couldn’t sustain the fluctuations. Innumerable universes and planets began to tremble and sink into instability. The moment the God Paragon revealed himself, evidence of hīs existence shone brightly everywhere.

It was extremely eye-catching. And it caught the attention of that which was pursuing hīm.

An instant later, two golden eyes appeared in the void behind hīm. They reflected all living beings, contained infinite universes, were profoundly majestic, and were inviolably holy. They were none other than Eminent Desolation’s eyes!

Hē had arrived in the Fifth Star Ring! And the moment it happened, all cultivators in that star ring reeled. It led to indescribable astonishment, unending fear, and it caused all flesh and blood to writhe.

The terrors which had been visited on the Revered Ancient mainland were now occurring in the Fifth Star Ring. As mutations began to flourish, Eminent Desolation’s gaze locked onto the God Paragon!

The God Paragon didn’t seem to care. Hīs eyes were apathetic and hīs expression was one of determination. As hīs divine will raged, hē imbued his voice with it to create a sound that could shock immortals!

“There isn’t anyone who can turn me into a pawn! And since you tried... I’ll destroy the game board!”

The God Paragon turned to face Eminent Desolation’s eyes. Hē allowed Eminent Desolation’s gaze to lock onto hīm, and even as hē started melting, hē did nothing to evade. But hīs divine will rocked the higher star rings.

“Immortal Paragon, I have abandoned any hope in the Third Star Ring. I have instead chosen to die to ensure that Eminent Desolation’s aura remains in the Fifth Star Ring forever!”

Hē seemed to pulse with derision, which became countless aspects of conception, like an easy path leading right to the Fifth Star Ring. Eminent Desolation’s gaze covered hīm, then followed that path to spread out into the starry sky.

It was such a large area it covered a third of the entire Fifth Star Ring! And then something happened that shocked all living beings and all gods.

1. I made an executive decision to do an editing change here. The God Paragon was referred to by a different name in this passage, but I’m 99.9% sure it’s the same one mentioned previously, who was called Nan Ke. So I edited this passage to maintain continuity. There is never any further elaboration about the name, so we have very few clues to go on other than the story as presented. I did not want to bother the author asking about this tiny thing. In the end, what makes most sense is that the God Paragon here is the same one as mentioned before. ☜

The endlessly majestic, infinitely mysterious starry sky was experiencing an extremely disturbing collapse. As every second passed, it was like a painting full of the most extreme levels of destruction filling the field of view and attacking all things in existence.

If one could view the collapse in slow motion, it would be possible to see that, starting in the distant, never-ending horizon, there was something like a golden thread floating there. It was almost like someone had casually painted a mouth in the darkness of the painting. It wasn’t particularly eye-catching, but it did contain an unspeakably dangerous aura.

It was the old God Paragon’s conception. And that was attracting the gaze of Eminent Desolation.

In the blink of an eye, the golden thread became many golden threads. They madly spread out in all directions like a greedy web. Where they passed, the previously tranquil starry sky became like the surface of a lake that a boulder had smashed into. Rippling waves surged out everywhere. As the ripples spread, the distortions became reality, bending even the light cast by the heavenly bodies.

Next, the heavenly bodies, which were like jewels set into the dark canopy of the various universes, began to dance wildly. Huge suns that normally burned like universal furnaces, unleashing never-ending light and heat, reacted as if they had been hit with gigantic, invisible hammers. Their external surfaces exploded, sending out angry crimson fire like savage dragons.

The light was so brightly red it was blinding enough to illuminate entire universes. The heat waves were so intense that entire planets were vaporized, leaving behind not a trace of their existence, other than shimmering lights that flowed into chaos.

The interior of the suns couldn’t stand up to the violent force, and collapsed into countless bizarre bits of glowing rubble that blasted out in all directions. Each bit of rubble seemed to contain the final defiance of the suns, as they streaked through the darkness like sharp swords to slice apart the rest of the starry sky. It was as if profoundly deep wounds were being ripped open in the starry sky, as if an epic poem were being written about the destruction of everything.

At the same time, the planets that were like millions upon millions of jewels inset into black silk fabric, began to experience the devastating force. Planet after planet exploded. Dazzling light spread out, becoming a blinding waterfall of light that spread with mountain-toppling, sea-draining force. Wherever it spread, space became like pure primal-chaos.

Before, there were planets and galaxies that had been clearly visible, but they were soon overwhelmed by the chaotic convergence of darkness and light. They were ripped apart like a scene from hell itself. With every beam of light that shot out, the universes seemed to issue despairing cries to form a last-ditch defense.

Galaxies could not escape the destruction. Innumerable galaxies, and even star domains, which had once been like majestic and mysteriously orderly islands in the sea of darkness around them, were now like piddling sandbanks collapsing beneath a strong tide. They were shattered, and heavenly bodies collapsed in all directions as the galaxies’ structures were destroyed.

In a very short period of time, the boundless starry sky became a wasteland of primal-chaos! All the heavenly bodies were crushed. Their light went out, all while darkness and gloom spread. It was as if all traces of things from before had been devoured.

There were a few scraps of defiant light that shone, which were the final, lingering effects of the collapse. They were short-lived. Eventually, everything was overwhelmed, and the only thing left behind was deathly silence.

Nothing existed.

In only a few short breaths of time, the majestic starry sky had lived an entire lifetime.

Even the old God Paragon and the gaze of Eminent Desolation became nothing. All of the universes, all of the planets, all of the living beings and inanimate objects were like the Peerless City of the past. They became nothing.

A final stream of divine will from the God Paragon was a howl that echoed coldly through the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring.

“I can’t beat you, Immortal Paragon, but neither can you prevail!”

That divine will became imprinted in the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring, becoming an indelible natural law, something that shook all other magical laws. It would last for all the aeons.

The God Paragon perished!

All entities with paramount personhood in the higher star rings were shaken down to their god souls.

The biggest reaction came in the Ninth Star Ring. In the east of that star ring, a gigantic sleeping beast’s golden eyes opened. In the north of the star ring, trembling figures could be seen atop blooming lotuses that floated atop the golden mother river. In the south of the star ring, in an astonishing black tower, a fire was lit. In the west of the star ring was a terrifying paper person seated cross-legged. The paper person licked his lips as he looked in the direction of Revered Ancient.

In Revered Ancient, Eminent Desolation’s opened eyes finally closed.

Time passed.

***

A figure strode through the star ring of the Fifth Star Ring, a tall old man with hemp sandals, with a golden rat on his shoulder. He was none other than the Immortal Paragon of the Fifth Star Ring.

He walked forward silently until he reached the spot where the God Paragon had died. Ruin stretched out everywhere. As he surveyed the surroundings, he could sense the strong aura of Eminent Desolation.

The Immortal Paragon said nothing. He knew that, going forward, the Fifth Star Ring would forever be missing thirty percent of itself. The ring... would never be whole. And whenever the eyes of Eminent Desolation’s true form opened, light would pour out from this location. The Fifth Star Ring’s karma was forever tainted.

Grandmaster Bai appeared. “This is the cost of using Eminent Desolation. You could have chosen not to lead Xu Qing and that other fellow over to hīm.”

The Immortal Paragon had nothing to say in response. Some time passed, and then he spoke in an ancient voice. It seemed as if his words were directed less to Grandmaster Bai and more to the other God Paragons in the other higher star rings.

“Do you remember what Eminent Desolation said upon failing to become a Living God? Hīs words filled all of the higher star rings. Fate can be broken, but constants must be respected. Isn’t it possible that the word that spread was wrong? What if hē didn’t fail? What if... everything that’s happened is just part of the process of rising to a higher level?”

Having said that, the Immortal Paragon faded from view. The paramount entities in the rest of the higher star rings said nothing. Grandmaster Bai merely sighed and looked at the spot in the Fourth Star Ring where Xu Qing had disappeared.

***

Time passed. In the blink of an eye, five years went by.

There were now only three years left until the appointed time came for Xu Qing to return. Yet he had not returned.

The Fourth Star Ring had changed a lot in those five years. The gods had been confined to a very small area. Everywhere else... there were numerous supply depot planets pulsing with immortal energy. As the destiny aura of the Fifth Star Ring expanded, more and more cultivators were coming to occupy the Fourth Star Ring.

Immortal Lord Mi Ming had returned to the Fifth Star Ring to take charge. The other Immortal Lords had also returned.

Grandmaster Bai was the only exception. He sat waiting in the spot where Xu Qing had disappeared.

In the five years that passed, something else changed for the living beings. Whenever they practiced cultivation, they would hear the final, echoing words of that God Paragon.

“I can’t beat you, Immortal Paragon, but neither can you prevail!”

What exactly was the chaotic flow of space-time? The vast majority of cultivators wouldn’t be able to offer a clear explanation.

To some extent, it was merely a term. Looking at the words that made it up, it obviously described the chaos that existed between space and time, which could be caused by an infinitely large or infinitely small singularity. That was why it could contain anything possible.

Unfortunately, limitations in perception made it impossible to go into finer details using such a description. Only people whose canon related to space-time would be able to offer a truly detailed explanation of the chaotic flow of space-time.

Xu Qing had originally believed in that more simplistic explanation. Before entering the chaotic flow of space-time, he thought that it was something similar to his own Infinite Timelessness, just more majestic and mysterious. Given his own canon, he had a greater chance of coming back out than anyone.

But after going in, things surpassed his predictions. The things he saw left him dazed mentally. Looking up, he saw an infinitude of multi-colored vortexes. They came in all sizes and went on endlessly. Some were orderly, some were chaotic. Some were still, some spun madly. Quite a few of them interacted with each other.

Altogether, they formed an image of a very complex starry sky. One glance would cause a painful swell of information in one’s mind. And after enough time passed, one would feel like their mind was about to crack.

The image wasn’t limited to that. Xu Qing and Erniu existed in unusual states thanks to being in this place.

Xu Qing no longer looked human. He was made of innumerable triangular, glowing bugs. Each glowing bug, from birth to death, lived for only 1/10,000th of a breath of time. Upon being born, the bug would become a dazzling light source. After dying, the result was like an image of the chaos that resulted after a firework exploded. The flame would turn into ashes and then cover over all the light. It was an endless cycle.

Because of the change to Xu Qing’s state, Erniu was no longer in his hair.

Erniu’s appearance was even more abstract. He seemed to be made of a million motes of light, which combined into a kaleidoscopic form that constantly changed. When he spoke, his words came out chaotically.

What he wanted to say was, “What’s going on here, little Ah Qing? Huh? Where are we?”

But what actually came out of his mouth and reached Xu Qing was something different. It sounded like, “Are what’s on, here Qing going? Ah? We are little?”

It was all in chaos. Time. Space. And the two of them. Everything was twisted. It was as if time had no meaning, and that space was pointless.

Xu Qing was stunned. This was completely different from his canon! Moving about and exploring didn’t involve any of the ordinary methods of movement.

One couldn’t physically move here. In fact, movement wasn’t required at all. All that was required was thought. When one exercised thought, the surroundings would spin into motion.

Studying the surroundings worked the same. It was as if all of the secrets in this location just needed to be seen clearly, and could then be understood. The premise, of course, was that one could survive, look around, and gain knowledge.

As Xu Qing numbly studied his surroundings, he saw what appeared to be himself off in the distance. Of course, the so-called distance involved could be time, in other words, the past, present, and future. Or it could be different dimensions and levels of space.
